// ── RESERVATIONS ────────────────────────────────────────────
/** Supabase `equipment_reservation_lines` ile aynı başlık sırası (Rezervasyonlar sayfası). */
const RESH=['reservation_group_id','equipment_id','equipment_name','equipment_category','student_id','student_name','handover_date','return_date','status','approver_email','purpose','created_at','updated_at'];

function _reservationHeaderNorm_(h) {
  return String(h || '').trim().toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '_').replace(/ı/g, 'i');
}

/** Dinamik sütun indeksleri — yeni (RESH) ve eski Türkçe başlıklar. */
function _reservationSheetColIxs_(data) {
  if (!data || !data.length) {
    return { group: 0, eqId: 1, handover: 5, ret: 6, status: 7, approver: 8, student: 4, studentName: 5, name: 2 };
  }
  var headers = data[0].map(function(x) { return _reservationHeaderNorm_(x); });
  function ix(keys) {
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      var w = _reservationHeaderNorm_(keys[i]);
      var fi = headers.indexOf(w);
      if (fi >= 0) return fi;
    }
    return -1;
  }
  var g = ix(['reservation_group_id', 'rezervasyon_id', 'rezervasyon id']);
  if (g < 0) g = 0;
  var e = ix(['equipment_id', 'equipment id', 'ekipman_id', 'ekipman id', 'item_id']);
  if (e < 0) e = 1;
  var st = ix(['status', 'onay_durumu', 'onay durumu']);
  if (st < 0) st = 7;
  var ap = ix(['approver_email', 'onayci_email', 'onaycı email', 'onayci e-posta']);
  if (ap < 0) ap = 8;
  var ho = ix(['handover_date', 'handover date', 'teslim']);
  if (ho < 0) ho = 5;
  var re = ix(['return_date', 'return date', 'iade']);
  if (re < 0) re = 6;
  var sid = ix(['student_id', 'student id']);
  if (sid < 0) sid = 3;
  var snm = ix(['student_name', 'student name']);
  if (snm < 0) snm = 4;
  var nm = ix(['equipment_name', 'equipment name']);
  if (nm < 0) nm = 2;
  var cat = ix(['equipment_category', 'ekipman_türü', 'ekipman turu', 'ekipman_turu', 'type_desc']);
  if (cat < 0) cat = 3;
  var purp = ix(['purpose', 'proje_açıklaması', 'proje aciklamasi']);
  if (purp < 0) purp = 10;
  return { group: g, eqId: e, handover: ho, ret: re, status: st, approver: ap, student: sid, studentName: snm, name: nm, category: cat, purpose: purp };
}

function _reservationRowGroupId_(r) {
  return String(r.reservation_group_id || r['Rezervasyon ID'] || r.id || '').trim();
}

function reservationsList(payload,user) {
  let raw = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_();
  let list = raw.filter(r => _reservationRowGroupId_(r) || r['Equipment_ID'] || r.equipment_id).map(r => ({
    id: _reservationRowGroupId_(r),
    item_id: String(r.equipment_id || r['Equipment_ID'] || r.item_id || '').trim(),
    item_name: String(r.equipment_name || r['Equipment_Name'] || '').trim(),
    user_id: String(r.student_id || r['Student_ID'] || r.user_id || '').trim(),
    user_name: String(r.student_name || r['Student_Name'] || '').trim(),
    start_dt: String(r.handover_date || r['Handover_Date'] || r.start_dt || '').trim(),
    end_dt: String(r.return_date || r['Return_Date'] || r.end_dt || '').trim(),
    status: String(r.status || r['Onay Durumu'] || 'Pending').trim(),
    purpose: String(r.purpose || r['Proje Açıklaması'] || '').trim(),
    type: 'equipment',
    _type: 'equipment',
    created_at: String(r.handover_date || r['Handover_Date'] || '').trim()
  }));
  if(user.role === ROLES.STUDENT || user.role === ROLES.INSTRUCTOR) list = list.filter(r => String(r.user_id||'') === String(user.id) || String(r.user_id||'') === String(user.student_no||''));
  if(payload.status)  list = list.filter(r => r.status === payload.status);
  if(payload.item_id) list = list.filter(r => r.item_id === payload.item_id);
  if(payload.user_id) list = list.filter(r => r.user_id === payload.user_id);
  if(payload.search)  list = multiSearch(list, payload.search, ['item_name','purpose','user_name','id']);
  return list;
}
function reservationsGet(id) { const r=_equipmentReservationRowsSource_().find(x=>_reservationRowGroupId_(x)===String(id||'').trim()); if(!r) throw new Error('Not found'); return r; }

function _reservationActorEmail_(actor) {
  var em = String((actor && actor.email) || '').trim();
  if (em) return em;
  try { return String(Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || '').trim(); } catch (_e) { return ''; }
}

function _ymdInTz_(d) {
  return Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}

function _officialHolidaySetInRange_(start, end) {
  var s = new Date(start); s.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  var e = new Date(end); e.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  var set = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < OFFICIAL_HOLIDAY_CALENDAR_IDS.length; i++) {
    var calId = OFFICIAL_HOLIDAY_CALENDAR_IDS[i];
    try {
      var cal = CalendarApp.getCalendarById(calId);
      if (!cal) continue;
      var evs = cal.getEvents(s, e);
      for (var j = 0; j < evs.length; j++) {
        var ev = evs[j];
        var allDay = false;
        try { allDay = !!ev.isAllDayEvent(); } catch (_e) {}
        if (!allDay) continue;
        set[_ymdInTz_(ev.getStartTime())] = true;
      }
    } catch (_err) {}
  }
  return set;
}

function _holidayConflictInfo_(start, end) {
  var hs = _officialHolidaySetInRange_(start, end);
  var sYmd = _ymdInTz_(start);
  var eYmd = _ymdInTz_(end);
  var dates = [];
  if (hs[sYmd]) dates.push(sYmd);
  if (eYmd !== sYmd && hs[eYmd]) dates.push(eYmd);
  return { blocked: dates.length > 0, dates: dates };
}

/**
 * Weekly studio grid uses this helper directly.
 * Keep lightweight + cache-backed to avoid repeated Calendar API calls.
 */
function isPublicHoliday(dateLike) {
  try {
    var d = dateLike instanceof Date ? new Date(dateLike.getTime()) : new Date(String(dateLike || ''));
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return false;
    d.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
    var ymd = _ymdInTz_(d);

    // Fixed national holidays (TR)
    var m = d.getMonth() + 1;
    var day = d.getDate();
    if ((day === 1 && m === 1) || (day === 23 && m === 4) || (day === 1 && m === 5) ||
        (day === 19 && m === 5) || (day === 15 && m === 7) || (day === 30 && m === 8) ||
        (day === 28 && m === 10) || (day === 29 && m === 10)) {
      return true;
    }

    // Fast path cache per day.
    var cKey = _cacheKey_('isPublicHoliday', [ymd]);
    var cached = _cacheGetJson_(cKey);
    if (cached && typeof cached.v === 'boolean') return cached.v;

    // Check official holiday calendars for that day.
    var start = new Date(d.getTime());
    var end = new Date(d.getTime());
    end.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
    var set = _officialHolidaySetInRange_(start, end);
    var v = !!set[ymd];
    _cachePutJson_(cKey, { v: v }, 6 * 60 * 60); // 6h
    return v;
  } catch (_e) {
    return false;
  }
}

function assertNoOfficialHolidayBoundary_(type, start, end) {
  var info = _holidayConflictInfo_(start, end);
  if (!info.blocked) return;
  var trType = (type === 'studio' || type === 'room') ? 'Stüdyo' : 'Ekipman';
  throw new Error(trType + ' rezervasyonunda resmi tatilde teslim/iade yapılamaz: ' + info.dates.join(', '));
}

function validateBookingDateTime(type, start_dt, end_dt, user) {
  if (!start_dt || !end_dt) throw new Error('Start and end date/time are required.');
  const start = new Date(start_dt); const end = new Date(end_dt);
  if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime())) throw new Error('Invalid format.');
  if (end <= start) throw new Error('End time must be after start time.');
  assertNoOfficialHolidayBoundary_(type, start, end);
  const openHour = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_open_hour') || '9', 10);
  const closeHour = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_close_hour') || '16', 10);
  const lastCheckin = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_last_checkin') || '15', 10);
  const lastCheckinMin = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_last_checkin_minute') || '30', 10);
  const lunchStart = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('lunch_start') || '12', 10);
  const lunchEnd = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('lunch_end') || '13', 10);
  const startH = start.getHours(); const startM = start.getMinutes(); const startDay = start.getDay();
  const isEq = type === 'equipment'; const isRoom = type === 'room' || type === 'studio';
  var isAdmin = user && (isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
  if (!isAdmin && isEq) {
    if (startDay === 0 || startDay === 6) throw new Error('No weekend pickup.');
    if (startH < openHour) throw new Error('Opens at ' + openHour + ':00.');
    if (startH > closeHour || (startH === closeHour && startM > 0)) throw new Error('Last equipment pickup slot is ' + closeHour + ':00.');
    const endH = end.getHours(); const endM = end.getMinutes();
    var lastRM = isNaN(lastCheckinMin) ? 30 : lastCheckinMin;
    if (endH > lastCheckin || (endH === lastCheckin && endM > lastRM)) {
      throw new Error('Last depot return is ' + lastCheckin + ':' + (lastRM < 10 ? '0' : '') + lastRM + '.');
    }
    if (startH >= lunchStart && startH < lunchEnd) throw new Error('Closed for lunch 12:00–13:00.');
    if (startM !== 0 && startM !== 30) throw new Error('30-minute slots only.');
    const endEM = end.getMinutes();
    if (endEM !== 0 && endEM !== 30) throw new Error('30-minute slots only.');
  }
  if (isEq) {
    try {
      assertDepotSlotCapacity_(start_dt, end_dt, '', {});
    } catch (slotEx) {
      throw slotEx;
    }
  }
  const diffDays = (end - start) / 86400000;
  if (isEq) {
    var maxEq = isAdmin ? Math.max(2, parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('max_reservation_days_admin') || '30', 10) || 30) : getMaxEquipmentReservationDays(user || {});
    if (diffDays > maxEq + 1e-9) throw new Error('EQUIPMENT_MAX_DAYS:' + maxEq);
  }
  if (isRoom) {
    var maxRoom = getMaxStudioReservationDaySpan(user || {});
    if (diffDays > maxRoom + 1e-9) throw new Error('STUDIO_MAX_DAYS:' + maxRoom);
  }
  if (!isAdmin && isRoom) {
    if (startM !== 0) throw new Error('Studio: hourly slots only (start at :00).');
    if (end.getMinutes() !== 0) throw new Error('Studio: hourly slots only (end at :00).');
  }
}

/** Level 4 extend: depot return window + max 4 calendar days from original handover (not normal 2-day cap). */
function validateEquipmentExtendReturn(start_dt, end_dt, user) {
  if (!start_dt || !end_dt) throw new Error('Start and end date/time are required.');
  var start = new Date(start_dt); var end = new Date(end_dt);
  if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime())) throw new Error('Invalid format.');
  if (end <= start) throw new Error('End time must be after start time.');
  var isAdmin = user && (isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
  var lastCheckin = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_last_checkin') || '15', 10);
  var lastCheckinMinEx = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_last_checkin_minute') || '30', 10);
  if (!isAdmin) {
    var endH = end.getHours(); var endM = end.getMinutes();
    var lastRMex = isNaN(lastCheckinMinEx) ? 30 : lastCheckinMinEx;
    if (endH > lastCheckin || (endH === lastCheckin && endM > lastRMex)) {
      throw new Error('Last depot return is ' + lastCheckin + ':' + (lastRMex < 10 ? '0' : '') + lastRMex + '.');
    }
    if (endM !== 0 && endM !== 30) throw new Error('30-minute slots only.');
  }
  var extendMax = 4;
  var spanDays = (end - start) / 86400000;
  if (spanDays > extendMax + 1e-9) throw new Error('EXTEND_MAX_DAYS:' + extendMax);
}

function reservationsCheckSlot(payload) {
  const [h, m] = (payload.time || '').split(':').map(Number); if (isNaN(h) || isNaN(m)) return { available: false, reason: 'Invalid format.' };
  const lunchStart = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('lunch_start') || '12', 10);
  const lunchEnd = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('lunch_end') || '13', 10);
  const openHour = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_open_hour') || '9', 10);
  const closeHour = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_close_hour') || '16', 10);
  if (h < openHour) return { available: false, reason: 'Opens at ' + openHour + ':00.' };
  if (h > closeHour || (h === closeHour && m > 0)) return { available: false, reason: 'Last pickup slot is ' + closeHour + ':00.' };
  if (h >= lunchStart && h < lunchEnd) return { available: false, reason: 'Lunch break.' };
  if (m !== 0 && m !== 30) return { available: false, reason: '30-min slots only.' };
  return { available: true };
}

function reservationsCreate(payload, user) {
  const isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role); const isEq = payload.type === 'equipment';
  const uEnrich = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
  const banCheck = restrictionsCheckBan(user.id); if (banCheck.banned) throw new Error('Account suspended: ' + banCheck.reason);
  if (isEq && !isAdmin) {
    const allRes = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_(); const invAll = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY));
    const sidChk = String(user.id || '').trim();
    const hasActiveRes = allRes.some(r => String(r.student_id || r['Student_ID'] || r.user_id || '').trim() === sidChk && [STATUS.PENDING, STATUS.APPROVED].includes(String(r.status || r['Onay Durumu'] || '').toLowerCase()));
    if (hasActiveRes) throw new Error('Active reservation exists.');
    const hasEquipment = invAll.some(i => String(i['Student_ID']||i.assigned_to||'') === String(user.id) && ['IN_USE','IN USE','TAKEN'].includes(String(i['Status']||i.status||'').toUpperCase()));
    if (hasEquipment) throw new Error('Equipment already checked out.');
    if (payload.item_ids && payload.item_ids.length) {
      const userAllowed = getAllowedEqLevelStrings(uEnrich);
      const EQ_LBL_RES = { TEMEL: '1', ORTA: '2', 'İLERİ': '3', ILERI: '3', PRO: '4', SENIOR: '5' };
      payload.item_ids.forEach(iid => {
        const itm = invAll.find(i => String(i['Equipment_ID'] || i.id || '').trim() === iid);
        if (!itm) return;
        const lp = parseEquipmentLevelCell_(itm['Ekipman Seviyesi'] || itm['Ekipman seviyesi'] || '');
        const el = EQ_LBL_RES[lp.levelToken] || lp.levelToken || '1';
        if (!userAllowed.includes(String(el).toUpperCase()) && !_hasActiveSpecialEquipmentAccessForItem_(uEnrich, iid)) throw new Error((itm['Equipment_Name'] || itm.name || iid) + ': insufficient access level.');
      });
    }
    if (payload.item_ids && payload.item_ids.length > 1) { const cartValidation = inventoryValidateCart({ item_ids: payload.item_ids }, user); if (!cartValidation.valid) throw new Error(cartValidation.error); }
  }
  validateBookingDateTime(payload.type || (isEq ? 'equipment' : 'room'), payload.start_dt, payload.end_dt, uEnrich);
  const itemsToBook = payload.item_ids || (payload.item_id ? [payload.item_id] : []); if (!itemsToBook.length) throw new Error('No items selected.');
  itemsToBook.forEach(iid => { const chk = reservationsCheckAvailability({ item_id: iid, start_dt: payload.start_dt, end_dt: payload.end_dt }); if (!chk.available) throw new Error('Date conflict for: ' + iid); });
  const sheet = _supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_() ? null : getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS); const resId = 'RES-' + Utilities.getUuid().substring(0,8).toUpperCase(); const invAll2 = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY));
  var tsCreate = now();
  var rowsToUpsert = [];
  itemsToBook.forEach(function(iid) {
    var itm = invAll2.find(function(i){ return String(i.id || i['Equipment_ID']||'').trim() === iid; }) || {};
    var eqCat = String(itm.type_desc || itm['Ekipman Türü'] || itm['Ekipman Turu'] || '').trim();
    var rowObj = {
      reservation_group_id: resId,
      equipment_id: iid,
      equipment_name: String(itm.name || itm['Equipment_Name'] || ''),
      equipment_category: eqCat,
      student_id: String(user.id),
      student_name: String(user.name || ''),
      handover_date: payload.start_dt,
      return_date: payload.end_dt,
      status: 'Pending',
      approver_email: '',
      purpose: payload.purpose || '',
      created_at: tsCreate,
      updated_at: tsCreate
    };
    if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
      rowsToUpsert.push(rowObj);
    } else {
      addRow(sheet, rowObj, RESH);
      trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_({
        equipment_id: iid,
        equipment_name: String(itm.name || itm['Equipment_Name'] || ''),
        equipment_category: eqCat,
        student_id: String(user.id),
        student_name: String(user.name || ''),
        handover_date: payload.start_dt,
        return_date: payload.end_dt,
        status: 'Pending',
        approver_email: '',
        reservation_group_id: resId,
        purpose: payload.purpose || ''
      });
    }
  });
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(rowsToUpsert);
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.flush(); notifyAdmins('reservation.new', 'New request: ' + resId, resId); audit('reservation.create', user.id, resId, null, payload); return { success: true, res_id: resId, items: itemsToBook.length };
}

function reservationsApprove(payload,actor) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.APPROVED, String(_reservationActorEmail_(actor) || ''), '');
    var oldS = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_().find(function(r) { return _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim(); }) || {};
    var sidS = String(oldS.student_id || oldS['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
    sendNotif(sidS, 'reservation.approved', 'Approved.', payload.id);
    audit('reservation.approve', actor.id, payload.id, oldS, Object.assign({}, oldS, { status: STATUS.APPROVED }));
    return Object.assign({}, oldS, { status: STATUS.APPROVED, approver_email: _reservationActorEmail_(actor), updated_at: now() });
  }
  if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_()) {
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.APPROVED, String(actor.id || ''), '');
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjs(sheet).find(r => _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim());
  const actorEm = _reservationActorEmail_(actor);
  const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.APPROVED, approver_email: actorEm, updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sheet, rn, up, RESH);
  trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(payload.id);
  var sid = String(old.student_id || old['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
  sendNotif(sid, 'reservation.approved', 'Approved.', payload.id);
  var u1 = _mailUserByReservationId(sid);
  var unm = String(old.student_name || old['Student_Name'] || '').trim();
  if (u1.email) sendReservationDecisionMail_(u1.email, unm || u1.name, String(payload.id), true, '', '');
  audit('reservation.approve', actor.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}
function reservationsReject(payload,actor) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.REJECTED, String(_reservationActorEmail_(actor) || ''), String(payload.reason || ''));
    var oldR = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_().find(function(r) { return _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim(); }) || {};
    var sidR = String(oldR.student_id || oldR['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
    sendNotif(sidR, 'reservation.rejected', 'Rejected.', payload.id);
    audit('reservation.reject', actor.id, payload.id, oldR, Object.assign({}, oldR, { status: STATUS.REJECTED }));
    return Object.assign({}, oldR, { status: STATUS.REJECTED, approver_email: _reservationActorEmail_(actor), updated_at: now() });
  }
  if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_()) {
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.REJECTED, String(actor.id || ''), String(payload.reason || ''));
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjs(sheet).find(r => _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim());
  const actorEm2 = _reservationActorEmail_(actor);
  const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.REJECTED, approver_email: actorEm2, updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sheet, rn, up, RESH);
  trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(payload.id);
  var sid2 = String(old.student_id || old['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
  sendNotif(sid2, 'reservation.rejected', 'Rejected.', payload.id);
  var u2 = _mailUserByReservationId(sid2);
  var rsn = String(payload.reason || '').trim();
  var unm2 = String(old.student_name || old['Student_Name'] || '').trim();
  if (u2.email) sendReservationDecisionMail_(u2.email, unm2 || u2.name, String(payload.id), false, '', rsn);
  audit('reservation.reject', actor.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}
function reservationsCancel(payload,user) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var oldC = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_().find(function(r) { return _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim(); }) || null;
    if (!oldC) throw new Error('Not found.');
    var sidC = String(oldC.student_id || oldC['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
    if (sidC !== String(user.id||'').trim() && !isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) throw new Error('Denied.');
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.CANCELLED, '', '');
    audit('reservation.cancel', user.id, payload.id, oldC, Object.assign({}, oldC, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED }));
    return Object.assign({}, oldC, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() });
  }
  if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_()) {
    _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(payload.id, STATUS.CANCELLED, '', '');
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjs(sheet).find(r => _reservationRowGroupId_(r) === String(payload.id || '').trim());
  var sid3 = String(old.student_id || old['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
  if (sid3 !== String(user.id||'').trim() && !isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) throw new Error('Denied.');
  const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sheet, rn, up, RESH);
  trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(payload.id);
  audit('reservation.cancel', user.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}
function reservationsCheckAvailability(payload) {
  return reservationsCheckAvailabilityExcludingGroup(Object.assign({}, payload, { exclude_group_id: payload.exclude_group_id || '' }));
}
/** Sheet'teki Onay Durumu hücresi — İngilizce + Türkçe; bitmiş/iptal satırları çakışma sayılmaz. */
function _reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(statusCell) {
  var raw = String(statusCell || '').trim();
  if (!raw) return false;
  var s = raw.toLowerCase();
  var norm = s.replace(/ı/g, 'i').replace(/ğ/g, 'g').replace(/ü/g, 'u').replace(/ş/g, 's').replace(/ö/g, 'o').replace(/ç/g, 'c');
  if (/cancel|cancelled|canceled|iptal|reject|rejected|redd|tamamlan|completed|closed|returned|iade|delivered/.test(norm)) return false;
  if (/^(pending|approved|picked up)$/.test(s)) return true;
  if (/beklemede|bekliyor|onay bekle|pending|onaylandi|onaylandı|approved|picked|teslim al|pick\s*up|aktif rez|in progress/.test(norm)) return true;
  return false;
}

function _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(d) {
  var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul';
  if (!(d instanceof Date) || isNaN(d.getTime())) return '';
  var ymd = Utilities.formatDate(d, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
  var hh = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(d, tz, 'HH'), 10);
  var mm = parseInt(Utilities.formatDate(d, tz, 'mm'), 10);
  if (isNaN(hh) || isNaN(mm)) return '';
  var slotM = mm < 30 ? 0 : 30;
  var pad = function(n) { return (n < 10 ? '0' : '') + n; };
  return ymd + '_' + pad(hh) + '-' + pad(slotM);
}

function getDepotSlotUsage_(slotKey, excludeGroupId) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var rowsSrc = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_();
    var handoverGids0 = {};
    var returnGids0 = {};
    for (var z = 0; z < rowsSrc.length; z++) {
      var rr = rowsSrc[z];
      if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(rr.status)) continue;
      var gid0 = String(rr.reservation_group_id || '').trim();
      if (!gid0) continue;
      if (excludeGroupId && gid0 === excludeGroupId) continue;
      if (rr.handover_date) {
        var hk0 = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(new Date(rr.handover_date));
        if (hk0 === slotKey) handoverGids0[gid0] = true;
      }
      if (rr.return_date) {
        var rk0 = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(new Date(rr.return_date));
        if (rk0 === slotKey) returnGids0[gid0] = true;
      }
    }
    var all0 = {};
    for (var h0 in handoverGids0) all0[h0] = true;
    for (var r0 in returnGids0) all0[r0] = true;
    return {
      pickupCount: Object.keys(handoverGids0).length,
      returnCount: Object.keys(returnGids0).length,
      totalDistinct: Object.keys(all0).length
    };
  }
  var data = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS).getDataRange().getValues();
  var c = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
  var handoverGids = {};
  var returnGids = {};
  for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    var row = data[i];
    if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(row[c.status])) continue;
    var gid = String(row[c.group] || '').trim();
    if (!gid) continue;
    if (excludeGroupId && gid === excludeGroupId) continue;
    if (row[c.handover]) {
      var hk = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(new Date(row[c.handover]));
      if (hk === slotKey) handoverGids[gid] = true;
    }
    if (row[c.ret]) {
      var rk = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(new Date(row[c.ret]));
      if (rk === slotKey) returnGids[gid] = true;
    }
  }
  var all = {};
  for (var h in handoverGids) all[h] = true;
  for (var r in returnGids) all[r] = true;
  return {
    pickupCount: Object.keys(handoverGids).length,
    returnCount: Object.keys(returnGids).length,
    totalDistinct: Object.keys(all).length
  };
}

function _depotSlotCapacityErrorEn_(slotKey, congestedRole, usage, maxB) {
  var parts = (slotKey || '').split('_');
  var datePart = parts[0] || '';
  var hm = (parts[1] || '').split('-');
  var timeLabel = hm.length >= 2 ? (hm[0] + ':' + hm[1]) : '';
  var p = usage.pickupCount;
  var r0 = usage.returnCount;
  var trafficHint = '';
  if (congestedRole === 'both') {
    trafficHint = 'This 30-minute window mixes handover (pickup) and return (drop-off) appointments and is at capacity. ';
  } else if (p > 0 && r0 > 0) {
    trafficHint = 'This 30-minute window is at capacity with both handover (pickup) and return traffic. ';
  } else if (congestedRole === 'handover' || (p > r0 && p > 0)) {
    trafficHint = 'The congestion is mainly from equipment pickup (handover) appointments. ';
  } else {
    trafficHint = 'The congestion is mainly from equipment return (drop-off) appointments. ';
  }
  return 'Because of depot equipment handover/return congestion at your selected time, please choose another 30-minute window. ' + trafficHint +
    'The slot starting ' + datePart + ' ' + timeLabel + ' (30 min) already has ' + usage.totalDistinct + '/' + maxB + ' reservation(s). ' +
    'Current mix: ' + p + ' handover (pickup) booking(s) and ' + r0 + ' return (drop-off) booking(s).';
}

function assertDepotSlotCapacity_(start_dt, end_dt, excludeGroupId, options) {
  options = options || {};
  var maxB = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('depot_slot_max_bookings') || '4', 10) || 4;
  var checkStart = options.checkStart !== false;
  var checkEnd = options.checkEnd !== false;
  var start = new Date(start_dt);
  var end = new Date(end_dt);
  if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime())) return;
  var skStart = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(start);
  var skEnd = _depotSlotKeyFromDate_(end);
  function check(slotKey, roleLabel) {
    if (!slotKey) return;
    var u = getDepotSlotUsage_(slotKey, excludeGroupId);
    if (u.totalDistinct >= maxB) {
      throw new Error(_depotSlotCapacityErrorEn_(slotKey, roleLabel, u, maxB));
    }
  }
  if (checkStart && checkEnd && skStart === skEnd) {
    check(skStart, 'both');
  } else {
    if (checkStart) check(skStart, 'handover');
    if (checkEnd) check(skEnd, 'return');
  }
}

function reservationsCheckAvailabilityExcludingGroup(payload) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var rows = _equipmentReservationRowsSource_();
    var itemId0 = String(payload.item_id || '').trim();
    var excludeGid0 = String(payload.exclude_group_id || '').trim();
    var s0 = new Date(payload.start_dt).getTime();
    var e0 = new Date(payload.end_dt).getTime();
    if (isNaN(s0) || isNaN(e0)) return { available: false, conflict: { reason: 'bad_range' } };
    for (var j = 0; j < rows.length; j++) {
      var rw = rows[j];
      if (String(rw.equipment_id || '').trim() !== itemId0) continue;
      var gidX = String(rw.reservation_group_id || '').trim();
      if (excludeGid0 && gidX === excludeGid0) continue;
      if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(rw.status)) continue;
      var rs0 = new Date(rw.handover_date).getTime();
      var re0 = new Date(rw.return_date).getTime();
      if (isNaN(rs0) || isNaN(re0)) continue;
      if (s0 < re0 && e0 > rs0) return { available: false, conflict: { group_id: gidX } };
    }
    return { available: true, conflict: null };
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  const c = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
  const itemId = String(payload.item_id || '').trim();
  const excludeGid = String(payload.exclude_group_id || '').trim();
  const s = new Date(payload.start_dt).getTime();
  const e = new Date(payload.end_dt).getTime();
  if (isNaN(s) || isNaN(e)) return { available: false, conflict: { reason: 'bad_range' } };
  for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    const row = data[i];
    const eqId = String(row[c.eqId] || '').trim();
    if (eqId !== itemId) continue;
    const gid = String(row[c.group] || '').trim();
    if (excludeGid && gid === excludeGid) continue;
    const stCell = row[c.status];
    if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(stCell)) continue;
    const rs = new Date(row[c.handover]).getTime();
    const re = new Date(row[c.ret]).getTime();
    if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) continue;
    if (s < re && e > rs) return { available: false, conflict: { group_id: gid } };
  }
  return { available: true, conflict: null };
}
function reservationsGetCalendar(payload, user) {
  if (!payload.from || !payload.to) throw new Error('Dates required.');
  const from = new Date(payload.from).getTime(); const to = new Date(payload.to + 'T23:59:59').getTime();
  let list = reservationsList({}, user).filter(r => r.status !== STATUS.CANCELLED && r.status !== STATUS.REJECTED).filter(r => new Date(r.start_dt).getTime() <= to && new Date(r.end_dt).getTime() >= from);
  if (payload.type) list = list.filter(r => r.type === payload.type);
  if (user.role === ROLES.STUDENT) list = list.filter(r => r.user_id === user.id);
  const invMap = {}; const roomMap = {}; toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)).forEach(i => invMap[i.id] = i.name); toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.ROOMS)).forEach(r => roomMap[r.id] = r.room_name);
  return list.map(r => ({ ...r, item_name: r.type === 'equipment' ? (invMap[r.item_id] || r.item_id) : (roomMap[r.item_id] || r.item_id) }));
}

const AH=['id','student_id','instructor_id','title','description','start_dt','deadline','equip_id','location','status','approved','approved_by','approved_at','completed_at','notes','created_by','created_at','updated_at'];
function assignmentsList(payload,user) { let list=toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS)); if(user.role===ROLES.STUDENT) list=list.filter(a=>a.student_id===user.id); if(user.role===ROLES.INSTRUCTOR) list=list.filter(a=>a.instructor_id===user.id); if(payload.student_id) list=list.filter(a=>a.student_id===payload.student_id); if(payload.instructor_id) list=list.filter(a=>a.instructor_id===payload.instructor_id); if(payload.status) list=list.filter(a=>a.status===payload.status); if(payload.search) list=multiSearch(list,payload.search,['title','description','notes','location']); return list; }

function assignmentsCreate(payload,actor) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS); const asgn=Object.assign({id:genId('ASGN'),status:STATUS.PENDING,approved:false,created_by:actor.id,created_at:now(),updated_at:now()},payload); addRow(sheet,asgn,AH); sendNotif(asgn.student_id,'assignment.new','New task: '+asgn.title,asgn.id); audit('assignment.create',actor.id,asgn.id,null,asgn); return asgn; }
function assignmentsUpdate(payload,actor) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS); const rn=findRow(sheet,payload.id); if(rn===-1) throw new Error('Not found.'); const old=toObjs(sheet).find(a=>a.id===payload.id); const up=Object.assign({},old,payload,{updated_at:now()}); setRow(sheet,rn,up,AH); audit('assignment.update',actor.id,payload.id,old,up); return up; }
function assignmentsApprove(payload,actor) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS); const rn=findRow(sheet,payload.id); if(rn===-1) throw new Error('Not found.'); const old=toObjs(sheet).find(a=>a.id===payload.id); const up=Object.assign({},old,{approved:true,status:STATUS.APPROVED,approved_by:actor.id,approved_at:now(),updated_at:now()}); setRow(sheet,rn,up,AH); sendNotif(old.student_id,'assignment.approved','Task approved: '+old.title,payload.id); audit('assignment.approve',actor.id,payload.id,old,up); return up; }
function assignmentsComplete(payload,user) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS); const rn=findRow(sheet,payload.id); if(rn===-1) throw new Error('Not found.'); const old=toObjs(sheet).find(a=>a.id===payload.id); if(old.student_id!==user.id&&!isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) throw new Error('Denied.'); const up=Object.assign({},old,{status:STATUS.COMPLETED,completed_at:now(),updated_at:now()}); setRow(sheet,rn,up,AH); sendNotif(old.instructor_id,'assignment.completed','Task completed: '+old.title,payload.id); audit('assignment.complete',user.id,payload.id,old,up); return up; }
function assignmentsDelete(id,actor) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS); const rn=findRow(sheet,id); if(rn===-1) throw new Error('Not found.'); sheet.deleteRow(rn); audit('assignment.delete',actor.id,id,null,null); return {deleted:true}; }

// ── RESTRICTIONS & BANS ──────────────────────────────
const BAH = ['id','user_id','user_name','ban_level','reason','banned_by','banned_at','expires_at','active','notes'];
function restrictionsCheckBan(userId) {
  try {
    const bans = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(b => String(b.user_id) === String(userId) && b.active === true);
    if (!bans.length) return { banned: false }; const b = bans[0];
    if (b.expires_at && new Date(b.expires_at) < new Date()) { const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.BANS); const rn = findRow(sheet, b.id); if (rn !== -1) { const up = Object.assign({}, b, { active: false }); setRow(sheet, rn, up, BAH); } return { banned: false }; }
    return { banned: true, reason: b.reason || '', expires_at: b.expires_at || null, ban_id: b.id };
  } catch(e) { return { banned: false }; }
}
function restrictionsBanUser(payload, actor) {
  if (!payload.user_id || !payload.reason) throw new Error('user_id and reason required.');
  const existing = restrictionsCheckBan(payload.user_id); if (existing.banned) throw new Error('Already suspended.');
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.BANS); const ban = { id: genId('BAN'), user_id: String(payload.user_id), user_name: payload.user_name || '', ban_level: payload.ban_level || 'manual', reason: payload.reason, banned_by: actor.id, banned_at: now(), expires_at: payload.expires_at || '', active: true, notes: payload.notes || '' };
  addRow(sheet, ban, BAH); sendNotif(payload.user_id, 'ban.applied', 'Suspended: ' + payload.reason, ban.id); notifyAdmins('ban.applied', payload.user_name + ' banned.', ban.id); audit('ban.apply', actor.id, payload.user_id, null, ban); return ban;
}
function restrictionsUnbanUser(payload, actor) {
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.BANS); let rn = -1, ban = null;
  if (payload.ban_id) { rn = findRow(sheet, payload.ban_id); ban = toObjs(sheet).find(b => b.id === payload.ban_id); }
  else if (payload.user_id) { ban = toObjs(sheet).find(b => String(b.user_id) === String(payload.user_id) && b.active === true); if (ban) rn = findRow(sheet, ban.id); }
  if (rn === -1 || !ban) throw new Error('No active ban.');
  const up = Object.assign({}, ban, { active: false, notes: (ban.notes||'') + ' | Kaldıran: ' + actor.id });
  setRow(sheet, rn, up, BAH); sendNotif(ban.user_id, 'ban.lifted', 'Suspension lifted.', ban.id); audit('ban.lift', actor.id, ban.user_id, ban, up); return { unban: true, user_id: ban.user_id };
}
function restrictionsListBans(payload) { payload = payload || {}; let list = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)); if (payload.active_only) list = list.filter(b => b.active === true); return list.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.banned_at) - new Date(a.banned_at)); }

function resolveLevelFromEmail(email, studentId) {
  try {
    const deptLookup = getDeptCodeLookup(); const isStaff = (email || '').includes('@bilgi.edu.tr'); if (isStaff) return '2';
    const sid = String(studentId || '').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '');
    if (sid.length >= 5) { const code2 = sid.substring(3, 5); const code3 = sid.substring(3, 6); const match = deptLookup[code2] || deptLookup[code3]; if (match) return match.level || '1'; }
    return '1';
  } catch(e) { return '1'; }
}
function getDeptCodeLookup() {
  try {
    const cache = CacheService.getScriptCache(); const cached = cache.get('dept_lookup'); if (cached) return JSON.parse(cached);
    const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.DEPT_CODES); const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues(); const lookup = {};
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) { const code = String(data[i][0] || '').trim(); if (code) lookup[code] = { name: String(data[i][1] || '').trim(), abbr: String(data[i][2] || '').trim(), level: String(data[i][3] || '1').trim().toUpperCase() }; }
    cache.put('dept_lookup', JSON.stringify(lookup), 300); return lookup;
  } catch(e) { return {}; }
}

function _isPodcastStudioByFields_(studioId, studioName) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid === 'PODCAST') return true;
  var sn = String(studioName || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  return sn.indexOf('PODCAST') >= 0;
}
function _fmtTrMailDate_(v) {
  try {
    var d = new Date(v);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(v || '');
    return Utilities.formatDate(d, 'GMT+3', 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm');
  } catch (_e) { return String(v || ''); }
}
function notifyIiwAdminsPodcastPendingMail_(res, requester) {
  try {
    if (!res || !_isPodcastStudioByFields_(res.studio_id, res.studio_name)) return { ok: true, skipped: true };
    var users = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.USERS)) || [];
    var recips = users.filter(function(u) {
      var role = String(u.role || u.yetki || u['Yetki'] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var em = String(u.email || u['E-Posta'] || '').trim();
      return role === 'iiw_admin' && em.indexOf('@') >= 0;
    });
    if (!recips.length) return { ok: true, skipped: true, reason: 'no_iiw_admin_email' };
    var reqName = String((requester && requester.name) || res.user_name || '').trim();
    var reqEmail = String((requester && requester.email) || lookupUserEmailById_(res.user_id) || '').trim();
    var reqId = String(res.user_id || '').trim();
    var startLabel = _fmtTrMailDate_(res.start_dt);
    var endLabel = _fmtTrMailDate_(res.end_dt);
    var purpose = String(res.purpose || '').trim() || '-';
    var reqType = String(res.request_type || '').trim() || '-';
    var subject = '[BookDeck] Podcast Stüdyosu Yeni Rezervasyon - Onayınız Bekleniyor';
    var html =
      '<p>IIW Admin merhaba,</p>' +
      '<p>Podcast stüdyosu için yeni bir rezervasyon talebi oluşturuldu. Onayınız bekleniyor.</p>' +
      '<ul>' +
      '<li><strong>Rezervasyon No:</strong> ' + String(res.id || '') + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Kullanıcı:</strong> ' + reqName + (reqEmail ? (' (' + reqEmail + ')') : '') + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Kullanıcı ID:</strong> ' + reqId + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Stüdyo:</strong> ' + String(res.studio_name || res.studio_id || 'Podcast') + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Talep Türü:</strong> ' + reqType + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Amaç:</strong> ' + purpose + '</li>' +
      '<li><strong>Saat Aralığı:</strong> ' + startLabel + ' → ' + endLabel + '</li>' +
      '</ul>' +
      '<p>Admin panelinden Bekleyen Onaylar ekranına girerek işlemi tamamlayabilirsiniz.</p>' +
      '<p>BookDeck</p>';
    recips.forEach(function(u) {
      var em = String(u.email || u['E-Posta'] || '').trim();
      if (em) sendMail(em, subject, html);
    });
    return { ok: true, sent: recips.length };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}
function notificationsList(user) { return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.NOTIFICATIONS)).filter(n=>n.recipient_id===user.id).sort((a,b)=>new Date(b.sent_at)-new Date(a.sent_at)); }
function notificationsMarkRead(id,user) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.NOTIFICATIONS); const rn=findRow(sheet,id); if(rn===-1) throw new Error('Not found.'); const old=toObjs(sheet).find(n=>n.id===id); const up=Object.assign({},old,{is_read:true}); setRow(sheet,rn,up,NH); return up; }
/**
 * Posta: yalnızca Gmail / MailApp (web app "Execute as: Me" → örn. ekipmanrezervasyon@gmail.com).
 * Microsoft Graph ve SERVICE_ACCOUNT_EMAIL yolu kaldırıldı.
 */
function sendMail(to, subject, html, options) {
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var fromName = String(props.getProperty('MAIL_FROM_NAME') || 'Bilgi Booking').trim() || 'Bilgi Booking';
  var plainBody = String(html || '').replace(/<[^>]*>/g, ' ').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').trim();
  if (!to || String(to).indexOf('@') < 0) return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid recipient.' };
  try {
    var payload = {
      to: String(to),
      subject: String(subject || ''),
      htmlBody: String(html || ''),
      body: plainBody || 'Bilgi Booking',
      name: fromName
    };
    if (options && options.attachments && options.attachments.length) payload.attachments = options.attachments;
    MailApp.sendEmail(payload);
    return { ok: true, channel: 'mailapp' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e && e.message ? e.message : String(e) };
  }
}

function resolveDeliveryPdfRecipientEmail_(userKey) {
  var raw = String(userKey || '').trim();
  if (!raw) return '';
  if (raw.indexOf('@') >= 0) return raw;
  try {
    var lu = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(raw);
    var em = String((lu && lu.email) || '').trim();
    if (em && em.indexOf('@') >= 0) return em;
  } catch (_eLu) {}
  return '';
}

function _driveFileIdFromUrl_(url) {
  var s = String(url || '').trim();
  if (!s) return '';
  var m1 = s.match(/\/d\/([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
  if (m1 && m1[1]) return m1[1];
  var m2 = s.match(/[?&]id=([a-zA-Z0-9_-]+)/);
  if (m2 && m2[1]) return m2[1];
  return '';
}

function mailDeliveryPdfCopyToBorrower_(userKey, userName, pdfUrl, formLabel, meta) {
  try {
    var url = String(pdfUrl || '').trim();
    if (!url) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing_pdf_url' };
    var to = resolveDeliveryPdfRecipientEmail_(userKey);
    if (!to) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing_recipient_email' };
    var nm = String(userName || '').trim() || 'Öğrenci';
    var lbl = String(formLabel || 'Teslim formu').trim();
    var subject = '[BookDeck] ' + lbl + ' kopyanız';
    var resId = String(meta && meta.resId || '').trim();
    var handover = String(meta && meta.handoverDate || '').trim();
    var ret = String(meta && meta.returnDate || '').trim();
    var details = '';
    if (resId) details += '<li><strong>Rezervasyon No:</strong> ' + resId + '</li>';
    if (handover) details += '<li><strong>Teslim:</strong> ' + handover + '</li>';
    if (ret) details += '<li><strong>İade:</strong> ' + ret + '</li>';
    var detailsHtml = details ? ('<ul>' + details + '</ul>') : '';
    var fileId = _driveFileIdFromUrl_(url);
    var attachments = [];
    if (fileId) {
      try {
        var blob = DriveApp.getFileById(fileId).getBlob();
        blob.setName((resId ? (resId + '_') : '') + 'teslim-formu.pdf');
        attachments.push(blob);
      } catch (_eBlob) {}
    }
    var html =
      '<p>Merhaba ' + nm + ',</p>' +
      '<p>İşleminize ait <strong>' + lbl + '</strong> oluşturuldu.</p>' +
      detailsHtml +
      '<p>PDF dosyası bu e-postaya ek olarak iliştirildi.</p>' +
      '<p>Yedek bağlantı: <a href="' + url + '" target="_blank" rel="noopener">Formu aç</a></p>' +
      '<p>BookDeck</p>';
    return sendMail(to, subject, html, { attachments: attachments });
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e && e.message ? e.message : String(e) };
  }
}

/**
 * Mail: yalnızca MailApp (Gmail). Editörden çalıştırınca aktif hesabı gösterir.
 */
function mailHealthCheck() {
  try {
    var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var fromName = String(props.getProperty('MAIL_FROM_NAME') || 'Bilgi Booking').trim();
    var effective = '';
    try { effective = Session.getEffectiveUser().getEmail(); } catch (e1) {}
    if (!effective) {
      try { effective = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail(); } catch (e2) {}
    }
    var quota = null;
    try { quota = MailApp.getRemainingDailyQuota(); } catch (eQ) {}
    return {
      ok: true,
      route: 'mailapp',
      sender: effective || '(deploy hesabı / editorde calistirin)',
      fromName: fromName,
      remainingDailyQuota: quota,
      note: 'Tüm mail MailApp ile; Web app Execute as: Me ile deploy eden Gmail hesabından gider. Microsoft Graph kullanılmıyor.'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

/**
 * Editor'den calistirinca mail durumunu log'a basar.
 */
function mailHealthCheckLog() {
  var r = mailHealthCheck();
  Logger.log(JSON.stringify(r));
  return r;
}

/**
 * Editörden bir kez çalıştırın (deploy hesabıyla, örn. ekipmanrezervasyon@gmail.com).
 * MailApp için `script.send_mail` izin penceresini açar; onaylayın. Web app bundan sonra OTP gönderebilir.
 * Proje ayarlarında appsscript.json içinde oauthScopes satırında bu izin olmalı:
 * https://www.googleapis.com/auth/script.send_mail
 */
function authorizeMailSendPermission() {
  var me = '';
  try { me = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail(); } catch (e1) {}
  if (!me) {
    try { me = Session.getEffectiveUser().getEmail(); } catch (e2) {}
  }
  if (!me) {
    throw new Error('Aktif kullanıcı e-postası alınamadı. Apps Script editöründe doğru Google hesabıyla açın.');
  }
  MailApp.sendEmail(me, '[BookDeck] Mail izni testi', 'Bu mesajı görüyorsanız MailApp izni tamam.');
  return { ok: true, sentTo: me };
}

function _mailRememberSent(key) {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    if (p.getProperty(key)) return true;
    p.setProperty(key, now());
    return false;
  } catch (e) { return false; }
}

function _mailUserByReservationId(userIdOrEmail) {
  var q = String(userIdOrEmail || '').trim();
  if (!q) return { email: '', name: '' };
  if (q.indexOf('@') >= 0) {
    var u1 = getUserByEmail(q);
    return { email: q, name: (u1 && u1.name) || '' };
  }
  var lu = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(q);
  if (lu && lu.ok && lu.email && lu.email.indexOf('@') >= 0) return { email: lu.email, name: lu.name || '' };
  return { email: '', name: '' };
}

function sendReservationCreatedMail_(email, userName, resId, startDt, endDt, items) {
  if (!email) return;
  var itemList = (items || []).map(function(it) { return '<li>' + it + '</li>'; }).join('');
  var body = '<p><strong>TR</strong></p>' +
    '<p>Sayin ' + (userName || '') + ',</p>' +
    '<p>Ekipman rezervasyonunuz olusturuldu.</p>' +
    '<p><strong>Rezervasyon ID:</strong> ' + resId + '<br><strong>Teslim:</strong> ' + startDt + '<br><strong>Iade:</strong> ' + endDt + '</p>' +
    (itemList ? '<p><strong>Ekipmanlar:</strong></p><ul>' + itemList + '</ul>' : '') +
    '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
    '<p><strong>EN</strong></p>' +
    '<p>Dear ' + (userName || '') + ',</p>' +
    '<p>Your equipment reservation has been created.</p>' +
    '<p><strong>Reservation ID:</strong> ' + resId + '<br><strong>Pickup:</strong> ' + startDt + '<br><strong>Return:</strong> ' + endDt + '</p>' +
    (itemList ? '<p><strong>Items:</strong></p><ul>' + itemList + '</ul>' : '') +
    '<p>Bilgi Booking</p>';
  sendMail(email, '[Bilgi Booking] Rezervasyon olusturuldu / Reservation created', body);
}

function _htmlEscapeMail_(s) {
  return String(s || '')
    .replace(/&/g, '&amp;')
    .replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    .replace(/>/g, '&gt;')
    .replace(/"/g, '&quot;');
}

function sendReservationDecisionMail_(email, userName, resId, approved, note, rejectReason) {
  if (!email) return;
  var st = approved ? 'onaylandi' : 'reddedildi';
  var stEn = approved ? 'approved' : 'rejected';
  var rr = String(rejectReason || '').trim();
  var rrEsc = rr ? _htmlEscapeMail_(rr) : '';
  var reasonBox = 'margin:8px 0;padding:10px 12px;background:#f9f9f9;border-left:3px solid #e30613;';
  var reasonTr = '';
  var reasonEn = '';
  if (!approved && rrEsc) {
    reasonTr = '<p><strong>Red gerekçesi</strong></p><p style="' + reasonBox + '">' + rrEsc + '</p>';
    reasonEn = '<p><strong>Reason for rejection</strong></p><p style="' + reasonBox + '">' + rrEsc + '</p>';
  }
  var pickupTr = '';
  var pickupEn = '';
  if (approved) {
    pickupTr = '<p>Ekipmanınızı rezervasyon saatinde <strong>E1-107</strong> depodan kimlik göstererek teslim alabilirsiniz. Zamanında teslim alınmayan cihazların rezervasyonu <strong>30 dakika</strong> sonunda iptal olur.</p>';
    pickupEn = '<p>You may pick up your equipment at the <strong>E1-107</strong> depot at the reserved time, with ID. Reservations for equipment not picked up on time are <strong>cancelled after 30 minutes</strong>.</p>';
  }
  var body = '<p><strong>TR</strong></p>' +
    '<p>Sayin ' + _htmlEscapeMail_(userName) + ',</p>' +
    '<p>' + _htmlEscapeMail_(resId) + ' numarali ekipman rezervasyonunuz <strong>' + st + '</strong>.</p>' +
    pickupTr +
    reasonTr +
    (note ? '<p><strong>Not:</strong> ' + note + '</p>' : '') +
    '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
    '<p><strong>EN</strong></p>' +
    '<p>Dear ' + _htmlEscapeMail_(userName) + ',</p>' +
    '<p>Your equipment reservation <strong>' + _htmlEscapeMail_(resId) + '</strong> has been <strong>' + stEn + '</strong>.</p>' +
    pickupEn +
    reasonEn +
    (note ? '<p><strong>Note:</strong> ' + note + '</p>' : '') +
    '<p>Bilgi Booking</p>';
  sendMail(email, '[Bilgi Booking] Rezervasyon ' + (approved ? 'Onaylandi' : 'Reddedildi') + ' / Reservation ' + stEn, body);
}

function reportsInventorySummary() { const items=toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)).filter(i=>i.status!=='deleted'); const s={total:items.length,byStatus:{},byCategory:{}}; items.forEach(i=>{s.byStatus[i.status]=(s.byStatus[i.status]||0)+1;s.byCategory[i.category]=(s.byCategory[i.category]||0)+1;}); return s; }
function reportsReservationStats(payload) { let list=reservationsList({}, { role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, id: 'SYSTEM' }); if(payload.from) list=list.filter(r=>new Date(r.created_at||r.start_dt)>=new Date(payload.from)); if(payload.to) list=list.filter(r=>new Date(r.created_at||r.start_dt)<=new Date(payload.to)); const s={total:list.length,byStatus:{},byType:{}}; list.forEach(r=>{var st=String(r.status||'');s.byStatus[st]=(s.byStatus[st]||0)+1;s.byType['equipment']=(s.byType['equipment']||0)+1;}); return s; }
function reportsAssignmentStats(payload) { let list=toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS)); if(payload.instructor_id) list=list.filter(a=>a.instructor_id===payload.instructor_id); const s={total:list.length,byStatus:{}}; list.forEach(a=>s.byStatus[a.status]=(s.byStatus[a.status]||0)+1); return s; }
function reportsOverdueItems() { const n=new Date(); return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)).filter(i=>i.status===STATUS.IN_USE&&i.due_date&&new Date(i.due_date)<n); }
function _reportsInc_(obj, key, n) {
  var k = String(key || '').trim() || 'Unknown';
  obj[k] = (obj[k] || 0) + (n || 1);
}
function _reportsDateKey_(d) {
  return Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}
function _reportsSafeDate_(v) {
  var d = new Date(v);
  return isNaN(d.getTime()) ? null : d;
}
function reportsTicketDepartmentSummary_(days) {
  var list = ticketsList({}) || [];
  var nowMs = Date.now();
  var spanMs = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30)) * 86400000;
  var dep = {};
  list.forEach(function(t) {
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(t.created_at);
    if (!cd) return;
    if (cd.getTime() < nowMs - spanMs) return;
    var d = String(t.department || 'Unknown').trim() || 'Unknown';
    if (!dep[d]) dep[d] = { department: d, total: 0, pending: 0, approved: 0, rejected: 0 };
    dep[d].total++;
    var st = String(t.status || '').toLowerCase();
    if (st.indexOf('bekle') >= 0 || st === 'pending') dep[d].pending++;
    else if (st.indexOf('onay') >= 0 || st.indexOf('approved') >= 0) dep[d].approved++;
    else if (st.indexOf('red') >= 0 || st.indexOf('reject') >= 0) dep[d].rejected++;
  });
  var arr = Object.keys(dep).map(function(k) {
    var x = dep[k];
    x.approval_rate = x.total ? Math.round((x.approved / x.total) * 1000) / 10 : 0;
    return x;
  });
  arr.sort(function(a, b) { return b.total - a.total; });
  return arr;
}
function reportsTicketTypeSummary_(days) {
  var list = ticketsList({}) || [];
  var nowMs = Date.now();
  var spanMs = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30)) * 86400000;
  var byType = {};
  list.forEach(function(t) {
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(t.created_at);
    if (!cd) return;
    if (cd.getTime() < nowMs - spanMs) return;
    _reportsInc_(byType, t.ticket_type || t.request_type || 'Unknown', 1);
  });
  return Object.keys(byType).map(function(k) { return { type: k, count: byType[k] }; }).sort(function(a, b) { return b.count - a.count; });
}
function reportsTicketStatusFunnel_(days) {
  var list = ticketsList({}) || [];
  var nowMs = Date.now();
  var spanMs = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30)) * 86400000;
  var out = { total: 0, pending: 0, approved: 0, rejected: 0 };
  list.forEach(function(t) {
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(t.created_at);
    if (!cd) return;
    if (cd.getTime() < nowMs - spanMs) return;
    out.total++;
    var st = String(t.status || '').toLowerCase();
    if (st.indexOf('bekle') >= 0 || st === 'pending') out.pending++;
    else if (st.indexOf('onay') >= 0 || st.indexOf('approved') >= 0) out.approved++;
    else if (st.indexOf('red') >= 0 || st.indexOf('reject') >= 0) out.rejected++;
  });
  return out;
}
function reportsTicketDailyTrend_(days) {
  var span = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30));
  var list = ticketsList({}) || [];
  var start = new Date();
  start.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  start.setDate(start.getDate() - (span - 1));
  var map = {};
  for (var i = 0; i < span; i++) {
    var d = new Date(start.getTime() + i * 86400000);
    map[_reportsDateKey_(d)] = 0;
  }
  list.forEach(function(t) {
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(t.created_at);
    if (!cd) return;
    var k = _reportsDateKey_(cd);
    if (map[k] === undefined) return;
    map[k]++;
  });
  return Object.keys(map).sort().map(function(k) { return { day: k, count: map[k] }; });
}
function reportsStudioUsageSummary_(days) {
  var span = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30));
  var nowMs = Date.now();
  var spanMs = span * 86400000;
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_() || [];
  var byStudio = {};
  var statusAgg = {};
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    var st = String(r.status || '').toLowerCase();
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(r.created_at || r.start_dt);
    if (!cd || cd.getTime() < nowMs - spanMs) return;
    var sid = String(r.studio_id || r.studio_name || 'Unknown').trim() || 'Unknown';
    if (!byStudio[sid]) byStudio[sid] = { studio: sid, total: 0, approved: 0, cancelled: 0, completed: 0 };
    byStudio[sid].total++;
    if (st === STATUS.APPROVED) byStudio[sid].approved++;
    if (st === STATUS.CANCELLED) byStudio[sid].cancelled++;
    if (st === STATUS.COMPLETED) byStudio[sid].completed++;
    _reportsInc_(statusAgg, st || 'unknown', 1);
  });
  return {
    by_studio: Object.keys(byStudio).map(function(k) { return byStudio[k]; }).sort(function(a, b) { return b.total - a.total; }),
    by_status: statusAgg
  };
}
function reportsEquipmentDemandSummary_(days) {
  var span = Math.max(1, Number(days || 30));
  var nowMs = Date.now();
  var spanMs = span * 86400000;
  var rows = reservationsList({}, { role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, id: 'SYSTEM' }) || [];
  var byItem = {};
  var byCategory = {};
  rows.forEach(function(r) {
    var cd = _reportsSafeDate_(r.created_at || r.start_dt || r.handover_date);
    if (!cd || cd.getTime() < nowMs - spanMs) return;
    _reportsInc_(byItem, r.item_name || r.equipment_name || r.eqName || r.eqId || 'Unknown', 1);
    _reportsInc_(byCategory, r.category || r.equipment_category || r.eqType || 'Unknown', 1);
  });
  return {
    top_items: Object.keys(byItem).map(function(k) { return { name: k, count: byItem[k] }; }).sort(function(a, b) { return b.count - a.count; }).slice(0, 20),
    by_category: Object.keys(byCategory).map(function(k) { return { category: k, count: byCategory[k] }; }).sort(function(a, b) { return b.count - a.count; })
  };
}
function dashboardStats(user) {
  const inv = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)).filter(i => i.status !== 'deleted'); const rooms = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.ROOMS)).filter(r => r.status !== 'deleted'); const res = reservationsList({}, { role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, id: 'SYSTEM' }); const asgn = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS)); const users = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.USERS)).filter(u => u.status !== 'deleted'); const today = new Date().toISOString().split('T')[0];
  const stats = { inventory: { total: inv.length, available: inv.filter(i => i.status === STATUS.AVAILABLE).length, in_use: inv.filter(i => i.status === STATUS.IN_USE).length, maintenance: inv.filter(i => i.status === STATUS.MAINTENANCE).length, overdue: inv.filter(i => i.status === STATUS.OVERDUE).length }, rooms: { total: rooms.length, available: rooms.filter(r => r.status === STATUS.AVAILABLE).length }, reservations: { total: res.length, pending: res.filter(r => r.status === STATUS.PENDING).length, today: res.filter(r => String(r.start_dt).startsWith(today)).length }, assignments: { total: asgn.length, pending: asgn.filter(a => a.status === STATUS.PENDING).length, overdue: asgn.filter(a => [STATUS.PENDING, STATUS.APPROVED].includes(a.status) && a.deadline && a.deadline < today).length, completed: asgn.filter(a => a.status === STATUS.COMPLETED).length }, users: { total: users.length, students: users.filter(u => u.role === ROLES.STUDENT).length } };
  if (user.role === ROLES.STUDENT || user.role === ROLES.INSTRUCTOR) { return { myReservations: { total: res.filter(r => r.user_id === user.id).length, pending: res.filter(r => r.user_id === user.id && r.status === STATUS.PENDING).length, approved: res.filter(r => r.user_id === user.id && r.status === STATUS.APPROVED).length }, myAssignments: { total: asgn.filter(a => a.student_id === user.id || a.instructor_id === user.id).length, pending: asgn.filter(a => (a.student_id === user.id || a.instructor_id === user.id) && a.status === STATUS.PENDING).length, completed: asgn.filter(a => (a.student_id === user.id || a.instructor_id === user.id) && a.status === STATUS.COMPLETED).length } }; }
  return stats;
}

// ── ADMIN / CONFIG ──────────────────────────────────────────
function adminGetConfigValue(key) { try { const row = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.CONFIG)).find(r => r.key === key); return row ? row.value : null; } catch(e) { return null; } }
function adminGetConfig() { const cfg={}; toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.CONFIG)).forEach(r=>cfg[r.key]=r.value); return cfg; }

/**
 * Basit denetim günlüğü yardımcısı.
 * Eski kodda sıkça audit(...) çağrıldığı için burada tanımlanır.
 * Hata durumunda sessizce düşer; iş mantığını bozmaz.
 */
function audit(action, userId, targetId, oldValue, newValue, note) {
  try {
    var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG);
    var id = genId('AUD');
    var oldJson = oldValue != null ? JSON.stringify(oldValue) : '';
    var newJson = newValue != null ? JSON.stringify(newValue) : '';
    sh.appendRow([id, String(action || ''), String(userId || ''), String(targetId || ''), oldJson, newJson, now(), String(note || '')]);
  } catch (e) {
    // Logging should never break main flow
  }
}

function adminSetConfig(payload,actor) { const sheet=getSheet(SHEETS.CONFIG); const list=toObjs(sheet); Object.entries(payload).forEach(([k,v])=>{ const idx=list.findIndex(r=>r.key===k); if(idx===-1) sheet.appendRow([k,v]); else sheet.getRange(idx+2,2).setValue(v); }); audit('admin.setConfig',actor.id,'CONFIG',null,payload); return {saved:true}; }
function adminGetAuditLog(payload) { let list=toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG)); if(payload.user_id) list=list.filter(l=>l.user_id===payload.user_id); if(payload.action) list=list.filter(l=>l.action.startsWith(payload.action)); if(payload.limit) list=list.slice(-payload.limit); return list.reverse(); }

// ── İLK KURULUM ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function adminInitSheets() {
  const ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
  const defs = { [SHEETS.USERS]: UH, [SHEETS.INVENTORY]: IH, [SHEETS.ROOMS]: RH, [SHEETS.RESERVATIONS]: RESH, [SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS]: AH, [SHEETS.NOTIFICATIONS]:NH, [SHEETS.AUDIT_LOG]: ['id','action','user_id','target_id','old_value','new_value','timestamp','note'], [SHEETS.CONFIG]: ['key','value'], [SHEETS.TICKETS]: TKTH, [SHEETS.BIZE_CONTACT]: BIZEH };
  Object.entries(defs).forEach(([name, headers]) => { let s = ss.getSheetByName(name); if (!s) s = ss.insertSheet(name); if (s.getLastRow() === 0) s.appendRow(headers); });
  const cfgSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.CONFIG); const cfgRows = cfgSheet.getLastRow();
  if (cfgRows <= 1) { [ ['app_name', CONFIG.APP_NAME], ['reminder_days', '1'], ['max_reservation_days', '2'], ['studio_max_days', '1'], ['depot_open_hour', '9'], ['depot_close_hour', '16'], ['depot_last_checkin', '15'], ['depot_last_checkin_minute', '30'], ['depot_last_checkout', '16'], ['depot_slot_max_bookings', '4'], ['pickup_no_show_blocked_grace_minutes', '30'], ['lunch_start', '12'], ['lunch_end', '13'], ['allow_self_register', 'false'] ].forEach(row => cfgSheet.appendRow(row)); }
  const userSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
  if (userSheet.getLastRow() <= 1) { const adminEmail = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('DEFAULT_ADMIN_EMAIL') || 'admin@university.edu'; addRow(userSheet, { id: genId('USR'), name: 'System Admin', email: adminEmail, role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, department: 'IT', ms_oid: '', status: STATUS.ACTIVE, created_at: now(), updated_at: now() }, UH); }
  _initBansSheet(ss); let stRes = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES); if (!stRes) stRes = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES); if (stRes.getLastRow() === 0) stRes.appendRow(SRSH);
  var eqN = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.EQ_NOTIFY); if (!eqN) eqN = ss.insertSheet(SHEETS.EQ_NOTIFY); if (eqN.getLastRow() === 0) eqN.appendRow(EQ_NOTIFY_H);
  return { initialized: true, sheets: [...Object.keys(defs), SHEETS.BANS, SHEETS.STUDIO_RES, SHEETS.EQ_NOTIFY] };
}

// ── GECİKME & BAN SİSTEMİ ──────────────────────────
const BAN_LEVELS = { YELLOW: 'yellow_warning', DAY7: '7_day_ban', DAY15: '15_day_ban', SEMESTER: 'semester_ban', PERMANENT: 'permanent_ban' };
function getSemesterEndDate() { const fromConfig = adminGetConfigValue('semester_end_date'); if (fromConfig) return new Date(fromConfig).toISOString(); const m = new Date().getMonth() + 1; const y = new Date().getFullYear(); return m <= 6 ? new Date(y, 5, 30, 23, 59).toISOString() : new Date(y + 1, 0, 31, 23, 59).toISOString(); }
function countHardDelays(userId) { return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(b => String(b.user_id) === String(userId) && b.ban_level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY15).length; }
function countNoShowPickupViolations_(userId) {
  var needle = 'No-show pickup';
  return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(function(b) {
    return String(b.user_id) === String(userId) && String(b.reason || '').indexOf(needle) !== -1;
  }).length;
}
function countNoShowStudioViolations_(userId) {
  var needle = 'No-show studio';
  return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(function(b) {
    return String(b.user_id) === String(userId) && String(b.reason || '').indexOf(needle) !== -1;
  }).length;
}
function applyNoShowPickupPenalty_(userId, userName, reservationId, itemListText, actorId) {
  var uid = String(userId || '').trim();
  if (!uid) return null;
  var prior = countNoShowPickupViolations_(uid);
  var banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW;
  var isActualBan = false;
  var expiresAt = '';
  var reason = 'No-show pickup: warning (first incident).';
  if (prior === 1) {
    var exp7 = new Date();
    exp7.setDate(exp7.getDate() + 7);
    banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.DAY7;
    isActualBan = true;
    expiresAt = exp7.toISOString();
    reason = 'No-show pickup: 7-day suspension (second incident).';
  } else if (prior >= 2) {
    var exp15 = new Date();
    exp15.setDate(exp15.getDate() + 15);
    banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.DAY15;
    isActualBan = true;
    expiresAt = exp15.toISOString();
    reason = 'No-show pickup: 15-day suspension (third+ incident).';
  }
  var ban = {
    id: genId('BAN'),
    user_id: uid,
    user_name: String(userName || ''),
    ban_level: banLevel,
    reason: reason,
    banned_by: String(actorId || 'SYSTEM'),
    banned_at: now(),
    expires_at: expiresAt,
    active: isActualBan,
    notes: 'Reservation: ' + String(reservationId || '') + (itemListText ? (' | Items: ' + itemListText) : '')
  };
  addRow(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS), ban, BAH);
  sendNotif(uid, 'ban.' + banLevel, reason, ban.id);
  notifyAdmins('ban.' + banLevel, reason + ' User: ' + uid, ban.id);
  audit('ban.applyNoShowPickup', String(actorId || 'SYSTEM'), uid, null, ban);
  return { level: banLevel, is_ban: isActualBan, reason: reason, expires_at: expiresAt, prior_count: prior };
}
function applyNoShowStudioPenalty_(userId, userName, reservationId, studioName, actorId) {
  var uid = String(userId || '').trim();
  if (!uid) return null;
  var prior = countNoShowStudioViolations_(uid);
  var banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW;
  var isActualBan = false;
  var expiresAt = '';
  var reason = 'No-show studio: warning (first incident).';
  if (prior === 1) {
    var exp7 = new Date();
    exp7.setDate(exp7.getDate() + 7);
    banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.DAY7;
    isActualBan = true;
    expiresAt = exp7.toISOString();
    reason = 'No-show studio: 7-day suspension (second incident).';
  } else if (prior >= 2) {
    var exp15 = new Date();
    exp15.setDate(exp15.getDate() + 15);
    banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.DAY15;
    isActualBan = true;
    expiresAt = exp15.toISOString();
    reason = 'No-show studio: 15-day suspension (third+ incident).';
  }
  var ban = {
    id: genId('BAN'),
    user_id: uid,
    user_name: String(userName || ''),
    ban_level: banLevel,
    reason: reason,
    banned_by: String(actorId || 'SYSTEM'),
    banned_at: now(),
    expires_at: expiresAt,
    active: isActualBan,
    notes: 'Studio reservation: ' + String(reservationId || '') + (studioName ? (' | Studio: ' + studioName) : '')
  };
  addRow(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS), ban, BAH);
  sendNotif(uid, 'ban.' + banLevel, reason, ban.id);
  notifyAdmins('ban.' + banLevel, reason + ' User: ' + uid, ban.id);
  audit('ban.applyNoShowStudio', String(actorId || 'SYSTEM'), uid, null, ban);
  return { level: banLevel, is_ban: isActualBan, reason: reason, expires_at: expiresAt, prior_count: prior };
}
/** Prior "major late, no pickup queue" yellows only (not minor 1-30 min late). */
function countMajorLateSoftYellowWarnings_(userId) {
  var needle = 'major, no pickup queue';
  return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(function(b) {
    return String(b.user_id) === String(userId) && b.ban_level === BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW && String(b.reason || '').indexOf(needle) !== -1;
  }).length;
}
/** True if this equipment has a blocking reservation whose Handover_Date falls in (returnDt, returnDt + windowMin]. */
function equipmentHasPickupWithinMinutesAfterReturn_(equipmentId, returnDt, windowMin) {
  if (!equipmentId || !returnDt) return false;
  var eq = String(equipmentId).trim();
  var t0 = returnDt instanceof Date ? returnDt.getTime() : new Date(returnDt).getTime();
  if (isNaN(t0)) return false;
  var t1 = t0 + windowMin * 60000;
  var raw = _equipmentReservationRowsSource();
  for (var i = 0; i < raw.length; i++) {
    var r = raw[i];
    if (String(r.equipment_id || r['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim() !== eq) continue;
    if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(r.status || r['Onay Durumu'])) continue;
    var ho = new Date(r.handover_date || r['Handover_Date']);
    if (isNaN(ho.getTime())) continue;
    var ht = ho.getTime();
    if (ht > t0 && ht <= t1) return true;
  }
  return false;
}
/** Next students queued for pickup in the window: tell them to see the desk and that they are not a no-show for this delay. */
function notifyQueuedPickupUsersEquipmentLate_(equipmentId, returnDt, windowMin, lateReturnUserId, itemName) {
  var eq = String(equipmentId || '').trim();
  var t0 = returnDt instanceof Date ? returnDt.getTime() : new Date(returnDt).getTime();
  if (!eq || isNaN(t0)) return;
  var t1 = t0 + windowMin * 60000;
  var ex = String(lateReturnUserId || '').trim();
  var raw = _equipmentReservationRowsSource();
  var seen = {};
  var label = String(itemName || 'equipment').trim();
  for (var i = 0; i < raw.length; i++) {
    var r = raw[i];
    if (String(r.equipment_id || r['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim() !== eq) continue;
    if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(r.status || r['Onay Durumu'])) continue;
    var ho = new Date(r.handover_date || r['Handover_Date']);
    if (isNaN(ho.getTime())) continue;
    var ht = ho.getTime();
    if (ht <= t0 || ht > t1) continue;
    var uid = String(r.student_id || r['Student_ID'] || '').trim();
    if (!uid || uid === ex) continue;
    if (seen[uid]) continue;
    seen[uid] = true;
    var ref = _reservationRowGroupId_(r);
    var msg = 'Equipment pickup may be delayed — the previous user returned late (' + label + '). Please contact the equipment desk; you are not penalized as a no-show for this. ' +
      'TR: Teslim alma gecikebilir (önceki kullanıcı geç iade). Ekipman masasına başvurun; bu durumda no-show sayılmazsınız.';
    sendNotif(uid, 'reservation.pickup_delayed', msg, ref);
  }
}
const DELAY_PICKUP_QUEUE_WINDOW_MIN = 32;
/** "Minor late" upper bound (minutes after due); beyond this = major late. */
const DELAY_MINOR_LATE_MAX_MIN = 30;
/** Major late, no one queued behind you: allow this many prior yellows of that type, then 15-day (value 1 → second major-late = ban). */
const DELAY_SOFT_MAJOR_LATE_YELLOW_CAP = 1;
/**
 * Simple late policy (no separate EOD rule — only minutes after booked due time):
 * - On time: no penalty.
 * - 1–30 min late: yellow warning only.
 * - >30 min late + another pickup for same item within 32 min after your return: 15-day ban (or semester if repeat), notify queued students.
 * - >30 min late + no such pickup: yellow once, then 15-day on next such return.
 * - Two prior 15-day late bans → semester suspension (countHardDelays).
 */
function restrictionsApplyDelay(payload, actor) {
  if (!payload.user_id) throw new Error('user_id is required.'); if (!payload.due_dt) throw new Error('due_dt is required.'); if (!payload.condition) throw new Error('condition is required.');
  const returnDt = payload.return_dt ? new Date(payload.return_dt) : new Date(); const dueDt = new Date(payload.due_dt); const diffMin = (returnDt - dueDt) / 60000;
  const majorLate = diffMin > DELAY_MINOR_LATE_MAX_MIN;
  const queuedPickupSoon = payload.item_id && equipmentHasPickupWithinMinutesAfterReturn_(payload.item_id, returnDt, DELAY_PICKUP_QUEUE_WINDOW_MIN);
  const priorMajorSoftYellows = countMajorLateSoftYellowWarnings_(payload.user_id);
  let banLevel = null; let banReason = ''; let expiresAt = ''; let isActualBan = false;
  function applyHardLate_() {
    const prevHardDelays = countHardDelays(payload.user_id);
    if (prevHardDelays >= 1) { banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.SEMESTER; banReason = 'Repeated violation.'; expiresAt = getSemesterEndDate(); isActualBan = true; }
    else { const exp = new Date(); exp.setDate(exp.getDate() + 15); banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.DAY15; banReason = 'Late return.'; expiresAt = exp.toISOString(); isActualBan = true; }
  }
  if (payload.condition === 'damaged' || payload.condition === 'missing_parts') { banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.PERMANENT; banReason = 'Equipment damaged: ' + (payload.item_name || payload.item_id); isActualBan = true; }
  else if (majorLate) {
    if (queuedPickupSoon) {
      notifyQueuedPickupUsersEquipmentLate_(payload.item_id, returnDt, DELAY_PICKUP_QUEUE_WINDOW_MIN, payload.user_id, payload.item_name || payload.item_id);
      applyHardLate_();
    } else if (priorMajorSoftYellows >= DELAY_SOFT_MAJOR_LATE_YELLOW_CAP) applyHardLate_();
    else { banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW; banReason = 'Yellow Warning: Late (major, no pickup queue).'; isActualBan = false; }
  }
  else if (diffMin > 0) { banLevel = BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW; banReason = 'Yellow Warning: Late.'; isActualBan = false; }
  if (!banLevel) return { action: 'clean_return', message: 'Clean.' };
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.BANS); const ban = { id: genId('BAN'), user_id: String(payload.user_id), user_name: payload.user_name || '', ban_level: banLevel, reason: banReason, banned_by: actor.id, banned_at: now(), expires_at: expiresAt, active: isActualBan, notes: payload.notes || ('Ekipman: ' + (payload.item_name||payload.item_id)) };
  addRow(sheet, ban, BAH); sendNotif(payload.user_id, 'ban.' + banLevel, banReason, ban.id); notifyAdmins('ban.' + banLevel, banReason, ban.id); audit('ban.applyDelay', actor.id, payload.user_id, null, ban);
  return { action: banLevel, is_ban: isActualBan, ban_id: ban.id, reason: banReason, expires_at: expiresAt };
}
function restrictionsGetUserHistory(userId) { const bans = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS)).filter(b => String(b.user_id) === String(userId)).sort((a, b) => new Date(b.banned_at) - new Date(a.banned_at)); return { user_id: userId, total: bans.length, yellow_count: bans.filter(b => b.ban_level === BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW).length, hard_count: bans.filter(b => b.ban_level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY15).length, active_ban: bans.find(b => b.active === true) || null, history: bans }; }

// ── STÜDYO REZERVASYON ─────────────────────────────
// Tablo başlıkları: A–Q kullanıcıya dönük Türkçe; R–Z teknik alanlar (sheet’te sütun ekleyin).
const SRSH = [
  'Seç',
  'İşlem Tarihi',
  'Stüdyo Adı',
  'Talep Türü',
  'Kimlik/Sicil No',
  'Ad Soyad',
  'Giriş Tarihi',
  'Giriş Saati',
  'Çıkış Tarihi',
  'Çıkış Saati',
  'Tekrar Durumu',
  'Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi',
  'Proje / Açıklama',
  'PDF Document By Student',
  'Stüdyo Kullanım Formu',
  'Stüdyo Durumu',
  'İade Teslim Notu',
  'studio_id',
  'key_id',
  'status',
  'approved_by',
  'approved_at',
  'rejected_reason',
  'is_weekend',
  'notes',
  'updated_at'
];

/** ISO / sheet tarih+saat → yyyy-MM-dd & HH:mm (GMT+3 gösterim) */
function studioSplitIsoToDateTime_(iso) {
  if (iso === '' || iso == null) return { d: '', t: '' };
  var x = new Date(iso);
  if (isNaN(x.getTime())) return { d: String(iso).split('T')[0] || '', t: '' };
  return {
    d: Utilities.formatDate(x, 'GMT+3', 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
    t: Utilities.formatDate(x, 'GMT+3', 'HH:mm')
  };
}

/** Giriş/çıkış hücrelerinden ISO üret (yyyy-MM-dd veya dd.MM.yyyy + HH:mm) */
function studioCombineSheetDateTime_(dateStr, timeStr) {
  // Date hücresi zaten datetime ise saati koru (00:00'a düşmesin).
  if (Object.prototype.toString.call(dateStr) === '[object Date]' && !isNaN(dateStr.getTime())) {
    var base = new Date(dateStr.getTime());
    var tRawObj = '';
    if (Object.prototype.toString.call(timeStr) === '[object Date]' && !isNaN(timeStr.getTime())) {
      tRawObj = Utilities.formatDate(timeStr, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'HH:mm');
    } else {
      tRawObj = String(timeStr || '').trim();
    }
    if (!tRawObj) return base.toISOString();
    var mObj = tRawObj.match(/^(\d{1,2}):(\d{2})/);
    if (mObj) {
      base.setHours(parseInt(mObj[1], 10), parseInt(mObj[2], 10), 0, 0);
      return base.toISOString();
    }
    return base.toISOString();
  }
  var d = String(dateStr || '').trim();
  var t = '';
  if (Object.prototype.toString.call(timeStr) === '[object Date]' && !isNaN(timeStr.getTime())) {
    t = Utilities.formatDate(timeStr, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'HH:mm');
  } else {
    t = String(timeStr || '').trim();
  }
  if (!d) return '';
  // Tek alanda tarih+saat string geldiyse direkt parse et.
  var dLoose = new Date(d);
  if (!isNaN(dLoose.getTime()) && !t) return dLoose.toISOString();
  if (!t) t = '00:00';
  if (d.indexOf('T') >= 0) {
    var dt = new Date(d);
    return isNaN(dt.getTime()) ? d : dt.toISOString();
  }
  var ymd = d;
  var m = d.match(/^(\d{1,2})[./](\d{1,2})[./](\d{4})$/);
  if (m) {
    var dd = m[1].length === 1 ? '0' + m[1] : m[1];
    var mo = m[2].length === 1 ? '0' + m[2] : m[2];
    ymd = m[3] + '-' + mo + '-' + dd;
  }
  var hm = t.length === 5 ? t + ':00' : t;
  var cand = ymd + 'T' + hm;
  var x = new Date(cand);
  return isNaN(x.getTime()) ? cand : x.toISOString();
}

/** Hücrede tek parça tarih-saat veya ISO */
function studioIsoFromLoose_(v) {
  var s = String(v || '').trim();
  if (!s) return '';
  var d = new Date(s);
  if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) return d.toISOString();
  var parts = s.split(/\s+/);
  if (parts.length >= 2) return studioCombineSheetDateTime_(parts[0], parts[1]);
  return '';
}

/**
 * Türkçe başlık satırı varken veri eski SRSH İngilizce sütun sırasıyla (A=id, B=studio_id, …) yazılmışsa.
 */
function canonicalFromStudioSheetRowLegacyUnderTurkishHeaders_(raw) {
  var id = String(raw['Seç'] || '').trim();
  if (!id) return null;
  var studio_id = String(raw['İşlem Tarihi'] || '').trim();
  var studio_name = String(raw['Stüdyo Adı'] || '').trim();
  var user_id = String(raw['Talep Türü'] || '').trim();
  var user_name = String(raw['Kimlik/Sicil No'] || '').trim();
  var start_dt = studioIsoFromLoose_(raw['Ad Soyad']) || studioCombineSheetDateTime_(raw['Giriş Tarihi'], raw['Giriş Saati']);
  var end_dt = studioIsoFromLoose_(raw['Giriş Tarihi']) || studioCombineSheetDateTime_(raw['Çıkış Tarihi'], raw['Çıkış Saati']);
  var purpose = String(raw['Giriş Saati'] || '').trim();
  var pdf_url = String(raw['Çıkış Tarihi'] || '').trim();
  var key_id = String(raw['Çıkış Saati'] || '').trim();
  var key_pickup_dt = '';
  var kRaw = String(raw['Tekrar Durumu'] || '').trim();
  if (kRaw) {
    var lowK = kRaw.toLowerCase();
    if (lowK !== 'pending' && lowK !== 'approved') {
      var kpd = new Date(kRaw);
      if (!isNaN(kpd.getTime())) key_pickup_dt = kpd.toISOString();
    }
  }
  var status = String(raw['Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi'] || raw.status || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!status || status === 'false') status = STATUS.PENDING;
  status = normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(status);
  var iw = raw['is_weekend'];
  if (iw === '' || iw == null) iw = raw.is_weekend;
  var isWeekendBool = iw === true || String(iw).toLowerCase() === 'true';
  var created_at = '';
  var cTry = String(raw.created_at || '').trim();
  if (cTry) {
    var cx = new Date(cTry);
    if (!isNaN(cx.getTime())) created_at = cx.toISOString();
  }
  if (!created_at) {
    var uTry = String(raw.updated_at || '').trim();
    if (uTry) {
      var ux = new Date(uTry);
      if (!isNaN(ux.getTime())) created_at = ux.toISOString();
    }
  }
  if (!created_at && start_dt) {
    var sx = new Date(start_dt);
    if (!isNaN(sx.getTime())) created_at = sx.toISOString();
  }
  return {
    id: id,
    studio_id: studio_id,
    studio_name: studio_name,
    user_id: user_id,
    user_name: user_name,
    start_dt: start_dt,
    end_dt: end_dt,
    purpose: purpose,
    pdf_url: pdf_url,
    key_id: key_id,
    key_pickup_dt: key_pickup_dt,
    status: status,
    approved_by: String(raw.approved_by != null ? raw.approved_by : '').trim(),
