    approved_at: String(raw.approved_at != null ? raw.approved_at : '').trim(),
    rejected_reason: String(raw.rejected_reason != null ? raw.rejected_reason : '').trim(),
    is_weekend: isWeekendBool,
    notes: String(raw.notes != null ? raw.notes : '').trim(),
    created_at: created_at || now(),
    updated_at: String(raw.updated_at != null ? raw.updated_at : '').trim(),
    request_type: String(raw.request_type != null ? raw.request_type : '').trim(),
    studio_usage_form_url: String(raw.studio_usage_form_url != null ? raw.studio_usage_form_url : '').trim(),
    studio_handover_note: String(raw['Stüdyo Durumu'] != null ? raw['Stüdyo Durumu'] : raw.studio_handover_note || '').trim(),
    return_handover_note: String(raw['İade Teslim Notu'] != null ? raw['İade Teslim Notu'] : raw.return_handover_note || '').trim()
  };
}

/**
 * Sheet satırı (toObjs) → uygulama içi canonical nesne (API / Supabase aynası aynı alan adları).
 */
function canonicalFromStudioSheetRow_(raw) {
  if (!raw) return null;
  var hasTurk = raw['Stüdyo Adı'] !== undefined || (raw['Seç'] !== undefined && raw['Seç'] !== '');
  var legacyEnglish = raw.studio_name !== undefined && raw.user_name !== undefined && !hasTurk;
  if (legacyEnglish) return raw;

  var id = String(raw['Seç'] != null && String(raw['Seç']).trim() !== '' ? raw['Seç'] : raw.id || '').trim();
  if (!id) return null;

  var techSid = String(raw.studio_id != null ? raw.studio_id : '').trim();
  var colB = String(raw['İşlem Tarihi'] || '').trim();
  if (!techSid && /^(GREEN|RED|PODCAST|DUBBING|BLUE)$/i.test(colB)) {
    return canonicalFromStudioSheetRowLegacyUnderTurkishHeaders_(raw);
  }

  var start_dt = studioCombineSheetDateTime_(raw['Giriş Tarihi'], raw['Giriş Saati']);
  var end_dt = studioCombineSheetDateTime_(raw['Çıkış Tarihi'], raw['Çıkış Saati']);
  var key_pickup_dt = '';
  var lTekrar = String(raw['Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi'] || '').trim();
  if (lTekrar) {
    var lowL = lTekrar.toLowerCase();
    if (
      lowL !== 'pending' && lowL !== 'approved' && lowL !== 'rejected' && lowL !== 'cancelled' &&
      lowL !== STATUS.KEY_OUT && lowL !== 'completed' && lowL !== STUDIO_STATUS_CHECKED_OUT && lowL !== STUDIO_STATUS_RETURNED
    ) {
      var kpd = new Date(lTekrar);
      if (!isNaN(kpd.getTime())) key_pickup_dt = kpd.toISOString();
    }
  }

  var status = String(raw.status != null && String(raw.status).trim() !== '' ? raw.status : '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!status) {
    var wrongL = String(raw['Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi'] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (
      wrongL === 'pending' || wrongL === 'approved' || wrongL === 'rejected' || wrongL === 'cancelled' ||
      wrongL === STATUS.KEY_OUT || wrongL === 'completed' || wrongL === STUDIO_STATUS_CHECKED_OUT || wrongL === STUDIO_STATUS_RETURNED
    ) {
      status = normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(wrongL);
    } else {
      status = STATUS.PENDING;
    }
  }
  status = normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(status);

  var iw = raw['is_weekend'];
  if (iw === '' || iw == null) iw = raw.is_weekend;
  var isWeekendBool = iw === true || String(iw).toLowerCase() === 'true';

  return {
    id: id,
    studio_id: String(raw.studio_id != null ? raw.studio_id : '').trim(),
    studio_name: String(raw['Stüdyo Adı'] != null ? raw['Stüdyo Adı'] : raw.studio_name || '').trim(),
    user_id: String(raw['Kimlik/Sicil No'] != null ? raw['Kimlik/Sicil No'] : raw.user_id || '').trim(),
    user_name: String(raw['Ad Soyad'] != null ? raw['Ad Soyad'] : raw.user_name || '').trim(),
    start_dt: start_dt || String(raw.start_dt || ''),
    end_dt: end_dt || String(raw.end_dt || ''),
    purpose: String(raw['Proje / Açıklama'] != null ? raw['Proje / Açıklama'] : raw.purpose || '').trim(),
    pdf_url: String(raw['PDF Document By Student'] != null ? raw['PDF Document By Student'] : raw.pdf_url || '').trim(),
    key_id: String(raw.key_id != null ? raw.key_id : '').trim(),
    key_pickup_dt: key_pickup_dt || String(raw.key_pickup_dt || ''),
    status: status,
    approved_by: String(raw.approved_by != null ? raw.approved_by : '').trim(),
    approved_at: String(raw.approved_at != null ? raw.approved_at : '').trim(),
    rejected_reason: String(raw.rejected_reason != null ? raw.rejected_reason : '').trim(),
    is_weekend: isWeekendBool,
    notes: String(raw.notes != null ? raw.notes : '').trim(),
    created_at: (function() {
      var b = String(raw['İşlem Tarihi'] || '').trim();
      if (!b) return String(raw.created_at || '');
      var p = new Date(b);
      if (!isNaN(p.getTime())) return p.toISOString();
      return String(raw.created_at || b);
    })(),
    updated_at: String(raw.updated_at != null ? raw.updated_at : '').trim(),
    request_type: String(raw['Talep Türü'] != null ? raw['Talep Türü'] : raw.request_type || '').trim(),
    studio_usage_form_url: String(raw['Stüdyo Kullanım Formu'] != null ? raw['Stüdyo Kullanım Formu'] : raw.studio_usage_form_url || '').trim(),
    studio_handover_note: String(raw['Stüdyo Durumu'] != null ? raw['Stüdyo Durumu'] : raw.studio_handover_note || '').trim(),
    return_handover_note: String(raw['İade Teslim Notu'] != null ? raw['İade Teslim Notu'] : raw.return_handover_note || '').trim()
  };
}

/** Canonical → SRSH sırasıyla yazılacak düz nesne */
function studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(c) {
  var sp = studioSplitIsoToDateTime_(c.start_dt);
  var ep = studioSplitIsoToDateTime_(c.end_dt);
  var cr = studioSplitIsoToDateTime_(c.created_at);
  var kTekrar = '';
  if (c.is_weekend === true || String(c.is_weekend).toLowerCase() === 'true') {
    kTekrar = c.key_pickup_dt ? 'Hafta sonu · Cuma anahtar teslimi' : 'Hafta sonu';
  } else {
    kTekrar = String(c.notes || '').trim() || '—';
  }
  var lTekrarBitis = '';
  if (c.key_pickup_dt) {
    var kx = new Date(c.key_pickup_dt);
    lTekrarBitis = !isNaN(kx.getTime()) ? Utilities.formatDate(kx, 'GMT+3', 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm') : String(c.key_pickup_dt);
  }
  var o = {};
  o['Seç'] = c.id || '';
  o['İşlem Tarihi'] = (cr.d && cr.t) ? (cr.d + ' ' + cr.t) : String(c.created_at || '');
  o['Stüdyo Adı'] = c.studio_name || '';
  o['Talep Türü'] = c.request_type || '';
  o['Kimlik/Sicil No'] = c.user_id || '';
  o['Ad Soyad'] = c.user_name || '';
  o['Giriş Tarihi'] = sp.d;
  o['Giriş Saati'] = sp.t;
  o['Çıkış Tarihi'] = ep.d;
  o['Çıkış Saati'] = ep.t;
  o['Tekrar Durumu'] = kTekrar;
  o['Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi'] = lTekrarBitis;
  o['Proje / Açıklama'] = c.purpose || '';
  o['PDF Document By Student'] = c.pdf_url || '';
  o['Stüdyo Kullanım Formu'] = c.studio_usage_form_url || '';
  o['Stüdyo Durumu'] = c.studio_handover_note || '';
  o['İade Teslim Notu'] = c.return_handover_note || '';
  o['studio_id'] = c.studio_id || '';
  o['key_id'] = c.key_id || '';
  o['status'] = c.status || '';
  o['approved_by'] = c.approved_by || '';
  o['approved_at'] = c.approved_at || '';
  o['rejected_reason'] = c.rejected_reason || '';
  o['is_weekend'] = c.is_weekend === true || String(c.is_weekend).toLowerCase() === 'true';
  o['notes'] = c.notes || '';
  o['updated_at'] = c.updated_at || '';
  return o;
}

/**
 * Stüdyo sayfası: 1. satırda R–Z başlıkları boşsa toObjs() status/studio_id vb. okuyamaz.
 * Boş başlıklı sütunlarda SRSH sırasına göre alan adı kullanılır.
 */
function studioRowToObj_(headerRow, dataRow) {
  var o = {};
  var h = headerRow || [];
  var r = dataRow || [];
  var len = Math.max(r.length, h.length, SRSH.length);
  for (var i = 0; i < len; i++) {
    var named = (i < h.length) ? String(h[i] || '').trim() : '';
    var key = named || (i < SRSH.length ? SRSH[i] : '');
    if (!key) continue;
    if (i < r.length) o[key] = r[i];
  }
  return o;
}

function toObjsStudioReservations_() {
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var cacheKey = 'studio_reservations_supabase_v1';
    try {
      var cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
      var cached = cache.get(cacheKey);
      if (cached) {
        var parsed = JSON.parse(cached);
        if (Array.isArray(parsed)) return parsed;
      }
    } catch (_eCacheRead) {}
    var pick = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['studio_reservations'], { select: '*', limit: 1000000 });
    var rows = (pick && pick.rows) ? pick.rows : [];
    var outSupa = rows.map(function(r) { return canonicalFromStudioSheetRow_(r); }).filter(function(c) { return c && c.id; });
    try {
      CacheService.getScriptCache().put(cacheKey, JSON.stringify(outSupa), 30);
    } catch (_eCacheWrite) {}
    return outSupa;
  }
  var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  if (!sheet) return [];
  var v = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (v.length < 2) return [];
  var header = v[0];
  var out = [];
  for (var ri = 1; ri < v.length; ri++) {
    var raw = studioRowToObj_(header, v[ri]);
    var c = canonicalFromStudioSheetRow_(raw);
    if (c && c.id) out.push(c);
  }
  return out;
}

function _invalidateStudioReservationsCache_() {
  try {
    CacheService.getScriptCache().remove('studio_reservations_supabase_v1');
  } catch (_eCacheInv) {}
}

/**
 * Sheet = doğruluk kaynağı (source of truth). Supabase = isteğe bağlı ayna.
 * Script Properties: SUPABASE_MIRROR=true | SUPABASE_URL | SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY
 * Ayna hata verirse kullanıcı akışı etkilenmez (yalnızca Logger).
 */
function isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_() {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SUPABASE_MIRROR') || '').toLowerCase() === 'true';
}

function isSupabaseReadEnabled_() {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED') || '').toLowerCase() === 'true';
}

function supabaseBaseAndKey_() {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var base = String(p.getProperty('SUPABASE_URL') || '').replace(/\/$/, '');
  var key = String(p.getProperty('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') || p.getProperty('SUPABASE_ANON_KEY') || '').trim();
  if (!base || !key) return null;
  return { base: base, key: key };
}

function supabaseRequest_(method, path, query, payload) {
  var cfg = supabaseBaseAndKey_();
  if (!cfg) throw new Error('Supabase credentials missing.');
  var q = [];
  var obj = query || {};
  for (var k in obj) {
    if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(obj, k)) continue;
    if (obj[k] === undefined || obj[k] === null || obj[k] === '') continue;
    q.push(encodeURIComponent(k) + '=' + encodeURIComponent(String(obj[k])));
  }
  var url = cfg.base + '/rest/v1/' + String(path || '').replace(/^\//, '') + (q.length ? ('?' + q.join('&')) : '');
  var opt = {
    method: String(method || 'get').toLowerCase(),
    muteHttpExceptions: true,
    headers: {
      apikey: cfg.key,
      Authorization: 'Bearer ' + cfg.key,
      Accept: 'application/json'
    }
  };
  if (payload !== undefined && payload !== null) {
    opt.contentType = 'application/json';
    opt.payload = JSON.stringify(payload);
    // PostgREST upsert (on_conflict=...) expects merge semantics; without Prefer some setups return 4xx.
    if (String(method || 'get').toLowerCase() === 'post') {
      opt.headers['Prefer'] = 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal';
    }
  }
  var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(url, opt, 'supabase.request');
  var code = resp.getResponseCode();
  var body = resp.getContentText() || '';
  if (code >= 400) throw new Error('Supabase HTTP ' + code + ': ' + body);
  if (!body) return [];
  return JSON.parse(body);
}

function supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(tables, query) {
  var t = tables || [];
  var lastErr = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < t.length; i++) {
    try {
      var rows = supabaseRequest_('get', t[i], query || {}, null);
      return { table: t[i], rows: rows || [] };
    } catch (e) {
      lastErr = e;
    }
  }
  if (lastErr) throw lastErr;
  return { table: '', rows: [] };
}

/**
 * Birden fazla aday tabloda ilki HTTP 200 dönüp [] verince yanlış "boş envanter" sonucuna düşmemek için:
 * satırı olan ilk tabloyu seçer; hepsi boşsa son denenen boş cevabı döner.
 */
function supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(tables, query) {
  var t = tables || [];
  var lastErr = null;
  var lastEmpty = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < t.length; i++) {
    try {
      var rows = supabaseRequest_('get', t[i], query || {}, null) || [];
      if (rows.length) return { table: t[i], rows: rows };
      lastEmpty = { table: t[i], rows: [] };
    } catch (e) {
      lastErr = e;
    }
  }
  if (lastEmpty) return lastEmpty;
  if (lastErr) throw lastErr;
  return { table: '', rows: [] };
}

function supaRowPick_(r, keys, def) {
  for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
    var k = keys[i];
    if (r[k] !== undefined && r[k] !== null && String(r[k]) !== '') return r[k];
  }
  return def;
}

function _supaNormalizeIso_(v) {
  if (v === '' || v === null || v === undefined) return null;
  var d = new Date(v);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null;
  return d.toISOString();
}

function _supaResRowStableId_(row) {
  var key = [
    String(row.reservation_group_id || ''),
    String(row.equipment_id || ''),
    String(row.student_id || ''),
    String(row.handover_date || ''),
    String(row.return_date || '')
  ].join('|');
  return 'ER_' + _digestHex_(key).substring(0, 32);
}

function _supaUpsertBatch_(tableName, rows, conflictCol) {
  if (!rows || !rows.length) return { ok: true, count: 0 };
  var q = { on_conflict: String(conflictCol || 'id') };
  supabaseRequest_('post', String(tableName || ''), q, rows);
  return { ok: true, count: rows.length };
}

/** Large batch POST can fail (payload limits / gateway). Split into chunks. */
function _supaUpsertBatchChunked_(tableName, rows, conflictCol, chunkSize) {
  if (!rows || !rows.length) return { ok: true, count: 0 };
  var cs = Math.max(5, Math.min(100, parseInt(chunkSize, 10) || 25));
  var total = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i += cs) {
    var chunk = rows.slice(i, i + cs);
    _supaUpsertBatch_(tableName, chunk, conflictCol);
    total += chunk.length;
  }
  return { ok: true, count: total };
}

function _supaUpsertBatchFirstExisting_(tableCandidates, rows, conflictCol) {
  var t = tableCandidates || [];
  var lastErr = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < t.length; i++) {
    var table = String(t[i] || '').trim();
    if (!table) continue;
    try {
      _supaUpsertBatch_(table, rows, conflictCol);
      return { ok: true, table: table, count: rows ? rows.length : 0 };
    } catch (e) {
      lastErr = e;
    }
  }
  if (lastErr) throw lastErr;
  return { ok: false, table: '', count: 0, error: 'No target table candidate.' };
}

function _supaInventoryRowsForTable_(rows, mode) {
  var src = rows || [];
  var out = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < src.length; i++) {
    var r = src[i] || {};
    if (mode === 'inventory_items') {
      var created = _supaNormalizeIso_(r.created_at || '');
      var updated = _supaNormalizeIso_(r.updated_at || '');
      var isSel = r.is_selected;
      if (typeof isSel === 'string') {
        var s = String(isSel || '').toLowerCase().trim();
        isSel = (s === 'true' || s === '1' || s === 'yes' || s === 'evet');
      } else {
        isSel = !!isSel;
      }
      out.push({
        equipment_id: String(r.equipment_id || r.id || '').trim(),
        equipment_name: String(r.equipment_name || r.name || '').trim(),
        type_desc: String(r.type_desc || r.equipment_type || '').trim(),
        status: String(r.status || 'AVAILABLE').trim(),
        condition_out: String(r.condition_out || '').trim(),
        condition_in: String(r.condition_in || '').trim(),
        location: String(r.location || '').trim(),
        photo: String(r.photo || '').trim(),
        eq_level: String(r.eq_level || '').trim(),
        is_selected: isSel,
        created_at: created,
        updated_at: updated || new Date().toISOString(),
        responsible: String(r.responsible || '').trim(),
        statik_id: String(r.statik_id || '').trim()
      });
    } else if (mode === 'minimal') {
      out.push({
        id: String(r.id || r.equipment_id || '').trim(),
        name: String(r.equipment_name || r.name || '').trim(),
        type_desc: String(r.equipment_type || r.type_desc || '').trim(),
        status: String(r.status || 'AVAILABLE').trim()
      });
    } else if (mode === 'legacy_full') {
      out.push({
        id: String(r.id || r.equipment_id || '').trim(),
        name: String(r.equipment_name || r.name || '').trim(),
        type_desc: String(r.equipment_type || r.type_desc || '').trim(),
        status: String(r.status || 'AVAILABLE').trim(),
        checked_out_at: _supaNormalizeIso_(r.handover_date || r.checked_out_at || ''),
        due_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(r.return_date || r.due_date || ''),
        condition_out: String(r.condition_out || '').trim(),
        condition_in: String(r.condition_in || '').trim(),
        location: String(r.location || '').trim(),
        email: String(r.email || '').trim(),
        photo: String(r.photo || '').trim(),
        eq_level: String(r.eq_level || '').trim(),
        responsible: String(r.responsible || '').trim(),
        statik_id: String(r.statik_id || '').trim(),
        updated_at: _supaNormalizeIso_(r.updated_at || '')
      });
    } else {
      out.push(r);
    }
  }
  return out;
}

function _supaInventoryConflictColForTable_(tableName) {
  return String(tableName || '').trim() === 'inventory_items' ? 'equipment_id' : 'id';
}

function _supaInventoryKeyColForTable_(tableName) {
  return String(tableName || '').trim() === 'inventory_items' ? 'equipment_id' : 'id';
}

function _supaUpsertInventoryRowsSmart_(rows) {
  var tables = _supaInventoryTableCandidates_();
  var resolved = _supaResolveWritableInventoryTable_();
  if (resolved) tables = [resolved];
  var lastErr = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < tables.length; i++) {
    var t = tables[i];
    var conflictCol = _supaInventoryConflictColForTable_(t);
    try {
      var primaryMode = (t === 'inventory_items') ? 'inventory_items' : 'full';
      _supaUpsertBatch_(t, _supaInventoryRowsForTable_(rows, primaryMode), conflictCol);
      return { ok: true, table: t, count: (rows || []).length, mode: primaryMode };
    } catch (e1) {
      lastErr = e1;
      try {
        _supaUpsertBatch_(t, _supaInventoryRowsForTable_(rows, 'legacy_full'), conflictCol);
        return { ok: true, table: t, count: (rows || []).length, mode: 'legacy_full' };
      } catch (eLegacy) {
        lastErr = eLegacy;
      }
      try {
        _supaUpsertBatch_(t, _supaInventoryRowsForTable_(rows, 'minimal'), conflictCol);
        return { ok: true, table: t, count: (rows || []).length, mode: 'minimal' };
      } catch (e2) {
        lastErr = e2;
      }
    }
  }
  if (lastErr) throw lastErr;
  return { ok: false, table: '', count: 0, error: 'No inventory table writable.' };
}

function _supaInventoryTableCandidates_() {
  var seen = {};
  var out = [];
  function pushT_(t) {
    var v = String(t || '').trim();
    if (!v || seen[v]) return;
    seen[v] = true;
    out.push(v);
  }
  try {
    var forced = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SUPABASE_INVENTORY_TABLE') || '').trim();
    if (forced) pushT_(forced);
  } catch (_e) {}
  pushT_('inventory_items');
  pushT_('inventory');
  pushT_('equipment_inventory');
  return out;
}

function _supaResolveWritableInventoryTable_() {
  var tables = _supaInventoryTableCandidates_();
  for (var i = 0; i < tables.length; i++) {
    var t = tables[i];
    try {
      // Table existence/schema cache probe (works even when table is empty).
      var keyCol = _supaInventoryKeyColForTable_(t);
      supabaseRequest_('get', t, { select: keyCol, limit: 1 }, null);
      return t;
    } catch (_eProbe) {}
  }
  return '';
}

/** BookGi şeması: ekipman rezervasyon satırları `equipment_reservation_lines` (PK genelde reservation_group_id + equipment_id). */
function _supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_() {
  return ['equipment_reservation_lines'];
}

function _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_() {
  return 'equipment_reservation_lines';
}

/**
 * `equipment_reservation_lines` şemasında olmayan kolonları göndermek PGRST204 verir.
 * Çekirdek alanlar (varsa) bırakılır; “opsiyonel” alanlar yalnızca property ile açılır.
 *
 * Script Property: SUPABASE_EQ_RES_LINE_EXTRA_COLS
 * Yalnızca tabloda OLMAYAN opsiyonel alanları korur (ör. rejected_reason).
 * equipment_name / purpose / student_name çoğu şemada vardır — artık varsayılan silinmez.
 */
function _supaEqResLineExtraColSet_() {
  var set = {};
  try {
    var s = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SUPABASE_EQ_RES_LINE_EXTRA_COLS') || '');
    s.split(',').forEach(function(p) {
      var k = String(p || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (k) set[k] = true;
    });
  } catch (_e) {}
  return set;
}

function _supaSanitizeEqResLineRowsForSchema_(rows) {
  var raw = rows || [];
  var extras = _supaEqResLineExtraColSet_();
  /** equipment_reservation_lines tipik şemada vardır; EXTRA_COLS=yalnızca gerçekten olmayan kolonlar için (ör. rejected_reason). */
  var optionalKeys = ['rejected_reason'];
  var out = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < raw.length; i++) {
    var o = Object.assign({}, raw[i] || {});
    if (!String(o.equipment_category || '').trim() && String(o.equipment_type || '').trim()) {
      o.equipment_category = String(o.equipment_type || '').trim();
    }
    if (!String(o.approver_email || '').trim() && String(o.approved_by_email || '').trim()) {
      o.approver_email = String(o.approved_by_email || '').trim();
    }
    delete o.equipment_type;
    delete o.approved_by_email;
    for (var j = 0; j < optionalKeys.length; j++) {
      var key = optionalKeys[j];
      if (!extras[key]) delete o[key];
    }
    out.push(o);
  }
  return out;
}

/**
 * `equipment_reservation_lines`: önce `id` ile upsert; yoksa bileşik (reservation_group_id, equipment_id).
 */
function _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(rows) {
  var payload = _supaSanitizeEqResLineRowsForSchema_(rows);
  if (!payload.length) return { ok: true, count: 0, table: _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_() };
  var table = _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_();
  for (var i = 0; i < payload.length; i++) {
    var r = payload[i] || {};
    if (!r.id) r.id = _supaResRowStableId_(r);
  }
  try {
    _supaUpsertBatch_(table, payload, 'id');
    return { ok: true, count: payload.length, table: table };
  } catch (e1) {
    try {
      var slim = [];
      for (var j = 0; j < payload.length; j++) {
        var o = Object.assign({}, payload[j]);
        delete o.id;
        slim.push(o);
      }
      _supaUpsertBatch_(table, slim, 'reservation_group_id,equipment_id');
      return { ok: true, count: payload.length, table: table };
    } catch (e2) {
      throw e1;
    }
  }
}

/**
 * Rezervasyon grubu (Sheet'teki Rezervasyon ID) ile satırları bulur.
 */
function _supaSelectEquipmentRowsByGroupId_(groupId) {
  var gid = String(groupId || '').trim();
  if (!gid) return { table: '', rows: [] };
  var table = _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_();
  try {
    var rows = supabaseRequest_('get', table, {
      select: '*',
      reservation_group_id: 'eq.' + gid
    }, null) || [];
    if (rows.length) return { table: table, rows: rows };
  } catch (_e) {}
  var filterKeys = ['group_id', 'reservation_id', 'res_id'];
  for (var fi = 0; fi < filterKeys.length; fi++) {
    var q = { select: '*' };
    q[filterKeys[fi]] = 'eq.' + gid;
    try {
      var r2 = supabaseRequest_('get', table, q, null) || [];
      if (r2.length) return { table: table, rows: r2 };
    } catch (_e2) {}
  }
  return { table: '', rows: [] };
}

function _supaSelectAllEquipmentReservationLines_() {
  var table = _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_();
  try {
    var rows = supabaseRequest_('get', table, { select: '*', limit: 1000000 }, null) || [];
    return { table: table, rows: rows };
  } catch (e) {
    return { table: table, rows: [], error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _equipmentReservationRowsSource_() {
  if (_supabaseOnlyEquipmentReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var sr = _supaSelectAllEquipmentReservationLines_();
    var rows = (sr && sr.rows) ? sr.rows : [];
    return rows.map(function(r) {
      return {
        reservation_group_id: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['reservation_group_id', 'group_id', 'reservation_id', 'res_id'], '')).trim(),
        equipment_id: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim(),
        equipment_name: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_name', 'item_name', 'name'], '')).trim(),
        equipment_category: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_category', 'equipment_type', 'type_desc', 'category'], '')).trim(),
        student_id: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_id', 'user_id'], '')).trim(),
        student_name: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_name', 'user_name'], '')).trim(),
        handover_date: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '')).trim(),
        return_date: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '')).trim(),
        status: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim(),
        approver_email: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['approver_email', 'approved_by_email'], '')).trim(),
        purpose: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['purpose', 'description'], '')).trim(),
        created_at: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['created_at'], '')).trim(),
        updated_at: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['updated_at'], '')).trim()
      };
    }).filter(function(x) { return !!(x.reservation_group_id && x.equipment_id); });
  }
  return toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS));
}

function _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsPrimary_(rows) {
  return _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(rows);
}

function _supaPatchEquipmentReservationGroupStatus_(groupId, status, approvedByEmail, rejectedReason) {
  var gid = String(groupId || '').trim();
  if (!gid) throw new Error('Missing reservation group id.');
  var rowsRes = _supaSelectEquipmentRowsByGroupId_(gid);
  var rows = (rowsRes && rowsRes.rows) ? rowsRes.rows : [];
  if (!rows.length) return { ok: true, count: 0, table: rowsRes.table || '' };
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    rows[i].status = String(status || rows[i].status || '').trim();
    try {
      var ex = _supaEqResLineExtraColSet_();
      if (ex['approver_email'] || ex['approved_by_email']) {
        rows[i].approver_email = String(approvedByEmail || rows[i].approver_email || rows[i].approved_by_email || '').trim();
      }
      if (rejectedReason !== undefined && ex['rejected_reason']) {
        rows[i].rejected_reason = String(rejectedReason || '').trim();
      }
    } catch (_eEx) {}
    rows[i].id = String(supaRowPick_(rows[i], ['id'], rows[i].id || '')).trim() || _supaResRowStableId_(rows[i]);
  }
  _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(rows);
  return { ok: true, count: rows.length, table: rowsRes.table || _supaEquipmentReservationLinesTable_() };
}

function _buildSupaEquipmentReservationRowsFromSheet_() {
  var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  var vals = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (!vals || vals.length < 2) return [];
  var c = _reservationSheetColIxs_(vals);
  var out = [];
  for (var i = 1; i < vals.length; i++) {
    var r = vals[i];
    var row = {
      reservation_group_id: String(r[c.group] || '').trim(),
      equipment_id: String(r[c.eqId] || '').trim(),
      equipment_name: String(r[c.name] || '').trim(),
      equipment_category: String(r[c.category] || '').trim(),
      student_id: String(r[c.student] || '').trim(),
      student_name: String(r[c.studentName] || '').trim(),
      handover_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(r[c.handover]),
      return_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(r[c.ret]),
      status: String(r[c.status] || '').trim(),
      approver_email: String(r[c.approver] || '').trim(),
      purpose: String(c.purpose >= 0 ? (r[c.purpose] || '') : '').trim()
    };
    if (!row.equipment_id || !row.reservation_group_id) continue;
    row.id = _supaResRowStableId_(row);
    out.push(row);
  }
  return out;
}

/**
 * vals = getDataRange().getValues(); dataRow = 1..vals.length-1 (header = 0).
 * Envanter sayfası başlıkları Türkçe/İngilizce karışık olabilir — sync ile aynı eşleme.
 */
function _supaInventoryHeaderMap_(headerRow) {
  var h = (headerRow || []).map(function(x) { return String(x || '').trim().toLowerCase(); });
  function colIx(keys) {
    for (var i = 0; i < keys.length; i++) {
      var k = keys[i];
      var p = h.findIndex(function(x) { return x === k || x.indexOf(k) >= 0; });
      if (p >= 0) return p;
    }
    return -1;
  }
  return {
    iEq: colIx(['equipment_id', 'ekipman_id', 'id']),
    iName: colIx(['equipment_name', 'name']),
    iType: colIx(['ekipman türü', 'type_desc', 'type', 'category']),
    iStatus: colIx(['status', 'durum']),
    iPhoto: colIx(['photo', 'image']),
    iLoc: colIx(['location', 'konum']),
    iEmail: colIx(['email', 'e-mail', 'eposta']),
    iResponsible: colIx(['responsible', 'sorumlu']),
    iStatik: colIx(['statik_id', 'eq_static_id', 'kayıt_id', 'kayit_id']),
    iHandover: colIx(['handover_date', 'checked_out_at', 'teslim']),
    iReturn: colIx(['return_date', 'due_date', 'iade']),
    iLevel: colIx(['eq_level', 'ekipman seviyesi', 'level']),
    iCondOut: colIx(['condition_out', 'condition out']),
    iCondIn: colIx(['condition_in', 'condition in'])
  };
}

function _supaInventoryPayloadFromRowByMap_(row, m) {
  if (!row || !m) return null;
  var equipmentId = String(m.iEq >= 0 ? row[m.iEq] : '').trim();
  if (!equipmentId) return null;
  return {
    id: equipmentId,
    equipment_id: equipmentId,
    equipment_name: String(m.iName >= 0 ? row[m.iName] : '').trim(),
    equipment_type: String(m.iType >= 0 ? row[m.iType] : '').trim(),
    status: String(m.iStatus >= 0 ? row[m.iStatus] : 'AVAILABLE').trim(),
    photo: String(m.iPhoto >= 0 ? row[m.iPhoto] : '').trim(),
    location: String(m.iLoc >= 0 ? row[m.iLoc] : '').trim(),
    email: String(m.iEmail >= 0 ? row[m.iEmail] : '').trim(),
    responsible: String(m.iResponsible >= 0 ? row[m.iResponsible] : '').trim(),
    statik_id: String(m.iStatik >= 0 ? row[m.iStatik] : '').trim(),
    handover_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(m.iHandover >= 0 ? row[m.iHandover] : ''),
    return_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(m.iReturn >= 0 ? row[m.iReturn] : ''),
    eq_level: String(m.iLevel >= 0 ? row[m.iLevel] : '').trim(),
    condition_out: String(m.iCondOut >= 0 ? row[m.iCondOut] : '').trim(),
    condition_in: String(m.iCondIn >= 0 ? row[m.iCondIn] : '').trim(),
    updated_at: new Date().toISOString()
  };
}

function _supaInventoryPayloadFromValuesIndex_(vals, dataRow) {
  if (!vals || vals.length < 2 || dataRow < 1 || dataRow >= vals.length) return null;
  var m = _supaInventoryHeaderMap_(vals[0] || []);
  return _supaInventoryPayloadFromRowByMap_(vals[dataRow], m);
}

function _buildSupaInventoryRowsFromSheet_() {
  var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
  var vals = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (!vals || vals.length < 2) return [];
  var m = _supaInventoryHeaderMap_(vals[0] || []);
  var out = [];
  for (var r = 1; r < vals.length; r++) {
    var o = _supaInventoryPayloadFromRowByMap_(vals[r], m);
    if (o) out.push(o);
  }
  return out;
}

function _supaInventorySheetIdSetUpper_(invRows) {
  var set = {};
  var rows = invRows || [];
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    var id = String(rows[i].id || rows[i].equipment_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (id) set[id] = true;
  }
  return set;
}

/**
 * Sheet'te artık olmayan equipment_id satırlarını Supabase envanter tablosundan siler.
 * Satırı sheet'ten silince onEdit mirror tetiklenmez; hayalet kayıt UI'da "müsait" görünüp
 * checkEquipmentReservationConflictsBridge (yalnız Sheet) reddeder.
 * Sheet'te hiç geçerli equipment_id yoksa çalışmaz (Supabase'i toplu silme riski).
 */
function _supaInventoryPruneOrphansForTable_(tableName, invRows) {
  var tn = String(tableName || '').trim();
  if (!tn) return { skipped: true, reason: 'no_table', deleted: 0, deleted_ids: [] };
  var sheetSet = _supaInventorySheetIdSetUpper_(invRows);
  if (!Object.keys(sheetSet).length) {
    return { skipped: true, reason: 'sheet_has_no_equipment_ids', deleted: 0, deleted_ids: [] };
  }
  var remote = [];
  try {
    var keyCol = _supaInventoryKeyColForTable_(tn);
    remote = supabaseRequest_('get', tn, { select: keyCol, limit: '100000' }, null) || [];
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('_supaInventoryPruneOrphansForTable_ get: ' + (e.message || e));
    return { skipped: true, reason: 'fetch_failed', error: e.message || String(e), deleted: 0, deleted_ids: [] };
  }
  var deletedIds = [];
  var keyCol2 = _supaInventoryKeyColForTable_(tn);
  for (var r = 0; r < remote.length; r++) {
    var rid = String(remote[r][keyCol2] || remote[r].id || remote[r].equipment_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (!rid || sheetSet[rid]) continue;
    try {
      var q = {};
      q[keyCol2] = 'eq.' + rid;
      supabaseRequest_('delete', tn, q, null);
      deletedIds.push(rid);
    } catch (e2) {
      Logger.log('_supaInventoryPruneOrphansForTable_ delete ' + rid + ': ' + (e2.message || e2));
    }
  }
  return { skipped: false, deleted: deletedIds.length, deleted_ids: deletedIds };
}

function _maybeSupabasePruneInventoryOrphans_(invUpsertResult, invRows) {
  var enabled = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('SUPABASE_INVENTORY_PRUNE_ORPHANS') || '').toLowerCase() === 'true';
  if (!enabled) return null;
  var tbl = invUpsertResult && invUpsertResult.table;
  if (!tbl) return { skipped: true, reason: 'no_table_after_upsert' };
  return _supaInventoryPruneOrphansForTable_(tbl, invRows);
}

/**
 * Apps Script'te bir kez çalıştırın: Sheet = doğruluk kaynağı; Supabase'te sheet'te olmayan ID'leri siler.
 */
function supabasePruneInventoryOrphansNow() {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Supabase is disabled. Set SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED=true or SUPABASE_MIRROR=true.' };
    }
    var invRows = _buildSupaInventoryRowsFromSheet_();
    var pick = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: 'equipment_id,id', limit: '100000' });
    var table = pick.table;
    if (!table) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Could not resolve Supabase inventory table.' };
    }
    var pr = _supaInventoryPruneOrphansForTable_(table, invRows);
    return { ok: true, inventoryTable: table, prune: pr };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

/**
 * Sheet satırı (1-based, başlık = 1) güncellendiğinde Supabase envanter tablosuna tek satır upsert.
 * Sheet düzenini bozmaz; hata olursa yalnızca Logger (rezervasyon mirror ile aynı felsefe).
 */
function trySupabaseMirrorInventorySheetRow_(row1Based) {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) return;
    var row = parseInt(row1Based, 10);
    if (isNaN(row) || row < 2) return;
    var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    if (!sh) return;
    var lastCol = sh.getLastColumn();
    if (!lastCol || lastCol < 1) return;
    var headers = sh.getRange(1, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues();
    var rowVals = sh.getRange(row, 1, 1, lastCol).getValues();
    var vals = [headers[0], rowVals[0]];
    var payload = _supaInventoryPayloadFromValuesIndex_(vals, 1);
    if (!payload) return;
    _supaUpsertInventoryRowsSmart_([payload]);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('trySupabaseMirrorInventorySheetRow_: ' + (e.message || e));
  }
}

/**
 * Sheet üzerinde art arda gelen editlerde Supabase'i yormamak için kısa aralıklı tam sync.
 * Reservations / Studio sheet manuel düzenlemelerinde "satır bazlı" mirror zor olduğundan
 * çekirdek tabloları toplu eşitler.
 */
function _debouncedSupabaseCoreSyncFromSheetEdit_() {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) return;
    var lock = LockService.getScriptLock();
    if (!lock.tryLock(250)) return;
    try {
      var cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
      var key = 'SUPA_CORE_SYNC_DEBOUNCE';
      if (cache.get(key)) return;
      cache.put(key, '1', 20);
      supabaseSyncCoreTablesNow();
    } finally {
      lock.releaseLock();
    }
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('_debouncedSupabaseCoreSyncFromSheetEdit_: ' + (e.message || e));
  }
}

function supabaseSyncCoreTablesNow() {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Supabase is disabled. Set SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED=true or SUPABASE_MIRROR=true.' };
    }
    var invRows = _buildSupaInventoryRowsFromSheet_();
    var resRows = _buildSupaEquipmentReservationRowsFromSheet_();
    var stRows = toObjsStudioReservations_().map(function(r) { return supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(r); }).filter(function(r) { return !!r.id; });

    var inv = _supaUpsertInventoryRowsSmart_(invRows);
    var invPrune = _maybeSupabasePruneInventoryOrphans_(inv, invRows);
    var res = _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(resRows);
    var st = _supaUpsertBatch_('studio_reservations', stRows, 'id');

    return {
      ok: true,
      inventory: inv.count,
      inventoryTable: inv.table || '',
      inventoryPayloadMode: inv.mode || 'full',
      inventoryPruneOrphans: invPrune,
      equipmentReservations: res.count,
      equipmentReservationsTable: res.table || '',
      studioReservations: st.count
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseSyncInventoryNow() {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Supabase is disabled. Set SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED=true or SUPABASE_MIRROR=true.' };
    }
    var invRows = _buildSupaInventoryRowsFromSheet_();
    var inv = _supaUpsertInventoryRowsSmart_(invRows);
    var invPrune = _maybeSupabasePruneInventoryOrphans_(inv, invRows);
    return {
      ok: true,
      inventory: inv.count,
      inventoryTable: inv.table || '',
      inventoryPayloadMode: inv.mode || 'full',
      inventoryPruneOrphans: invPrune
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseReadinessReportNow() {
  try {
    var resSheetVals = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS).getDataRange().getValues();
    var invSheetVals = getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY).getDataRange().getValues();
    var stSheetRows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
    var sheetCounts = {
      equipment_reservations: Math.max(0, (resSheetVals && resSheetVals.length ? resSheetVals.length - 1 : 0)),
      inventory_items: Math.max(0, (invSheetVals && invSheetVals.length ? invSheetVals.length - 1 : 0)),
      studio_reservations: stSheetRows.length || 0
    };
    var supaRes = [];
    try {
      supaRes = supabaseRequest_('get', 'equipment_reservation_lines', { select: 'equipment_id', limit: 1000000 }, null) || [];
    } catch (_eResCt) {
      try {
        supaRes = supabaseRequest_('get', 'equipment_reservation_lines', { select: '*', limit: 1000000 }, null) || [];
      } catch (_eResCt2) {
        supaRes = [];
      }
    }
    var invPick = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: 'equipment_id,id', limit: 1000000 });
    var supaInv = invPick.rows || [];
    var supaSt = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['studio_reservations'], { select: 'id', limit: 1000000 }).rows || [];
    var eqLineCount = supaRes.length;
    var supaCounts = {
      equipment_reservation_lines: eqLineCount,
      equipment_reservations: eqLineCount,
      inventory_items: supaInv.length,
      studio_reservations: supaSt.length
    };
    var mismatch = {
      equipment_reservations: sheetCounts.equipment_reservations - supaCounts.equipment_reservations,
      inventory_items: sheetCounts.inventory_items - supaCounts.inventory_items,
      studio_reservations: sheetCounts.studio_reservations - supaCounts.studio_reservations
    };
    return {
      ok: true,
      supabaseReadEnabled: isSupabaseReadEnabled_(),
      supabaseMirrorEnabled: isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_(),
      supabaseStrictReadEnabled: _supabaseStrictReadEnabled_(),
      sheet: sheetCounts,
      supabase: supaCounts,
      supabaseInventoryTable: invPick.table || '',
      deltaSheetMinusSupabase: mismatch
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseActivatePrimaryReadNow() {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_MIRROR', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ALLOW_EMPTY', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', 'true');
    return { ok: true, message: 'Supabase primary read mode enabled.' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseSetHybridReadNow() {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_MIRROR', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ALLOW_EMPTY', 'false');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', 'false');
    return { ok: true, mode: 'hybrid', message: 'Hybrid mode enabled (Supabase-first + Sheet fallback).' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseEnableReservationsSupabaseOnlyNow() {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    // Inventory: Supabase-first, Sheet fallback (hybrid read)
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_MIRROR', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ALLOW_EMPTY', 'false');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', 'false');
    // Reservations + Studio reservations: write/read directly from Supabase
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ONLY_EQUIPMENT_RESERVATIONS', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ONLY_STUDIO_RESERVATIONS', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_PRIMARY_WRITE', 'true');
    return {
      ok: true,
      mode: 'supabase-only-reservations',
      equipment_reservations: 'supabase-only',
      studio_reservations: 'supabase-only',
      inventory: 'supabase-first-sheet-fallback'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function supabaseMigrationCutoverNow() {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED', 'true');
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_MIRROR', 'true');
    // Cutover sırasında boş Supabase sonucu gizlenmesin; gerekiyorsa fallback'e dönmeyi kolaylaştırır.
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_ALLOW_EMPTY', 'false');

    var sync = supabaseSyncCoreTablesNow();
    if (!sync || sync.ok !== true) {
      p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', 'false');
      return { ok: false, step: 'sync', sync: sync || null, message: 'Sync failed; kept hybrid mode.' };
    }

    var report = supabaseReadinessReportNow();
    if (!report || report.ok !== true) {
      p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', 'false');
      return { ok: false, step: 'readiness', report: report || null, message: 'Readiness failed; kept hybrid mode.' };
    }

    var invReady = Number(report.supabase && report.supabase.inventory_items || 0) > 0;
    var resReady = Number(report.supabase && report.supabase.equipment_reservations || 0) > 0;
    var canStrict = invReady && resReady;
    p.setProperty('SUPABASE_STRICT_READ', canStrict ? 'true' : 'false');

    return {
      ok: true,
      mode: canStrict ? 'strict' : 'hybrid',
      strictEnabled: canStrict,
      sync: sync,
      report: report,
      message: canStrict
        ? 'Supabase strict read enabled after successful sync/readiness.'
        : 'Sync completed but strict not enabled (missing core rows). Hybrid mode kept.'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_(row) {
  try {
    if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() && !isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_()) return;
    if (!row) return;
    var payload = {
      equipment_id: String(row.equipment_id || '').trim(),
      equipment_name: String(row.equipment_name || '').trim(),
      equipment_category: String(row.equipment_category || row.equipment_type || '').trim(),
      student_id: String(row.student_id || '').trim(),
      student_name: String(row.student_name || '').trim(),
      handover_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(row.handover_date),
      return_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(row.return_date),
      status: String(row.status || '').trim(),
      approver_email: String(row.approver_email || row.approved_by_email || '').trim(),
      reservation_group_id: String(row.reservation_group_id || '').trim(),
      purpose: String(row.purpose || '').trim()
    };
    if (!payload.equipment_id || !payload.reservation_group_id) return;
    payload.id = _supaResRowStableId_(payload);
    _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_([payload]);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_: ' + (e.message || e));
  }
}

function trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(groupId) {
  try {
    var gid = String(groupId || '').trim();
    if (!gid) return;
    var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var vals = sh.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (!vals || vals.length < 2) return;
    var c = _reservationSheetColIxs_(vals);
    var rows = [];
    for (var i = 1; i < vals.length; i++) {
      var r = vals[i];
      if (String(r[c.group] || '').trim() !== gid) continue;
      rows.push({
        reservation_group_id: gid,
        equipment_id: String(r[c.eqId] || '').trim(),
        equipment_name: String(r[c.name] || '').trim(),
        equipment_category: String(r[c.category] || '').trim(),
        student_id: String(r[c.student] || '').trim(),
        student_name: String(r[c.studentName] || '').trim(),
        handover_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(r[c.handover]),
        return_date: _supaNormalizeIso_(r[c.ret]),
        status: String(r[c.status] || '').trim(),
        approver_email: String(r[c.approver] || '').trim(),
        purpose: String(c.purpose >= 0 ? (r[c.purpose] || '') : '').trim()
      });
    }
    for (var j = 0; j < rows.length; j++) rows[j].id = _supaResRowStableId_(rows[j]);
    _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsToLines_(rows);
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_: ' + (e.message || e));
  }
}

function supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(v) {
  if (v === '' || v == null) return null;
  var d = new Date(v);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null;
  return d.toISOString();
}

function supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(row) {
  var r = row || {};
  var wk = r.is_weekend;
  var boolWk = wk === true || String(wk).toLowerCase() === 'true';
  return {
    id: r.id ? String(r.id) : null,
    studio_id: r.studio_id != null ? String(r.studio_id) : null,
    studio_name: r.studio_name != null ? String(r.studio_name) : null,
    user_id: r.user_id != null ? String(r.user_id) : null,
    user_name: r.user_name != null ? String(r.user_name) : null,
    start_dt: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.start_dt),
    end_dt: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.end_dt),
    purpose: r.purpose != null ? String(r.purpose) : null,
    pdf_url: r.pdf_url != null ? String(r.pdf_url) : null,
    key_id: r.key_id != null ? String(r.key_id) : null,
    key_pickup_dt: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.key_pickup_dt),
    status: r.status != null ? normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(String(r.status)) : null,
    approved_by: r.approved_by != null ? String(r.approved_by) : null,
    approved_at: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.approved_at),
    rejected_reason: r.rejected_reason != null ? String(r.rejected_reason) : null,
    is_weekend: boolWk,
    notes: r.notes != null ? String(r.notes) : null,
    created_at: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.created_at),
    updated_at: supabaseMirrorStudioIso_(r.updated_at),
    request_type: r.request_type != null ? String(r.request_type) : null,
    studio_usage_form_url: r.studio_usage_form_url != null ? String(r.studio_usage_form_url) : null,
    studio_handover_note: r.studio_handover_note != null ? String(r.studio_handover_note) : null,
    return_handover_note: r.return_handover_note != null ? String(r.return_handover_note) : null
  };
}

function trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(row) {
  if (!isSupabaseStudioMirrorEnabled_() || !row || !row.id) return;
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var base = String(p.getProperty('SUPABASE_URL') || '').replace(/\/$/, '');
    var key = String(p.getProperty('SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY') || '').trim();
    if (!base || !key) return;
    var url = base + '/rest/v1/studio_reservations?on_conflict=id';
    var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(url, {
      method: 'POST',
      headers: {
        apikey: key,
        Authorization: 'Bearer ' + key,
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
        Prefer: 'resolution=merge-duplicates,return=minimal'
      },
      payload: JSON.stringify([supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(row)]),
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }, 'supabase.mirror.studio');
    var code = resp.getResponseCode();
    if (code >= 400) Logger.log('Supabase mirror studio HTTP ' + code + ': ' + resp.getContentText());
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_: ' + (e.message || e));
  }
}

/**
 * Stüdyonun Google Takviminde [start, end) ile çakışan etkinlik var mı?
 * Web uygulaması "Benim adıma çalıştır" ile yayınlandıysa script sahibi takvime erişebilmeli.
 */
function studioCalendarCheckRange_(studioId, startIso, endIso) {
  var start = new Date(startIso);
  var end = new Date(endIso);
  if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime()) || end <= start) {
    return { ok: false, busy: false, error: 'Invalid time range.' };
  }
  // Google Calendar integration disabled: rely on internal reservation checks only.
  return { ok: true, busy: false, skipped: true };
}

/** index.html — anlık uyarı için */
function checkStudioCalendarBridge(studioId, startIso, endIso, testToken) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'Not signed in.' };
    var access = canUserAccessStudio(enrichUserMatrix(user) || user, studioId);
    if (!access.ok) return { error: access.reason };
    var r = studioCalendarCheckRange_(studioId, startIso, endIso);
    if (r.error && !r.skipped) return { error: r.error };
    if (r.busy) return { busy: true, message: r.message || 'The time range you selected is not available for this studio reservation.' };
    return { busy: false, skipped: !!r.skipped };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function _mondayStartForIso_(isoOrDate) {
  var d = isoOrDate instanceof Date ? new Date(isoOrDate.getTime()) : new Date(String(isoOrDate || ''));
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) d = new Date();
  d.setHours(0, 0, 0, 0);
  var day = d.getDay(); // Sun=0..Sat=6
  var diff = (day === 0 ? -6 : (1 - day)); // Monday-first
  d.setDate(d.getDate() + diff);
  return d;
}

function _studioSlotLabel_(mins) {
  var h = Math.floor(mins / 60);
  var m = mins % 60;
  return String(h).padStart(2, '0') + ':' + String(m).padStart(2, '0');
}

function _studioWeeklyGridPayload_(studioId, weekStartIso, actorUser, includeDetails) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  var studio = resolveStudio(sid);
  if (!studio) return { error: 'Invalid studio.' };
  if (actorUser) {
    var access = canUserAccessStudio(enrichUserMatrix(actorUser) || actorUser, sid);
    if (!access.ok) return { error: access.reason };
  }
  var weekStart = _mondayStartForIso_(weekStartIso);
  var weekEnd = new Date(weekStart.getTime() + 7 * 86400000);
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
  var block = studioStatusesBlockingKey_();
  var active = rows.filter(function(r) {
    if (String(r.studio_id || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== sid) return false;
    if (block.indexOf(String(r.status || '').toLowerCase()) === -1) return false;
    var rs = new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
    var re = new Date(r.end_dt).getTime();
    if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) return false;
    return rs < weekEnd.getTime() && re > weekStart.getTime();
  });

  var slots = [];
  for (var mins = 9 * 60; mins < 21 * 60; mins += 60) {
    slots.push(mins);
  }
  slots.push(21 * 60);
  var days = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < 7; i++) {
    var d = new Date(weekStart.getTime() + i * 86400000);
    var dayKind = 'open';
    if (isPublicHoliday(d)) dayKind = 'closed';
    else {
      var wd = d.getDay();
      if (!studio.weekendOk && (wd === 0 || wd === 6)) dayKind = 'closed';
    }
    days.push({
      iso: Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
      dow: d.getDay(),
      day: d.getDate(),
      month: d.getMonth() + 1,
      kind: dayKind
    });
  }

  var cells = {};
  var slotDetails = {};
  var cellBusyStart = {};
  var cellAdminCaption = {};
  days.forEach(function(day) {
    slots.forEach(function(m) {
      var key = day.iso + '|' + m;
      if (day.kind !== 'open') {
        cells[key] = 'closed';
        return;
      }
      if (m === 21 * 60) {
        // Visual boundary marker row (21:00). Not a bookable start slot.
        cells[key] = 'boundary';
        return;
      }
      var sh = Math.floor(m / 60), sm = m % 60;
      var startMs = new Date(day.iso + 'T' + _studioSlotLabel_(m) + ':00').getTime();
      var endMs = startMs + 60 * 60000;
      var busyRows = active.filter(function(r) {
        var rs = new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
        var re = new Date(r.end_dt).getTime();
        return rs < endMs && re > startMs;
      });
      var busy = busyRows.length > 0;
      cells[key] = busy ? 'busy' : 'free';
      var startRows = busyRows.filter(function(r) {
        var rs = new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
        return rs >= startMs && rs < endMs;
      });
      if (busy && startRows.length) {
        cellBusyStart[key] = true;
        if (includeDetails) {
          var capParts = startRows.map(function(r) {
            var p = String(r.purpose || '').trim();
            if (p) return p;
            var u = String(r.user_name || '').trim();
            return u || '—';
          });
          cellAdminCaption[key] = capParts.join(' · ');
        }
      }
      if (includeDetails && busy) {
        slotDetails[key] = busyRows.map(function(r) {
          return {
            id: String(r.id || ''),
            user_name: String(r.user_name || ''),
            purpose: String(r.purpose || ''),
            status: String(r.status || ''),
            start_dt: String(r.start_dt || ''),
            end_dt: String(r.end_dt || '')
          };
        });
      }
    });
  });

  return {
    ok: true,
    studio_id: sid,
    studio_name: studio.name,
    week_start: Utilities.formatDate(weekStart, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'yyyy-MM-dd'),
    days: days,
    slots: slots.map(function(m) { return { mins: m, label: _studioSlotLabel_(m) }; }),
    cells: cells,
    slot_details: includeDetails ? slotDetails : {},
    cell_busy_start: cellBusyStart,
    cell_admin_caption: includeDetails ? cellAdminCaption : {}
  };
}

/**
 * One-time migration: Google Calendar events -> studio_reservations table/sheet.
 * Safe to rerun (idempotent): reservation id is deterministic per event.
 */
function importGoogleCalendarStudioEventsOnce(fromIso, toIso, dryRun) {
  var rows = [];
  try {
    var from = fromIso ? new Date(fromIso) : new Date(Date.now() - 180 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    var to = toIso ? new Date(toIso) : new Date(Date.now() + 365 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000);
    if (isNaN(from.getTime()) || isNaN(to.getTime()) || to <= from) {
      return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid from/to range.' };
    }
    var previewOnly = String(dryRun || '').toLowerCase() === 'true' || dryRun === true;
    rows = [];
    var studios = Object.keys(STUDIO_CALENDAR_EMBEDS || {});
    for (var i = 0; i < studios.length; i++) {
      var sid = studios[i];
      var meta = STUDIO_CALENDAR_EMBEDS[sid] || {};
      var calId = String(meta.calId || '').trim();
      if (!calId) continue;
      var studio = resolveStudio(sid);
      if (!studio) continue;
      var cal = null;
      try { cal = CalendarApp.getCalendarById(calId); } catch (_ec) { cal = null; }
      if (!cal) continue;
      var evs = [];
      try { evs = cal.getEvents(from, to) || []; } catch (_ee) { evs = []; }
      for (var e = 0; e < evs.length; e++) {
        var ev = evs[e];
        var st = ev.getStartTime();
        var en = ev.getEndTime();
        if (!st || !en || isNaN(st.getTime()) || isNaN(en.getTime()) || en <= st) continue;
        if (ev.isAllDayEvent && ev.isAllDayEvent()) continue;
        // Guard against malformed calendar entries (observed as 1970 timestamps).
        if (st.getFullYear() < 2000 || en.getFullYear() < 2000) continue;
        // Keep imported slots aligned with native studio operating window.
        // Instead of dropping out-of-window events entirely, clip to [09:00, 21:00]
        // if there is any overlap.
        var dayStart = new Date(st.getTime());
        dayStart.setHours(9, 0, 0, 0);
        var dayEnd = new Date(st.getTime());
        dayEnd.setHours(21, 0, 0, 0);
        if (en <= dayStart || st >= dayEnd) continue; // no overlap with studio hours
        var importStart = st < dayStart ? dayStart : st;
        var importEnd = en > dayEnd ? dayEnd : en;
        if (importEnd <= importStart) continue;
        var eventId = '';
        try { eventId = String(ev.getId() || ''); } catch (_eid) { eventId = ''; }
        if (!eventId) continue;
        var rid = 'SRES_GCAL_' + _digestHex_(sid + '|' + eventId).substring(0, 20).toUpperCase();
        rows.push({
          id: rid,
          studio_id: studio.id,
          studio_name: studio.name,
          user_id: 'GCAL_IMPORT',
          user_name: 'Google Calendar Import',
          start_dt: importStart.toISOString(),
          end_dt: importEnd.toISOString(),
          purpose: String(ev.getTitle() || '').trim() || 'Imported from Google Calendar',
          pdf_url: '',
          key_id: (studio.keys && studio.keys.length) ? String(studio.keys[0]) : '',
          key_pickup_dt: importStart.toISOString(),
          status: STATUS.APPROVED,
          approved_by: 'GCAL_IMPORT',
          approved_at: now(),
          rejected_reason: '',
          is_weekend: (st.getDay() === 0 || st.getDay() === 6),
          notes: 'Imported from Google Calendar (' + sid + ')',
          created_at: now(),
          updated_at: now(),
          request_type: 'Google Calendar Import',
          studio_usage_form_url: '',
          studio_handover_note: '',
          return_handover_note: ''
        });
      }
    }
    if (previewOnly) {
      return { ok: true, dryRun: true, count: rows.length, sample: rows.slice(0, 10) };
    }
    var supaOnly = _supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_();
    if (!rows.length) return { ok: true, imported: 0, rowsBuilt: 0, mode: supaOnly ? 'supabase-only' : 'sheet+mirror' };
    if (supaOnly) {
      var payloads = rows.map(function(r) { return supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(r); });
      _supaUpsertBatchChunked_('studio_reservations', payloads, 'id', 25);
      return { ok: true, imported: rows.length, rowsBuilt: rows.length, mode: 'supabase-only' };
    }
    var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
    for (var k = 0; k < rows.length; k++) addRow(sh, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(rows[k]), SRSH);
    return { ok: true, imported: rows.length, rowsBuilt: rows.length, mode: 'sheet+mirror' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e), rowsBuilt: (rows && rows.length) ? rows.length : 0 };
  }
}

function getStudioWeeklyGridBridge(studioId, weekStartIso, testToken) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'Not signed in.' };
    return _studioWeeklyGridPayload_(studioId, weekStartIso, user, false);
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function getAdminStudioWeeklyGrid(studioId, weekStartIso, adminToken) {
  try {
    var adminUser = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!adminUser) return { error: 'Unauthorized.' };
    var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    var wk = Utilities.formatDate(_mondayStartForIso_(weekStartIso), Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'yyyy-MM-dd');
    var ck = _cacheKey_('adminStudioWeeklyGrid', [sid, wk, String(adminUser.role || '')]);
    var hit = _cacheGetJson_(ck);
    if (hit) return hit;
    var out = _studioWeeklyGridPayload_(sid, wk, adminUser, true);
    if (out && !out.error) _cachePutJson_(ck, out, 45);
    return out;
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(row) {
  var payload = supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(row);
  _supaUpsertBatch_('studio_reservations', [payload], 'id');
  _invalidateStudioReservationsCache_();
}

function _outlookStudioSyncCfg_() {
  // Outlook studio sync is intentionally disabled in this deployment.
  // Keep this hard-off so no Graph UrlFetch calls are attempted.
  return {
    enabled: false,
    tenantId: '',
    clientId: '',
    clientSecret: '',
    owner: '',
    redCalendarId: '',
    greenCalendarId: ''
  };
}

function _outlookStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(studioId) {
  var cfg = _outlookStudioSyncCfg_();
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid === 'RED') return cfg.redCalendarId;
  if (sid === 'GREEN') return cfg.greenCalendarId;
  return '';
}

function _outlookStudioSyncReadyForStudio_(studioId) {
  var cfg = _outlookStudioSyncCfg_();
  if (!cfg.enabled) return false;
  if (!cfg.tenantId || !cfg.clientId || !cfg.clientSecret || !cfg.owner) return false;
  return !!_outlookStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(studioId);
}

function _msGraphAppToken_() {
  var cfg = _outlookStudioSyncCfg_();
  if (!cfg.tenantId || !cfg.clientId || !cfg.clientSecret) throw new Error('Missing Microsoft Graph app credentials.');
  var tokenUrl = 'https://login.microsoftonline.com/' + encodeURIComponent(cfg.tenantId) + '/oauth2/v2.0/token';
  var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(tokenUrl, {
    method: 'post',
    muteHttpExceptions: true,
    payload: {
      grant_type: 'client_credentials',
      client_id: cfg.clientId,
      client_secret: cfg.clientSecret,
      scope: 'https://graph.microsoft.com/.default'
    }
  }, 'outlook.token');
  var code = resp.getResponseCode();
  var txt = resp.getContentText() || '';
  if (code >= 400) throw new Error('Graph token error ' + code + ': ' + txt);
  var obj = JSON.parse(txt || '{}');
  if (!obj.access_token) throw new Error('Graph token missing access_token.');
  return obj.access_token;
}

function _outlookStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId) {
  return 'OUTLOOK_STUDIO_EVENT_' + String(reservationId || '').trim();
}

function _outlookStudioGetStoredEventId_(reservationId) {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(_outlookStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId)) || '').trim();
}

function _outlookStudioSetStoredEventId_(reservationId, eventId) {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var key = _outlookStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId);
  var val = String(eventId || '').trim();
  if (!val) p.deleteProperty(key);
  else p.setProperty(key, val);
}

function _graphDateTimeLocal_(iso) {
  var d = new Date(iso);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) throw new Error('Invalid datetime: ' + iso);
  return Utilities.formatDate(d, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm:ss");
}

function _outlookStudioEventPayload_(res) {
  var studioName = String(res.studio_name || res.studio_id || 'Studio').trim();
  var userName = String(res.user_name || '').trim();
  var subject = studioName + ' | ' + (userName || String(res.user_id || 'Unknown'));
  var body = [
    'BookDeck Studio Reservation',
    'Reservation ID: ' + String(res.id || ''),
    'Studio: ' + studioName,
    'User: ' + (userName || '-'),
    'User ID: ' + String(res.user_id || '-'),
    'Purpose: ' + String(res.purpose || '-'),
    'Status: ' + String(res.status || '-')
  ].join('\n');
  return {
    subject: subject,
    body: { contentType: 'Text', content: body },
    start: { dateTime: _graphDateTimeLocal_(res.start_dt), timeZone: 'Turkey Standard Time' },
    end: { dateTime: _graphDateTimeLocal_(res.end_dt), timeZone: 'Turkey Standard Time' },
    location: { displayName: studioName },
    categories: ['BookDeck', studioName]
  };
}

function _graphCalendarEventsBaseUrl_(studioId) {
  var cfg = _outlookStudioSyncCfg_();
  var calId = _outlookStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(studioId);
  if (!cfg.owner || !calId) throw new Error('Outlook calendar mapping missing for studio.');
  return 'https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/users/' + encodeURIComponent(cfg.owner) + '/calendars/' + encodeURIComponent(calId) + '/events';
}

function syncStudioReservationToOutlook_(res) {
  if (!res) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'empty' };
  var sid = String(res.studio_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_outlookStudioSyncReadyForStudio_(sid)) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'not-configured' };
  var token = _msGraphAppToken_();
  var baseUrl = _graphCalendarEventsBaseUrl_(sid);
  var payload = _outlookStudioEventPayload_(res);
  var eventId = _outlookStudioGetStoredEventId_(res.id);
  var url = eventId ? (baseUrl + '/' + encodeURIComponent(eventId)) : baseUrl;
  var method = eventId ? 'patch' : 'post';
  var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(url, {
    method: method,
    muteHttpExceptions: true,
    contentType: 'application/json',
    headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token, Accept: 'application/json' },
    payload: JSON.stringify(payload)
  }, 'outlook.event.upsert');
  var code = resp.getResponseCode();
  var txt = resp.getContentText() || '';
  if (code >= 400) throw new Error('Graph event upsert error ' + code + ': ' + txt);
  if (!eventId) {
    var out = JSON.parse(txt || '{}');
    if (out && out.id) _outlookStudioSetStoredEventId_(res.id, out.id);
  }
  return { ok: true, action: eventId ? 'updated' : 'created' };
}

function deleteStudioReservationFromOutlook_(res) {
  if (!res) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'empty' };
  var sid = String(res.studio_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_outlookStudioSyncReadyForStudio_(sid)) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'not-configured' };
  var eventId = _outlookStudioGetStoredEventId_(res.id);
  if (!eventId) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'event-id-missing' };
  var token = _msGraphAppToken_();
  var url = _graphCalendarEventsBaseUrl_(sid) + '/' + encodeURIComponent(eventId);
  var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(url, {
    method: 'delete',
    muteHttpExceptions: true,
    headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token, Accept: 'application/json' }
  }, 'outlook.event.delete');
  var code = resp.getResponseCode();
  var txt = resp.getContentText() || '';
  if (code >= 400 && code !== 404) throw new Error('Graph event delete error ' + code + ': ' + txt);
  _outlookStudioSetStoredEventId_(res.id, '');
  return { ok: true, action: 'deleted' };
}

function _safeSyncStudioReservationOutlook_(res, mode, actorId) {
  try {
    if (mode === 'delete') return deleteStudioReservationFromOutlook_(res);
    return syncStudioReservationToOutlook_(res);
  } catch (e) {
    try {
      audit('studio.outlook_sync_error', String(actorId || 'system'), String((res && res.id) || ''), null, {
        mode: mode || 'upsert',
        message: e.message || String(e)
      });
    } catch (_eA) {}
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _googleStudioSyncEnabled_() {
  var v = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('GOOGLE_STUDIO_SYNC_ENABLED') || '').toLowerCase();
  if (!v) return true;
  return v === 'true';
}

function _googleStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(studioId) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  var meta = (STUDIO_CALENDAR_EMBEDS || {})[sid] || {};
  return String(meta.calId || '').trim();
}

function _googleStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId) {
  return 'GOOGLE_STUDIO_EVENT_' + String(reservationId || '').trim();
}

function _googleStudioGetStoredEventId_(reservationId) {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(_googleStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId)) || '').trim();
}

function _googleStudioSetStoredEventId_(reservationId, eventId) {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var key = _googleStudioEventPropKey_(reservationId);
  var val = String(eventId || '').trim();
  if (!val) p.deleteProperty(key);
  else p.setProperty(key, val);
}

function _isBookDeckManagedGoogleEvent_(ev) {
  try {
    var d = String(ev.getDescription() || '').toLowerCase();
    return d.indexOf('reservation id: sres-') >= 0 || d.indexOf('[bookdeck]') >= 0;
  } catch (_e) {
    return false;
  }
}

function _syncStudioReservationToGoogleCalendar_(res) {
  if (!res) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'empty' };
  var sid = String(res.studio_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_googleStudioSyncEnabled_()) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'disabled' };
  var calId = _googleStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(sid);
  if (!calId) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing-calendar-id' };
  var cal = CalendarApp.getCalendarById(calId);
  if (!cal) throw new Error('Google Calendar not accessible: ' + sid);
  var sdt = new Date(res.start_dt);
  var edt = new Date(res.end_dt);
  if (isNaN(sdt.getTime()) || isNaN(edt.getTime())) throw new Error('Invalid reservation datetime.');
  var title = String(res.studio_name || sid) + ' | ' + String(res.user_name || res.user_id || 'Unknown');
  var desc = [
    '[BookDeck]',
    'Reservation ID: ' + String(res.id || ''),
    'Studio: ' + String(res.studio_name || sid),
    'User: ' + String(res.user_name || '-'),
    'User ID: ' + String(res.user_id || '-'),
    'Purpose: ' + String(res.purpose || '-'),
    'Status: ' + String(res.status || '-')
  ].join('\n');
  var eventId = _googleStudioGetStoredEventId_(res.id);
  var ev = eventId ? cal.getEventById(eventId) : null;
  if (!ev) {
    ev = cal.createEvent(title, sdt, edt, { description: desc, location: String(res.studio_name || sid) });
    _googleStudioSetStoredEventId_(res.id, ev.getId());
    return { ok: true, action: 'created' };
  }
  ev.setTitle(title);
  ev.setDescription(desc);
  ev.setLocation(String(res.studio_name || sid));
  ev.setTime(sdt, edt);
  return { ok: true, action: 'updated' };
}

function _deleteStudioReservationFromGoogleCalendar_(res) {
  if (!res) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'empty' };
  var sid = String(res.studio_id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_googleStudioSyncEnabled_()) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'disabled' };
  var calId = _googleStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(sid);
  if (!calId) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing-calendar-id' };
  var cal = CalendarApp.getCalendarById(calId);
  if (!cal) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'calendar-not-found' };
  var eventId = _googleStudioGetStoredEventId_(res.id);
  if (!eventId) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'event-id-missing' };
  var ev = cal.getEventById(eventId);
  if (ev) ev.deleteEvent();
  _googleStudioSetStoredEventId_(res.id, '');
  return { ok: true, action: 'deleted' };
}

function _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(res, mode, actorId) {
  try {
    if (mode === 'delete') return _deleteStudioReservationFromGoogleCalendar_(res);
    return _syncStudioReservationToGoogleCalendar_(res);
  } catch (e) {
    try {
      audit('studio.calendar_sync_error', String(actorId || 'system'), String((res && res.id) || ''), null, {
        mode: mode || 'upsert',
        message: e.message || String(e)
      });
    } catch (_eA) {}
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _googleSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId) {
  return 'GOOGLE_SYNC_RES_' + String(studioId || '').toUpperCase() + '_' + String(eventId || '').trim();
}

function _googleSyncGetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eventId) {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(_googleSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId)) || '').trim();
}

function _googleSyncSetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eventId, resId) {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var key = _googleSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId);
  var val = String(resId || '').trim();
  if (!val) p.deleteProperty(key);
  else p.setProperty(key, val);
}

function _googleEventToStudioReservation_(studioId, studioName, ev) {
  if (!ev || ev.isAllDayEvent()) return null;
  var eid = String(ev.getId() || '').trim();
  if (!eid) return null;
  var mappedResId = _googleSyncGetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eid);
  var rid = mappedResId || ('SRES-GGL-' + eid.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/g, '').substring(0, 16).toUpperCase());
  var sdt = ev.getStartTime();
  var edt = ev.getEndTime();
  return {
    id: rid,
    studio_id: String(studioId || '').toUpperCase(),
    studio_name: studioName,
    user_id: 'GOOGLE_SYNC',
    user_name: String((ev.getCreators && ev.getCreators()[0]) || ev.getTitle() || 'Google User'),
    start_dt: sdt.toISOString(),
    end_dt: edt.toISOString(),
    purpose: String(ev.getTitle() || 'Google Event').substring(0, STUDIO_PROJECT_NAME_MAX_),
    pdf_url: 'GOOGLE_SYNC',
    key_id: '',
    key_pickup_dt: sdt.toISOString(),
    status: STATUS.APPROVED,
    approved_by: 'GOOGLE_SYNC',
    approved_at: now(),
    rejected_reason: '',
    is_weekend: (function() { var d = sdt.getDay(); return d === 0 || d === 6; })(),
    notes: '[GOOGLE_SYNC] event_id=' + eid,
    created_at: now(),
    updated_at: now(),
    request_type: 'Google Calendar',
    studio_usage_form_url: '',
    studio_handover_note: 'Google takvim senkron etkinliği',
    return_handover_note: ''
  };
}

function syncGoogleCalendarIntoStudio_(studioId, options) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_googleStudioSyncEnabled_()) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'disabled' };
  var calId = _googleStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(sid);
  if (!calId) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing-calendar-id' };
  var cal = CalendarApp.getCalendarById(calId);
  if (!cal) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'calendar-not-found' };
  var opts = options || {};
  var nowD = new Date();
  var from = new Date(nowD.getTime() - ((Number(opts.pastDays || 2) || 2) * 86400000));
  var to = new Date(nowD.getTime() + ((Number(opts.futureDays || 60) || 60) * 86400000));
  var evs = cal.getEvents(from, to) || [];
  var studioName = sid === 'RED' ? 'RED STUDIO' : 'GREEN STUDIO';
  var seen = {};
  var created = 0, updated = 0, ignored = 0;
  evs.forEach(function(ev) {
    var eid = String(ev.getId() || '').trim();
    if (!eid) return;
    seen[eid] = true;
    if (_isBookDeckManagedGoogleEvent_(ev)) { ignored++; return; }
    var res = _googleEventToStudioReservation_(sid, studioName, ev);
    if (!res) { ignored++; return; }
    var existed = !!toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) { return String(r.id) === String(res.id); });
    _upsertStudioReservationById_(res);
    _googleSyncSetResIdByEvent_(sid, eid, res.id);
    if (existed) updated++;
    else created++;
  });
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
  var prefix = 'GOOGLE_SYNC_RES_' + sid + '_';
  for (var k in props) {
    if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(props, k)) continue;
    if (k.indexOf(prefix) !== 0) continue;
    var eId = k.substring(prefix.length);
    if (seen[eId]) continue;
    var rid = String(props[k] || '').trim();
    if (rid) _deleteStudioReservationById_(rid);
    _googleSyncSetResIdByEvent_(sid, eId, '');
  }
  return { ok: true, studio: sid, created: created, updated: updated, ignored: ignored, totalEvents: evs.length };
}

function syncGoogleCalendarsToStudiosBridge(testToken) {
  var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
  if (!u || String(u.role || '').toLowerCase() !== 'super_admin') return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
  try {
    var a = syncGoogleCalendarIntoStudio_('RED', {});
    var b = syncGoogleCalendarIntoStudio_('GREEN', {});
    return { success: true, red: a, green: b };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function triggerGoogleStudioSyncPolling() {
  try {
    var r = syncGoogleCalendarIntoStudio_('RED', {});
    var g = syncGoogleCalendarIntoStudio_('GREEN', {});
    return { ok: true, red: r, green: g };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _outlookWebhookClientState_() {
  var v = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('OUTLOOK_WEBHOOK_CLIENT_STATE') || '').trim();
  return v || 'bookdeck-studio-sync';
}

function _clearOutlookStudioSyncProps_() {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var all = p.getProperties() || {};
  var removed = 0;
  Object.keys(all).forEach(function(k) {
    if (
      k.indexOf('OUTLOOK_') === 0 ||
      k.indexOf('MS_') === 0
    ) {
      p.deleteProperty(k);
      removed++;
    }
  });
  return { removed: removed };
}

function disableOutlookStudioInfraBridge(testToken) {
  try {
    var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!u || String(u.role || '').toLowerCase() !== 'super_admin') return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var c = _clearOutlookStudioSyncProps_();
    return { success: true, removed: c.removed, message: 'Outlook studio sync disabled and properties cleared.' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _outlookSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId) {
  return 'OUTLOOK_SYNC_RES_' + String(studioId || '').toUpperCase() + '_' + String(eventId || '').trim();
}

function _outlookSyncGetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eventId) {
  return String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(_outlookSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId)) || '').trim();
}

function _outlookSyncSetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eventId, resId) {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var key = _outlookSyncResIdByEventKey_(studioId, eventId);
  var val = String(resId || '').trim();
  if (!val) p.deleteProperty(key);
  else p.setProperty(key, val);
}

function _isBookDeckManagedOutlookEvent_(ev) {
  var body = String((((ev || {}).body || {}).content) || '').toLowerCase();
  if (body.indexOf('reservation id: sres-') >= 0) return true;
  var cats = (ev && ev.categories) || [];
  for (var i = 0; i < cats.length; i++) {
    if (String(cats[i] || '').toLowerCase() === 'bookdeck') return true;
  }
  return false;
}

function _outlookEventToStudioReservation_(studioId, studioName, ev) {
  var st = (((ev || {}).start || {}).dateTime) || '';
  var en = (((ev || {}).end || {}).dateTime) || '';
  var sdt = new Date(st);
  var edt = new Date(en);
  if (isNaN(sdt.getTime()) || isNaN(edt.getTime())) return null;
  var eid = String((ev && ev.id) || '').trim();
  if (!eid) return null;
  var mappedResId = _outlookSyncGetResIdByEvent_(studioId, eid);
  var rid = mappedResId || ('SRES-OLK-' + eid.replace(/[^A-Za-z0-9]/g, '').substring(0, 16).toUpperCase());
  var who = String((((ev || {}).organizer || {}).emailAddress || {}).name || '').trim() ||
    String((((ev || {}).organizer || {}).emailAddress || {}).address || '').trim() || 'Outlook User';
  var subj = String((ev && ev.subject) || '').trim() || 'Outlook Event';
