  return {
    id: rid,
    studio_id: String(studioId || '').toUpperCase(),
    studio_name: studioName,
    user_id: 'OUTLOOK_SYNC',
    user_name: who,
    start_dt: sdt.toISOString(),
    end_dt: edt.toISOString(),
    purpose: subj.substring(0, STUDIO_PROJECT_NAME_MAX_),
    pdf_url: 'OUTLOOK_SYNC',
    key_id: (function() {
      try {
        var stx = resolveStudio(studioId);
        return stx && stx.keys && stx.keys.length ? stx.keys[0] : '';
      } catch (_e) { return ''; }
    })(),
    key_pickup_dt: sdt.toISOString(),
    status: STATUS.APPROVED,
    approved_by: 'OUTLOOK_SYNC',
    approved_at: now(),
    rejected_reason: '',
    is_weekend: (function() { var d = sdt.getDay(); return d === 0 || d === 6; })(),
    notes: '[OUTLOOK_SYNC] event_id=' + eid,
    created_at: now(),
    updated_at: now(),
    request_type: 'Outlook',
    studio_usage_form_url: '',
    studio_handover_note: 'Outlook senkron etkinliği',
    return_handover_note: ''
  };
}

function _upsertStudioReservationById_(res) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(res);
    return;
  }
  var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  var rn = findRow(sh, res.id);
  if (rn === -1) addRow(sh, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(res), SRSH);
  else setRow(sh, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(res), SRSH);
  trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(res);
  _invalidateStudioReservationsCache_();
}

function _deleteStudioReservationById_(resId) {
  var id = String(resId || '').trim();
  if (!id) return;
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    var oldS = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) { return String(r.id) === id; });
    if (!oldS) return;
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(Object.assign({}, oldS, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() }));
    return;
  }
  var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  var rn = findRow(sh, id);
  if (rn === -1) return;
  var old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) { return String(r.id) === id; });
  if (!old) return;
  var up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sh, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
  trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  _invalidateStudioReservationsCache_();
}

function _fetchOutlookCalendarEventsWindow_(studioId, fromIso, toIso) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').toUpperCase();
  if (!_outlookStudioSyncReadyForStudio_(sid)) return [];
  var token = _msGraphAppToken_();
  var base = _graphCalendarEventsBaseUrl_(sid);
  var qs = '?$select=id,subject,start,end,organizer,categories,body,lastModifiedDateTime'
    + '&$top=200'
    + '&$filter=' + encodeURIComponent("start/dateTime ge '" + _graphDateTimeLocal_(fromIso) + "' and end/dateTime le '" + _graphDateTimeLocal_(toIso) + "'");
  var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_(base + qs, {
    method: 'get',
    muteHttpExceptions: true,
    headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token, Accept: 'application/json' }
  }, 'outlook.events.list');
  var code = resp.getResponseCode();
  var txt = resp.getContentText() || '';
  if (code >= 400) throw new Error('Graph list events error ' + code + ': ' + txt);
  var out = JSON.parse(txt || '{}');
  return (out && out.value) ? out.value : [];
}

function syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_(studioId, options) {
  var sid = String(studioId || '').toUpperCase();
  if (sid !== 'RED' && sid !== 'GREEN') return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'unsupported-studio' };
  if (!_outlookStudioSyncReadyForStudio_(sid)) return { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'not-configured' };
  var opts = options || {};
  var nowD = new Date();
  var from = new Date(nowD.getTime() - ((Number(opts.pastDays || 2) || 2) * 86400000));
  var to = new Date(nowD.getTime() + ((Number(opts.futureDays || 60) || 60) * 86400000));
  var evs = _fetchOutlookCalendarEventsWindow_(sid, from.toISOString(), to.toISOString());
  var studioName = sid === 'RED' ? 'RED STUDIO' : 'GREEN STUDIO';
  var seen = {};
  var created = 0, updated = 0, ignored = 0;
  evs.forEach(function(ev) {
    var eid = String((ev && ev.id) || '').trim();
    if (!eid) return;
    seen[eid] = true;
    if (_isBookDeckManagedOutlookEvent_(ev)) { ignored++; return; }
    var res = _outlookEventToStudioReservation_(sid, studioName, ev);
    if (!res) { ignored++; return; }
    var existed = !!toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) { return String(r.id) === String(res.id); });
    _upsertStudioReservationById_(res);
    _outlookSyncSetResIdByEvent_(sid, eid, res.id);
    if (existed) updated++;
    else created++;
  });
  // Cleanup deleted Outlook events from previously synced mappings.
  var props = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperties();
  var prefix = 'OUTLOOK_SYNC_RES_' + sid + '_';
  for (var k in props) {
    if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(props, k)) continue;
    if (k.indexOf(prefix) !== 0) continue;
    var eId = k.substring(prefix.length);
    if (seen[eId]) continue;
    var rid = String(props[k] || '').trim();
    if (rid) _deleteStudioReservationById_(rid);
    _outlookSyncSetResIdByEvent_(sid, eId, '');
  }
  return { ok: true, studio: sid, created: created, updated: updated, ignored: ignored, totalEvents: evs.length };
}

function syncOutlookCalendarsToStudiosBridge(testToken) {
  var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
  if (!u || String(u.role || '').toLowerCase() !== 'super_admin') return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
  try {
    var a = syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('RED', {});
    var b = syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('GREEN', {});
    return { success: true, red: a, green: b };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function handleMicrosoftGraphWebhook_(e) {
  var bodyTxt = (e && e.postData && e.postData.contents) ? String(e.postData.contents) : '{}';
  var body = JSON.parse(bodyTxt || '{}');
  var val = body.value || [];
  var expectedState = _outlookWebhookClientState_();
  var accepted = 0;
  for (var i = 0; i < val.length; i++) {
    var n = val[i] || {};
    var cs = String(n.clientState || '').trim();
    if (cs && cs !== expectedState) continue;
    accepted++;
  }
  if (accepted > 0) {
    try { syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('RED', {}); } catch (_e1) {}
    try { syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('GREEN', {}); } catch (_e2) {}
  }
  return { accepted: accepted, notifications: val.length };
}

function ensureOutlookStudioWebhookSubscriptions() {
  var cfg = _outlookStudioSyncCfg_();
  if (!cfg.enabled) return { ok: false, error: 'OUTLOOK_STUDIO_SYNC_ENABLED false.' };
  if (!cfg.tenantId || !cfg.clientId || !cfg.clientSecret || !cfg.owner) return { ok: false, error: 'Missing Graph app settings.' };
  var appUrl = String(CONFIG.APP_URL || '').trim();
  if (!appUrl) return { ok: false, error: 'CONFIG.APP_URL missing.' };
  var notifUrl = appUrl + (appUrl.indexOf('?') >= 0 ? '&' : '?') + 'msgraph=1';
  var token = _msGraphAppToken_();
  var expires = new Date(Date.now() + (2 * 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000)); // ~2 days, safer than max
  var expIso = expires.toISOString();
  var out = {};
  ['RED', 'GREEN'].forEach(function(sid) {
    var calId = _outlookStudioCalendarIdByStudio_(sid);
    if (!calId) { out[sid] = { ok: false, skipped: true, reason: 'missing-calendar-id' }; return; }
    var payload = {
      changeType: 'created,updated,deleted',
      notificationUrl: notifUrl,
      resource: 'users/' + cfg.owner + '/calendars/' + calId + '/events',
      expirationDateTime: expIso,
      clientState: _outlookWebhookClientState_()
    };
    var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_('https://graph.microsoft.com/v1.0/subscriptions', {
      method: 'post',
      muteHttpExceptions: true,
      contentType: 'application/json',
      headers: { Authorization: 'Bearer ' + token, Accept: 'application/json' },
      payload: JSON.stringify(payload)
    }, 'outlook.subscription.create');
    var code = resp.getResponseCode();
    var txt = resp.getContentText() || '';
    if (code >= 400) {
      out[sid] = { ok: false, code: code, error: txt };
      return;
    }
    var sub = JSON.parse(txt || '{}');
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('OUTLOOK_SUB_' + sid + '_ID', String(sub.id || ''));
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty('OUTLOOK_SUB_' + sid + '_EXPIRES', String(sub.expirationDateTime || ''));
    out[sid] = { ok: true, id: sub.id || '', expires: sub.expirationDateTime || '' };
  });
  return out;
}

function triggerOutlookStudioSyncPolling() {
  try {
    var r = syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('RED', {});
    var g = syncOutlookCalendarIntoStudio_('GREEN', {});
    return { ok: true, red: r, green: g };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function triggerOutlookStudioSubscriptionRenewal() {
  return ensureOutlookStudioWebhookSubscriptions();
}

/** Stüdyo rezervasyonu "project name" (purpose) — max karakter. */
var STUDIO_PROJECT_NAME_MAX_ = 20;
function studioProjectNameNormalized_(rawPurpose, isAdmin) {
  var s = String(rawPurpose || '').trim();
  if (s.length > STUDIO_PROJECT_NAME_MAX_) s = s.substring(0, STUDIO_PROJECT_NAME_MAX_);
  if (!isAdmin && !s) throw new Error('Project name is required (max 20 characters).');
  if (isAdmin && !s) s = 'Admin';
  return s;
}

function studioReservationsCreate(payload, user) {
  const isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role);
  const uEnrich = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
  const access = canUserAccessStudio(user, payload.studio_id); if (!access.ok) throw new Error(access.reason);
  const studio = resolveStudio(payload.studio_id); if (!studio) throw new Error('Invalid studio.');
  const banCheck = restrictionsCheckBan(user.id); if (banCheck.banned) throw new Error('Account suspended.');
  const start = new Date(payload.start_dt); const end = new Date(payload.end_dt); const startDay = start.getDay(); const isWeekend = startDay === 0 || startDay === 6;
  if (!payload.start_dt || !payload.end_dt) throw new Error('Dates required.'); if (end <= start) throw new Error('Invalid dates.');
  if (!isAdmin && start.toDateString() !== end.toDateString()) throw new Error('Same day only.');
  validateBookingDateTime('studio', payload.start_dt, payload.end_dt, uEnrich);
  const openH = 9, closeH = 21;
  if (!isAdmin) { const sh = start.getHours(), em = end.getHours() * 60 + end.getMinutes(); if (sh < openH || em > closeH * 60) throw new Error('09:00-21:00 only.'); if (start.getMinutes() !== 0) throw new Error('Hourly slots only (start at :00).'); if (end.getMinutes() !== 0) throw new Error('Hourly slots only (end at :00).'); if (isWeekend && !studio.weekendOk) throw new Error('Closed weekends.'); }
  // Aynı kullanıcı aynı stüdyo için çakışan ikinci rezervasyon açamasın.
  try {
    var block = studioStatusesBlockingKey_();
    var uidMe = String(user.id || '').trim();
    var sidMe = String(studio.id || '').trim();
    var sMs = start.getTime();
    var eMs = end.getTime();
    var dup = toObjsStudioReservations_().some(function(r) {
      if (String(r.user_id || '').trim() !== uidMe) return false;
      if (String(r.studio_id || '').trim() !== sidMe) return false;
      if (block.indexOf(String(r.status || '').toLowerCase()) === -1) return false;
      var rs = new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
      var re = new Date(r.end_dt).getTime();
      if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) return false;
      return sMs < re && eMs > rs;
    });
    if (dup) throw new Error('You already have an active reservation for this studio and time range.');
  } catch (_dupErr) {
    if (_dupErr && _dupErr.message) throw _dupErr;
  }
  var calCheck = studioCalendarCheckRange_(payload.studio_id, payload.start_dt, payload.end_dt);
  if (calCheck.error && !calCheck.skipped) throw new Error(calCheck.error);
  if (calCheck.busy) throw new Error('The time range you selected is not available for this studio reservation.');
  var reqType = String(payload.request_type || '').trim();
  if (!isAdmin) {
    if (!reqType || STUDIO_REQUEST_TYPES.indexOf(reqType) === -1) throw new Error('Geçerli bir talep türü seçin.');
  } else if (reqType && STUDIO_REQUEST_TYPES.indexOf(reqType) === -1) {
    throw new Error('Geçersiz talep türü.');
  }
  var purposeNorm = studioProjectNameNormalized_(payload.purpose, isAdmin);
  let pdfUrl = payload.pdf_url || '';
  if (payload.pdf_base64 && !pdfUrl) { try { const folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.STUDIO_PDF_FOLDER_ID); const fname = (user.id + '_studio_' + Date.now() + '.pdf').replace(/[^a-zA-Z0-9._-]/g, '_'); const blob = Utilities.newBlob(Utilities.base64Decode(payload.pdf_base64), 'application/pdf', fname); const file = folder.createFile(blob); file.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW); pdfUrl = file.getUrl(); } catch(e) { throw new Error('PDF upload failed.'); } }
  let keyPickupDt = payload.key_pickup_dt || '';
  let keyId = '';
  if (studio.id === 'GREEN') {
    if (isWeekend) {
      if (!payload.key_pickup_dt) throw new Error('Friday pickup required.');
      const pickup = new Date(payload.key_pickup_dt);
      if (pickup.getDay() !== 5) throw new Error('Friday pickup only.');
      const ph = pickup.getHours(), pm = pickup.getMinutes();
      if (ph < 9 || ph > 16 || (ph === 16 && pm > 0)) throw new Error('09:00-16:00 pickup only.');
      keyPickupDt = payload.key_pickup_dt;
    } else {
      // Hafta içi: stüdyo kullanımıyla aynı zaman anahtar teslim zamanı kabul edilir.
      keyPickupDt = payload.start_dt;
    }
    keyId = studioFindAvailableKey('GKEY', studio.keyCount, payload.start_dt, payload.end_dt, isWeekend ? keyPickupDt : null); if (!keyId) throw new Error('No keys.');
  } else {
    // Tüm stüdyolarda rezervasyon = anahtar teslim/iade akışı.
    keyPickupDt = payload.start_dt;
    const studioKey = studio.keys[0];
    const keyBusy = studioCheckKeyBusy(studioKey, payload.start_dt, payload.end_dt);
    if (keyBusy) throw new Error('Fully booked.');
    keyId = studioKey;
  }
  var isAdminWebDirect = payload._bookdeck_admin_direct_studio === true && String(pdfUrl || '').trim() === 'ADMIN_RESERVATION' && String(payload.admin_approved_by || '').trim() !== '';
  var statusVal = isAdminWebDirect ? STATUS.APPROVED : STATUS.PENDING;
  var apprBy = isAdminWebDirect ? (String(payload.admin_approved_by || '').trim() || 'admin_web') : '';
  var apprAt = isAdminWebDirect ? now() : '';
  const sheet = _supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_() ? null : getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  const resId = genId('SRES');
  var res = { id: resId, studio_id: studio.id, studio_name: studio.name, user_id: user.id, user_name: user.name, start_dt: payload.start_dt, end_dt: payload.end_dt, purpose: purposeNorm, pdf_url: pdfUrl, key_id: keyId, key_pickup_dt: keyPickupDt, status: statusVal, approved_by: apprBy, approved_at: apprAt, rejected_reason: '', is_weekend: isWeekend, notes: payload.notes || '', created_at: now(), updated_at: now(), request_type: reqType, studio_usage_form_url: '', studio_handover_note: '', return_handover_note: '' };
  if (isAdminWebDirect) {
    try {
      var _formAdm = generateDeliveryPDF(CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID, buildStudioUsageFormMergeData_(res, 'Onaylandı — depo tesliminde imza ve not güncellenir.'));
      if (_formAdm) res.studio_usage_form_url = _formAdm;
    } catch (_pdfAdm) {}
  }
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(res);
  else { addRow(sheet, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(res), SRSH); trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(res); }
  if (String(res.status || '').toLowerCase() === STATUS.APPROVED) {
    _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(res, 'upsert', user.id);
  }
  if (isAdminWebDirect) {
    try { sendNotif(res.user_id, 'studio.approved', 'Approved.', resId); } catch (_snAdm) {}
  } else {
    notifyAdmins('studio.new', 'Studio request: ' + resId, resId);
    try { notifyIiwAdminsPodcastPendingMail_(res, user); } catch (_eIiwMail) {}
  }
  audit('studio.create', user.id, resId, null, res);
  return { success: true, res_id: resId, studio: studio.name };
}
function studioFindAvailableKey(prefix, count, startDt, endDt, fridayPickupDt, excludeReservationId) {
  const block = studioStatusesBlockingKey_();
  const ex = String(excludeReservationId || '').trim();
  const existing = toObjsStudioReservations_().filter(function(r) {
    if (ex && String(r.id) === ex) return false;
    return String(r.key_id).startsWith(prefix) && block.indexOf(String(r.status).toLowerCase()) !== -1;
  });
  for (let i = 1; i <= count; i++) {
    const keyId = prefix + '-0' + i;
    const s = new Date(startDt).getTime();
    const e = new Date(endDt).getTime();
    const busy = existing.some(function(r) {
      if (r.key_id !== keyId) return false;
      const rs = new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
      const re = new Date(r.end_dt).getTime();
      if (s < re && e > rs) return true;
      if (fridayPickupDt && r.key_pickup_dt) {
        const fp = new Date(fridayPickupDt).getTime();
        const rfp = new Date(r.key_pickup_dt).getTime();
        if (Math.abs(fp - rfp) < 1800000) return true;
      }
      return false;
    });
    if (!busy) return keyId;
  }
  return null;
}
function studioCheckKeyBusy(keyId, startDt, endDt, excludeReservationId) {
  const s = new Date(startDt).getTime();
  const e = new Date(endDt).getTime();
  const block = studioStatusesBlockingKey_();
  const ex = String(excludeReservationId || '').trim();
  return toObjsStudioReservations_().filter(function(r) {
    if (ex && String(r.id) === ex) return false;
    return r.key_id === keyId && block.indexOf(String(r.status).toLowerCase()) !== -1;
  }).some(function(r) {
    return s < new Date(r.end_dt).getTime() && e > new Date(r.start_dt).getTime();
  });
}
function studioReservationsList(payload, user) { const isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role); let list = toObjsStudioReservations_(); if (!isAdmin) list = list.filter(r => r.user_id === user.id); if (payload.studio_id) list = list.filter(r => r.studio_id === payload.studio_id); if (payload.status) list = list.filter(r => r.status === payload.status); return list.sort((a, b) => new Date(b.created_at) - new Date(a.created_at)); }
function studioReservationsApprove(payload, actor) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    const oldS = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) { return r.id === payload.id; });
    if (!oldS) throw new Error('Not found.');
    var upS = Object.assign({}, oldS, { status: STATUS.APPROVED, approved_by: actor.id, approved_at: now(), updated_at: now() });
    try {
      var formUrlS = generateDeliveryPDF(CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID, buildStudioUsageFormMergeData_(upS, 'Onaylandı — depo tesliminde imza ve not güncellenir.'));
      if (formUrlS) upS = Object.assign({}, upS, { studio_usage_form_url: formUrlS });
    } catch (_pdfErrS) {}
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(upS);
    _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(upS, 'upsert', actor.id);
    sendNotif(oldS.user_id, 'studio.approved', 'Approved.', payload.id);
    audit('studio.approve', actor.id, payload.id, oldS, upS);
    return upS;
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(r => r.id === payload.id);
  if (!old) throw new Error('Not found.');
  var up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.APPROVED, approved_by: actor.id, approved_at: now(), updated_at: now() });
  var formUrl = '';
  try {
    formUrl = generateDeliveryPDF(CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID, buildStudioUsageFormMergeData_(up, 'Onaylandı — depo tesliminde imza ve not güncellenir.'));
  } catch (pdfErr) {
    Logger.log('studioReservationsApprove PDF: ' + (pdfErr.message || pdfErr));
  }
  if (formUrl) up = Object.assign({}, up, { studio_usage_form_url: formUrl });
  setRow(sheet, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
  trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(up, 'upsert', actor.id);
  sendNotif(old.user_id, 'studio.approved', 'Approved.', payload.id);
  audit('studio.approve', actor.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}
function studioReservationsReject(payload, actor) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    const old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(r => r.id === payload.id);
    if (!old) throw new Error('Not found.');
    const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.REJECTED, approved_by: actor.id, approved_at: now(), rejected_reason: payload.reason || '', updated_at: now() });
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(up);
    _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(up, 'delete', actor.id);
    sendNotif(old.user_id, 'studio.rejected', 'Rejected.', payload.id);
    audit('studio.reject', actor.id, payload.id, old, up);
    return up;
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(r => r.id === payload.id);
  if (!old) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.REJECTED, approved_by: actor.id, approved_at: now(), rejected_reason: payload.reason || '', updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sheet, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
  trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(up, 'delete', actor.id);
  sendNotif(old.user_id, 'studio.rejected', 'Rejected.', payload.id);
  audit('studio.reject', actor.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}
function studioReservationsCancel(payload, user) {
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    const old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(r => r.id === payload.id);
    if (!old) throw new Error('Not found.');
    const isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role);
    if (old.user_id !== user.id && !isAdmin) throw new Error('Denied.');
    const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() });
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(up);
    _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(up, 'delete', user.id);
    if (!isAdmin) { try { var stDt0 = new Date(old.start_dt); if (!isNaN(stDt0.getTime())) { var leftMs0 = stDt0.getTime() - Date.now(); if (leftMs0 <= 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) { var ban0 = { id: genId('BAN'), user_id: String(user.id || ''), user_name: String(user.name || old.user_name || ''), ban_level: BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, reason: 'Yellow Warning: Studio late cancellation (<=24h).', banned_by: String(user.id || ''), banned_at: now(), expires_at: '', active: false, notes: 'Studio reservation: ' + String(old.id || '') }; addRow(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS), ban0, BAH); sendNotif(String(user.id || ''), 'ban.' + BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, ban0.reason, ban0.id); notifyAdmins('ban.' + BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, ban0.reason + ' User: ' + String(user.id || ''), ban0.id); audit('ban.applyStudioLateCancel', String(user.id || ''), String(user.id || ''), null, ban0); } } } catch (_eLate0) {} }
    audit('studio.cancel', user.id, payload.id, old, up);
    return up;
  }
  const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  const rn = findRow(sheet, payload.id);
  if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const old = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(r => r.id === payload.id);
  if (!old) throw new Error('Not found.');
  const isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role);
  if (old.user_id !== user.id && !isAdmin) throw new Error('Denied.');
  const up = Object.assign({}, old, { status: STATUS.CANCELLED, updated_at: now() });
  setRow(sheet, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
  trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  _safeSyncStudioReservationExternalCalendar_(up, 'delete', user.id);
  if (!isAdmin) { try { var stDt = new Date(old.start_dt); if (!isNaN(stDt.getTime())) { var leftMs = stDt.getTime() - Date.now(); if (leftMs <= 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000) { var ban = { id: genId('BAN'), user_id: String(user.id || ''), user_name: String(user.name || old.user_name || ''), ban_level: BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, reason: 'Yellow Warning: Studio late cancellation (<=24h).', banned_by: String(user.id || ''), banned_at: now(), expires_at: '', active: false, notes: 'Studio reservation: ' + String(old.id || '') }; addRow(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS), ban, BAH); sendNotif(String(user.id || ''), 'ban.' + BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, ban.reason, ban.id); notifyAdmins('ban.' + BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW, ban.reason + ' User: ' + String(user.id || ''), ban.id); audit('ban.applyStudioLateCancel', String(user.id || ''), String(user.id || ''), null, ban); } } } catch (_eLate) {} }
  audit('studio.cancel', user.id, payload.id, old, up);
  return up;
}

    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return String(iso || '');

  } catch (e) { return String(iso || ''); }
}

function setupTriggers() {
  ScriptApp.getProjectTriggers().forEach(function(t) { ScriptApp.deleteTrigger(t); });
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('triggerCheckOverdue').timeBased().everyDays(1).atHour(7).create();
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('triggerReservationReminderMails').timeBased().everyHours(1).create();
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('triggerAutoCancelPickupNoShow').timeBased().everyMinutes(15).create();
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('triggerAutoCancelStudioNoShow').timeBased().everyMinutes(15).create();
  ScriptApp.newTrigger('triggerGoogleStudioSyncPolling').timeBased().everyMinutes(15).create();
  return { triggers_set: 5 };
}
function triggerCheckOverdue() { const n = new Date(); const items = reportsOverdueItems(); const systemActor = { id: 'SYSTEM', role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN }; items.forEach(item => { const sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY); const rn = findRow(sheet, item.id); if (rn !== -1) setRow(sheet, rn, Object.assign({}, item, { status: STATUS.OVERDUE, updated_at: now() }), IH); if (item.assigned_to && item.due_date) { restrictionsApplyDelay({ user_id: item.assigned_to, item_id: item.id, item_name: item.name, due_dt: item.due_date, condition: 'good', notes: 'Automated overdue.' }, systemActor); } }); }

function triggerAutoCancelPickupNoShow() {
  try {
    var graceMinCfg = parseInt(adminGetConfigValue('pickup_no_show_blocked_grace_minutes') || '30', 10);
    if (isNaN(graceMinCfg)) graceMinCfg = 30;
    graceMinCfg = Math.max(5, Math.min(180, graceMinCfg));
    var GRACE_MS = graceMinCfg * 60 * 1000;
    var stateKey = 'NOSHOW_BLOCKED_GRACE_V1';
    function rowGraceKey_(rid, eqid) { return String(rid || '').trim() + '|' + String(eqid || '').trim(); }
    function parseGraceMap_() {
      try {
        var raw = String(PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty(stateKey) || '');
        if (!raw) return {};
        var obj = JSON.parse(raw);
        return (obj && typeof obj === 'object') ? obj : {};
      } catch (_e) { return {}; }
    }
    function saveGraceMap_(m) {
      try {
        PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().setProperty(stateKey, JSON.stringify(m || {}));
      } catch (_e) {}
    }

    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (!data || data.length < 2) return { ok: true, cancelled: 0 };
    var colN = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var invList = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY));
    var graceMap = parseGraceMap_();
    var graceChanged = false;
    var activeApprovedKeys = {};
    function pickupBlockedBecauseEquipmentStillWithSomeoneElse_(equipmentId, reservationStudentId) {
      var eq = String(equipmentId || '').trim();
      var sid = String(reservationStudentId || '').trim();
      for (var k = 0; k < invList.length; k++) {
        var it = invList[k];
        if (String(it.id || '').trim() !== eq) continue;
        var ust = String(it.status || '').toUpperCase().replace(/\s/g, '_');
        var inUse = ust === 'IN_USE' || ust === 'TAKEN' || ust === 'OVERDUE';
        if (!inUse) return false;
        var holder = String(it.assigned_to || '').trim();
        if (!holder || holder === sid) return false;
        return true;
      }
      return false;
    }
    var grouped = {}; // resId -> {userId,userName,start,items[]}
    var cancelled = 0;
    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      var st = String(row[colN.status] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (st !== 'approved') continue;
      var pickup = new Date(row[colN.handover]);
      if (isNaN(pickup.getTime())) continue;
      var eqIdForRow = String(row[colN.eqId] || '').trim();
      var resStudent = String(row[colN.student] || '').trim();
      var rid = String(row[colN.group] || '').trim() || ('ROW_' + (i + 1));
      var gk = rowGraceKey_(rid, eqIdForRow);
      activeApprovedKeys[gk] = true;
      var baseThresholdMs = pickup.getTime() + GRACE_MS;

      if (pickupBlockedBecauseEquipmentStillWithSomeoneElse_(eqIdForRow, resStudent)) {
        var ext = nowMs + GRACE_MS;
        var cur = Number(graceMap[gk] || 0);
        if (ext > cur) {
          graceMap[gk] = ext;
          graceChanged = true;
          audit('reservation.no_show_grace_due_to_late_return', 'SYSTEM', rid, null, {
            equipment_id: eqIdForRow,
            grace_until: new Date(ext).toISOString()
          }, 'Auto no-show grace applied');
        }
        continue;
      }

      var effectiveThresholdMs = Math.max(baseThresholdMs, Number(graceMap[gk] || 0));
      if (nowMs <= effectiveThresholdMs) continue;
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, colN.status + 1).setValue('Cancelled');
      cancelled++;
      if (!grouped[rid]) grouped[rid] = {
        userId: String(row[colN.student] || '').trim(),
        userName: String(row[colN.studentName] || '').trim(),
        start: String(row[colN.handover] || ''),
        items: []
      };
      grouped[rid].items.push(String(row[colN.name] || row[colN.eqId] || '').trim());
      if (graceMap[gk]) {
        delete graceMap[gk];
        graceChanged = true;
      }
    }

    // approved olmayan (picked up/cancelled/rejected...) kayıtların eski grace state'ini temizle.
    Object.keys(graceMap).forEach(function(k) {
      if (!activeApprovedKeys[k]) {
        delete graceMap[k];
        graceChanged = true;
      }
    });
    if (graceChanged) saveGraceMap_(graceMap);

    if (!cancelled) return { ok: true, cancelled: 0 };
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    Object.keys(grouped).forEach(function(rid) {
      var g = grouped[rid];
      var itemCsv = g.items.join(', ');
      var penalty = applyNoShowPickupPenalty_(g.userId, g.userName, rid, itemCsv, 'SYSTEM');
      var u = _mailUserByReservationId(g.userId);
      if (!u.email) return;
      var list = g.items.map(function(x) { return '<li>' + x + '</li>'; }).join('');
      var penaltyTr = '';
      var penaltyEn = '';
      if (penalty) {
        if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> İlk no-show olduğu için sarı uyarı kaydı oluşturulmuştur.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> First no-show recorded as a yellow warning.</p>';
        } else if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY7) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> İkinci no-show nedeniyle hesabınız 7 gün askıya alınmıştır.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> Your account is suspended for 7 days due to second no-show.</p>';
        } else if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY15) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> Üçüncü ve üzeri no-show nedeniyle hesabınız 15 gün askıya alınmıştır.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> Your account is suspended for 15 days due to repeated no-show.</p>';
        }
      }
      var body = '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayın ' + (g.userName || u.name || '') + ',</p>' +
        '<p><strong>' + rid + '</strong> numaralı rezervasyonunuz, teslim alma saatinden itibaren 30 dakika içinde E1-107 Depo’dan teslim alınmadığı için otomatik iptal edilmiştir.</p>' +
        (list ? '<p>Iptal edilen kalemler:</p><ul>' + list + '</ul>' : '') +
        penaltyTr +
        '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
        '<p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (g.userName || u.name || '') + ',</p>' +
        '<p>Your reservation <strong>' + rid + '</strong> has been automatically cancelled because pickup was not completed within 30 minutes of the pickup time.</p>' +
        (list ? '<p>Cancelled items:</p><ul>' + list + '</ul>' : '') +
        penaltyEn +
        '<p>Bilgi Booking</p>';
      sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Rezervasyon otomatik iptal edildi / Reservation auto-cancelled', body);
    });
    return { ok: true, cancelled: cancelled, groups: Object.keys(grouped).length };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

function triggerAutoCancelStudioNoShow() {
  try {
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
    var cancelled = 0;
    for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
      var old = rows[i];
      var st = String(old.status || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (st !== 'approved') continue;
      var pickupAt = old.key_pickup_dt ? new Date(old.key_pickup_dt) : new Date(old.start_dt);
      if (isNaN(pickupAt.getTime())) continue;
      if (nowMs - pickupAt.getTime() < 30 * 60 * 1000) continue; // 30 min grace
      var up = Object.assign({}, old, {
        status: STATUS.CANCELLED,
        updated_at: now(),
        rejected_reason: String(old.rejected_reason || '') || 'Auto-cancelled: studio no-show (>30m).'
      });
      var sh = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
      var rn = findRow(sh, old.id);
      if (rn === -1) continue;
      setRow(sh, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
      trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
      cancelled++;

      var penalty = applyNoShowStudioPenalty_(old.user_id, old.user_name, old.id, old.studio_name, 'SYSTEM');
      var u = _mailUserByReservationId(old.user_id);
      if (!u.email) continue;
      var penaltyTr = '';
      var penaltyEn = '';
      if (penalty) {
        if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.YELLOW) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> İlk stüdyo no-show olduğu için sarı uyarı kaydı oluşturulmuştur.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> First studio no-show recorded as a yellow warning.</p>';
        } else if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY7) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> İkinci stüdyo no-show nedeniyle hesabınız 7 gün askıya alınmıştır.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> Your account is suspended for 7 days due to second studio no-show.</p>';
        } else if (penalty.level === BAN_LEVELS.DAY15) {
          penaltyTr = '<p><strong>Ceza:</strong> Üçüncü ve üzeri stüdyo no-show nedeniyle hesabınız 15 gün askıya alınmıştır.</p>';
          penaltyEn = '<p><strong>Penalty:</strong> Your account is suspended for 15 days due to repeated studio no-show.</p>';
        }
      }
      var body = '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayın ' + (old.user_name || u.name || '') + ',</p>' +
        '<p><strong>' + String(old.id || '') + '</strong> numaralı stüdyo rezervasyonunuz, başlangıç saatinden itibaren 30 dakika içinde teslim alınmadığı için otomatik iptal edilmiştir.</p>' +
        '<p><strong>Stüdyo:</strong> ' + String(old.studio_name || '') + '</p>' +
        penaltyTr +
        '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
        '<p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (old.user_name || u.name || '') + ',</p>' +
        '<p>Your studio reservation <strong>' + String(old.id || '') + '</strong> has been automatically cancelled because pickup/check-in was not completed within 30 minutes of the start time.</p>' +
        '<p><strong>Studio:</strong> ' + String(old.studio_name || '') + '</p>' +
        penaltyEn +
        '<p>Bilgi Booking</p>';
      sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Stüdyo rezervasyonu otomatik iptal / Studio reservation auto-cancelled', body);
      audit('studio.no_show.auto_cancel', 'SYSTEM', old.id, old, up);
    }
    return { ok: true, cancelled: cancelled };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function triggerReservationReminderMails() {
  try {
    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (!data || data.length < 2) return { ok: true, sent: 0 };
    var colR = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var today = new Date(nowMs);
    var hour = today.getHours();
    var sent = 0;
    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      var status = String(row[colR.status] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (status !== 'approved' && status !== 'picked up') continue;
      var eqId = String(row[colR.eqId] || '').trim();
      var eqName = String((colR.name >= 0 ? row[colR.name] : '') || eqId).trim();
      var userRef = String(row[colR.student] || '').trim();
      var userName = String(row[colR.studentName] || '').trim();
      var start = new Date(row[colR.handover]);
      var end = new Date(row[colR.ret]);
      if (isNaN(start.getTime()) || isNaN(end.getTime())) continue;
      var u = _mailUserByReservationId(userRef);
      if (!u.email) continue;
      var baseKey = String(row[colR.group] || '') + '_' + eqId;

      // Pickup day morning reminder (08:00)
      var isPickupDay = start.getFullYear() === today.getFullYear() && start.getMonth() === today.getMonth() && start.getDate() === today.getDate();
      if (isPickupDay && hour === 8) {
        var k1 = 'mail_pickup_' + baseKey + '_' + Utilities.formatDate(today, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd');
        if (!_mailRememberSent(k1)) {
          sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Bugun teslim alinacak ekipman / Pickup reminder', '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayin ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>Bugun teslim alacaginiz ekipman: <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong>.</p><hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;"><p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>Your pickup reminder for today: <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong>.</p><p>Bilgi Booking</p>');
          sent++;
        }
      }

      // Return reminders
      var durMs = end.getTime() - start.getTime();
      var leftMs = end.getTime() - nowMs;
      if (durMs > 86400000) {
        // >1 day: return day morning at 08:00
        var isReturnDay = end.getFullYear() === today.getFullYear() && end.getMonth() === today.getMonth() && end.getDate() === today.getDate();
        if (isReturnDay && hour === 8) {
          var k2 = 'mail_return_day_' + baseKey + '_' + Utilities.formatDate(today, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd');
          if (!_mailRememberSent(k2)) {
            sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Bugun iade hatirlatmasi / Return reminder', '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayin ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>Bugun iade etmeniz gereken ekipman: <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong>.</p><p>Lutfen ekipmanlari eksiksiz, pilleri sarj ederek; tripod varsa plate aksami eksiksiz ve kameraya takili olmayacak sekilde teslim edin.</p><hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;"><p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>Your return reminder for today: <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong>.</p><p>Please return all items complete; charge batteries; and if a tripod is included, return the plate complete and not attached to the camera.</p><p>Bilgi Booking</p>');
            sent++;
          }
        }
      } else {
        // <=1 day: 2 hours before, but no mail if total duration < 2 hours
        if (durMs >= 7200000 && leftMs <= 7200000 && leftMs > 3600000) {
          var k3 = 'mail_return_2h_' + baseKey + '_' + Utilities.formatDate(today, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMddHH');
          if (!_mailRememberSent(k3)) {
            sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Iade zamani yaklasiyor / Return in 2 hours', '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayin ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p><strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong> iadesine yaklasik 2 saat kaldi.</p><p>Lutfen ekipmanlari eksiksiz, pilleri sarj ederek; tripod varsa plate aksami eksiksiz ve kameraya takili olmayacak sekilde teslim edin.</p><hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;"><p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>Your item <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong> is due in about 2 hours.</p><p>Please return all items complete; charge batteries; and if a tripod is included, return the plate complete and not attached to the camera.</p><p>Bilgi Booking</p>');
            sent++;
          }
        }
      }

      // Overdue warning
      if (leftMs < 0) {
        var odDay = Utilities.formatDate(today, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), 'yyyyMMdd');
        var k4 = 'mail_overdue_' + baseKey + '_' + odDay;
        if (!_mailRememberSent(k4)) {
          sendMail(u.email, '[Bilgi Booking] Gecikmis ekipman uyarisi / Overdue equipment warning', '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Sayin ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p><strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong> iade suresi gecmistir. Lutfen en kisa surede depoya teslim ediniz.</p><p><strong>Ceza Kurallari / Penalty Regulations</strong><br>1-30 dakika gecikme: sari uyari.<br>30+ dakika gecikme: sonraki teslim zinciri etkilenirse dogrudan 15 gun aski uygulanabilir; tekrarinda daha agir yaptirimlar uygulanabilir.</p><hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;"><p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Dear ' + (userName || u.name || '') + ',</p><p>The return deadline for <strong>' + eqName + ' (' + eqId + ')</strong> has passed. Please return it to the depot as soon as possible.</p><p><strong>Penalty Regulations</strong><br>1-30 minutes late: yellow warning.<br>30+ minutes late: if it disrupts the next pickup chain, a 15-day suspension may be applied immediately; repeated violations may lead to stricter penalties.</p><p>Bilgi Booking</p>');
          sent++;
        }
      }
    }
    return { ok: true, sent: sent };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

// =================================================================
// 🔄 BLOK 2: checkAdminAccess FONKSİYONUNU DEĞİŞTİRİN
function checkAdminAccess(email) {
  try {
    if (!email) email = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail();
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var stfSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS); // Personel
    var data = stfSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    
    // E-Posta = index 2
    var staffRow = data.find(function(r) { 
      return String(r[2]).trim().toLowerCase() === email.toLowerCase(); 
    });
    
    if (!staffRow) return { allowed: false, name: 'Bilinmiyor', role: 'Yok', isSuperAdmin: false, isIiwPanelOnly: false };
    
    // Personel sheet gerçek yapısı:
    // [0] Kimlik No
    // [1] Ad Soyad
    // [2] E-Posta
    // [5] Yetki (super_admin / technician / iiw_instructor / instructor / 1–5 …)
    // [6] Staff Status (akademik / idari)
    // [7] Fakülte/Birim
    // [8] Bölüm
    // [9] Admin (active / inactive)
    
    var role = String(staffRow[5] || '').trim();           // F sütunu: Yetki
    var adminStatus = String(staffRow[9] || '').trim().toLowerCase(); // J sütunu: Admin
    var rl = role.toLowerCase();
    var isAdmin = (rl === 'super_admin' || rl === 'technician' || rl === 'iiw_instructor' || rl === 'iiw_admin');
    var isActive = (adminStatus === 'active' || adminStatus === 'aktif' || adminStatus === 'admin');
    
    return { 
      allowed: isActive && isAdmin, 
      role: role, 
      name: String(staffRow[1] || 'Admin').trim(),  // B sütunu: Ad Soyad
      isSuperAdmin: rl === 'super_admin',
      isIiwPanelOnly: rl === 'iiw_admin'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { allowed: false, name: 'Hata', role: '', isSuperAdmin: false, isIiwPanelOnly: false };
  }
}

function checkAdminAccessBridge(adminToken) {
  try {
    var u = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!u) {
      return { allowed: false, name: '', role: '', isSuperAdmin: false, isIiwPanelOnly: false };
    }
    var rl = String(u.role || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    return {
      allowed: true,
      name: u.name || 'Admin',
      role: u.role || '',
      isSuperAdmin: rl === 'super_admin',
      isIiwPanelOnly: rl === 'iiw_admin'
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { allowed: false, error: e.message, isSuperAdmin: false, isIiwPanelOnly: false };
  }
}

function getAdminReportsSummaryBridge(testToken) {
  try {
    var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!u || String(u.role || '').toLowerCase() !== 'super_admin') return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var ov = reportsOverdueItems();
    var days = 30;
    var ticketStatus = reportsTicketStatusFunnel_(days);
    return {
      inventory: reportsInventorySummary(),
      overdue: ov || [],
      overdueCount: (ov || []).length,
      windowDays: days,
      tickets: {
        status: ticketStatus,
        byDepartment: reportsTicketDepartmentSummary_(days),
        byType: reportsTicketTypeSummary_(days),
        trend: reportsTicketDailyTrend_(days),
        avgPerDay: Math.round(((ticketStatus.total || 0) / days) * 10) / 10
      },
      studio: reportsStudioUsageSummary_(days),
      equipmentDemand: reportsEquipmentDemandSummary_(days)
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken) {
  var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
  if (!u || String(u.role || '').toLowerCase() !== 'super_admin') return null;
  return u;
}

function _normalizeSpecialAccessStudio_(raw) {
  var s = String(raw || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (s === 'GREEN' || s === 'RED' || s === 'PODCAST' || s === 'DUBBING') return s;
  return '';
}

function _normalizeSpecialAccessUntilForWrite_(raw) {
  var txt = String(raw || '').trim();
  if (!txt) return '';
  if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(txt)) return txt;
  var d = new Date(txt);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) throw new Error('Geçersiz bitiş tarihi.');
  var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul';
  return Utilities.formatDate(d, tz, 'yyyy-MM-dd');
}

function _adminFindUserRowForSpecialAccess_(email) {
  var em = String(email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  if (!em) return null;
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
  var stu = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT);
  if (stu) {
    var lrS = stu.getLastRow();
    if (lrS >= 2) {
      var vS = stu.getRange(2, 1, lrS - 1, 14).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < vS.length; i++) {
        if (String(vS[i][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase() === em) {
          return { kind: 'student', sheet: stu, rowNum: i + 2, name: String(vS[i][1] || '').trim(), email: em };
        }
      }
    }
  }
  var stf = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
  if (stf) {
    var lrP = stf.getLastRow();
    if (lrP >= 2) {
      var vP = stf.getRange(2, 1, lrP - 1, 14).getValues();
      for (var j = 0; j < vP.length; j++) {
        if (String(vP[j][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase() === em) {
          return { kind: 'staff', sheet: stf, rowNum: j + 2, name: String(vP[j][1] || '').trim(), email: em };
        }
      }
    }
  }
  return null;
}

function _normalizeSpecialEquipmentAccessId_(raw) {
  return String(raw || '').trim().toUpperCase();
}

/**
 * Özel ekipman izni: envanter kaynağı (getEquipmentData ile aynı mantık).
 * SUPABASE_READ_ENABLED + dolu liste → yalnızca Supabase.
 * Strict veya boş+strict → sheet yok.
 */
function _inventorySourceForSpecialEquipmentAccess_() {
  if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_()) return { fromSheet: true, rows: null };
  try {
    var invRes = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*', limit: 1000000 });
    var rows = invRes.rows || [];
    if (rows.length) return { fromSheet: false, rows: rows };
    if (_supabaseStrictReadEnabled_()) return { fromSheet: false, rows: [] };
  } catch (_e) {
    if (_supabaseStrictReadEnabled_()) return { fromSheet: false, rows: [] };
  }
  return { fromSheet: true, rows: null };
}

function _isLevel45EquipmentById_(eqId) {
  var target = String(eqId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!target) return false;
  var src = _inventorySourceForSpecialEquipmentAccess_();
  if (!src.fromSheet && src.rows) {
    for (var si = 0; si < src.rows.length; si++) {
      var row = src.rows[si];
      var id = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_id', 'id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (id !== target) continue;
      var st = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (st === 'DELETED' || st === 'HIDDEN' || st === 'DAMAGED') return false;
      var lvlRaw = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['eq_level', 'equipment_level', 'level'], '')).trim();
      var lv = normalizeEquipmentLevelNumeric_(lvlRaw);
      return lv === '4' || lv === '5';
    }
    return false;
  }
  var inv = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)) || [];
  for (var i = 0; i < inv.length; i++) {
    var id2 = String(inv[i].id || inv[i]['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (id2 !== target) continue;
    var st2 = String(inv[i].status || inv[i]['Status'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (st2 === 'DELETED' || st2 === 'HIDDEN' || st2 === 'DAMAGED') return false;
    var rawLv = inventoryEquipmentLevelRawFromObj_(inv[i]);
    var lv2 = normalizeEquipmentLevelNumeric_(rawLv);
    return lv2 === '4' || lv2 === '5';
  }
  return false;
}

function _hasActiveSpecialEquipmentAccessForItem_(user, itemId) {
  if (!user) return false;
  var target = String(itemId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!target) return false;
  var allowedId = _normalizeSpecialEquipmentAccessId_(user.special_equipment_access || '');
  if (!allowedId || allowedId !== target) return false;
  return _isSpecialStudioAccessActiveUntil_(user.special_equipment_access_until || '');
}

function adminSpecialAccessUpsertBridge(testToken, email, studioKeyword, untilDate) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var em = String(email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!em || em.indexOf('@') < 0) return { error: 'Geçerli e-posta gerekli.' };
    var studio = _normalizeSpecialAccessStudio_(studioKeyword);
    if (!studio) return { error: 'Özel izin yalnızca GREEN, RED, PODCAST, DUBBING olabilir.' };
    var untilNorm = _normalizeSpecialAccessUntilForWrite_(untilDate);
    var target = _adminFindUserRowForSpecialAccess_(em);
    if (!target) return { error: 'E-posta Öğrenciler/Personel sayfalarında bulunamadı.' };
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 11).setValue(studio); // K: special_access
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 12).setValue(untilNorm); // L: special_access_until
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { _userCacheDel_(em); } catch (_eC) {}
    audit('admin.special_access.upsert', String(actor.id || actor.email || ''), em, null, {
      kind: target.kind,
      special_access: studio,
      special_access_until: untilNorm
    });
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function adminSpecialAccessListBridge(testToken) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.', list: [] };
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var out = [];
    var eqOut = [];
    function pushFromSheet_(sheetName, kind) {
      var sh = ss.getSheetByName(sheetName);
      if (!sh) return;
      var lr = sh.getLastRow();
      if (lr < 2) return;
      var v = sh.getRange(2, 1, lr - 1, 14).getValues();
      for (var i = 0; i < v.length; i++) {
        var em = String(v[i][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
        var name = String(v[i][1] || '').trim();
        var special = _normalizeSpecialAccessStudio_(v[i][10]);
        var untilRaw = String(v[i][11] || '').trim();
        if (!em || !special) continue;
        var active = true;
        if (untilRaw) {
          var d = new Date(untilRaw);
          if (!isNaN(d.getTime())) {
            d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
            active = d.getTime() >= Date.now();
          } else {
            active = false;
          }
        }
        out.push({
          kind: kind,
          name: name,
          email: em,
          special_access: special,
          special_access_until: untilRaw,
          active: active
        });
        var eqId = _normalizeSpecialEquipmentAccessId_(v[i][12]);
        var eqUntil = String(v[i][13] || '').trim();
        if (em && eqId) {
          var eqActive = true;
          if (eqUntil) {
            var d2 = new Date(eqUntil);
            if (!isNaN(d2.getTime())) {
              d2.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
              eqActive = d2.getTime() >= Date.now();
            } else {
              eqActive = false;
            }
          }
          eqOut.push({
            kind: kind,
            name: name,
            email: em,
            special_equipment_access: eqId,
            special_equipment_access_until: eqUntil,
            active: eqActive
          });
        }
      }
    }
    pushFromSheet_(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT, 'student');
    pushFromSheet_(SHEETS.USERS, 'staff');
    out.sort(function(a, b) {
      var aa = String(a.active) === 'true' ? 0 : 1;
      var bb = String(b.active) === 'true' ? 0 : 1;
      if (aa !== bb) return aa - bb;
      return String(a.email || '').localeCompare(String(b.email || ''));
    });
    return { list: out, equipment_list: eqOut };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e), list: [], equipment_list: [] };
  }
}

function adminSpecialEquipmentAccessUpsertBridge(testToken, email, equipmentId, untilDate) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var em = String(email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!em || em.indexOf('@') < 0) return { error: 'Geçerli e-posta gerekli.' };
    var eqId = _normalizeSpecialEquipmentAccessId_(equipmentId);
    if (!eqId) return { error: 'Ekipman seçimi gerekli.' };
    if (!_isLevel45EquipmentById_(eqId)) return { error: 'Yalnızca seviye 4-5 ekipman seçilebilir.' };
    var untilNorm = _normalizeSpecialAccessUntilForWrite_(untilDate);
    var target = _adminFindUserRowForSpecialAccess_(em);
    if (!target) return { error: 'E-posta Öğrenciler/Personel sayfalarında bulunamadı.' };
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 13).setValue(eqId); // M
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 14).setValue(untilNorm); // N
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { _userCacheDel_(em); } catch (_eC) {}
    audit('admin.special_equipment_access.upsert', String(actor.id || actor.email || ''), em, null, {
      kind: target.kind,
      special_equipment_access: eqId,
      special_equipment_access_until: untilNorm
    });
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function adminSpecialEquipmentAccessDeleteBridge(testToken, email) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var em = String(email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!em) return { error: 'E-posta gerekli.' };
    var target = _adminFindUserRowForSpecialAccess_(em);
    if (!target) return { error: 'Kullanıcı bulunamadı.' };
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 13).setValue('');
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 14).setValue('');
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { _userCacheDel_(em); } catch (_eC2) {}
    audit('admin.special_equipment_access.delete', String(actor.id || actor.email || ''), em, null, { kind: target.kind });
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function adminSpecialEquipmentOptionsBridge(testToken) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.', list: [] };
    var out = [];
    var src = _inventorySourceForSpecialEquipmentAccess_();
    if (!src.fromSheet && src.rows) {
      src.rows.forEach(function(row) {
        var id = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_id', 'id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (!id || isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)) return;
        var st = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (st === 'DELETED' || st === 'HIDDEN' || st === 'DAMAGED') return;
        var lvlRaw = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['eq_level', 'equipment_level', 'level'], 'TEMEL')).trim();
        var lv = normalizeEquipmentLevelNumeric_(lvlRaw);
        if (lv !== '4' && lv !== '5') return;
        var nm = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_name', 'name'], '')).trim() || id;
        out.push({ id: id, name: nm, eq_level: lv });
      });
    } else {
      var inv = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY)) || [];
      inv.forEach(function(i) {
        var id = String(i.id || i['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (!id || isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)) return;
        var st = String(i.status || i['Status'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (st === 'DELETED' || st === 'HIDDEN' || st === 'DAMAGED') return;
        var rawLv = inventoryEquipmentLevelRawFromObj_(i);
        var lv = normalizeEquipmentLevelNumeric_(rawLv);
        if (lv !== '4' && lv !== '5') return;
        out.push({ id: id, name: String(i.name || i['Equipment_Name'] || id).trim(), eq_level: lv });
      });
    }
    out.sort(function(a, b) { return String(a.name || '').localeCompare(String(b.name || '')); });
    return { list: out };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e), list: [] };
  }
}

function adminSpecialAccessDeleteBridge(testToken, email) {
  try {
    var actor = _requireSuperAdminToken_(testToken);
    if (!actor) return { error: 'Sadece super_admin.' };
    var em = String(email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!em) return { error: 'E-posta gerekli.' };
    var target = _adminFindUserRowForSpecialAccess_(em);
    if (!target) return { error: 'Kullanıcı bulunamadı.' };
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 11).setValue('');
    target.sheet.getRange(target.rowNum, 12).setValue('');
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { _userCacheDel_(em); } catch (_eC2) {}
    audit('admin.special_access.delete', String(actor.id || actor.email || ''), em, null, { kind: target.kind });
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}
