    return { list: getIIWTasks() || [] };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function saveIIWHoursAdminBridge(testToken, taskId, studentEmail, hours) {
  try {
    var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!u || !canAccessAdminWeb_(u.role)) return { error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    return saveIIWHours(taskId, studentEmail, hours);
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function getPendingCount(adminToken) {
  try {
    var u = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!u) return 0;
    if (u && isIiwAdminRole_(u.role)) {
      try {
        var stOnly = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['studio_reservations'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
        return stOnly.filter(function(r) {
          return String(r.status || '').toLowerCase() === STATUS.PENDING && _isPodcastStudioByFields_(r.studio_id, r.studio_name);
        }).length;
      } catch (eI) { return 0; }
    }
    var eq = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(_supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_(), { select: 'reservation_group_id,status', status: 'eq.pending', limit: 1000000 }).rows || [];
    var groups = {};
    eq.forEach(function(r) {
      var gid = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['reservation_group_id', 'group_id', 'reservation_id', 'res_id'], '')).trim();
      if (gid) groups[gid] = true;
    });
    var st = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['studio_reservations'], { select: 'id,status', status: 'eq.pending', limit: 1000000 }).rows || [];
    return Object.keys(groups).length + st.length;
  } catch (e) { return 0; }
}

function pendingRequestUserProfile_(userKey) {
  var key = String(userKey || '').trim();
  if (!key) return { profileRoleKind: '', profileLine1: '', profileLine2: '' };
  var u = null;
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
  if (key.indexOf('@') >= 0) {
    u = getUserByEmail(key.toLowerCase());
  } else {
    var stu = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT);
    if (stu) {
      var data = stu.getDataRange().getValues();
      for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][0] || '').trim() === key && data[i][2]) {
          u = getUserByEmail(String(data[i][2]).trim().toLowerCase());
          break;
        }
      }
    }
    if (!u) {
      var stf = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
      if (stf) {
        var d2 = stf.getDataRange().getValues();
        for (var j = 1; j < d2.length; j++) {
          if (String(d2[j][0] || '').trim() === key && d2[j][2]) {
            u = getUserByEmail(String(d2[j][2]).trim().toLowerCase());
            break;
          }
        }
      }
    }
  }
  if (!u) {
    return { profileRoleKind: 'Kayıt eşleşmedi', profileLine1: key, profileLine2: '' };
  }
  if (u.role === 'student') {
    return {
      profileRoleKind: 'Öğrenci',
      profileLine1: (u.department || '-') + ' · ' + (u.bolum || '-'),
      profileLine2: (u.student_no || u.id) + (u.email ? ' · ' + u.email : '')
    };
  }
  var stTr = u.staff_status === 'idari' ? 'İdari personel' : (u.staff_status === 'akademik' ? 'Akademik personel' : 'Personel');
  return {
    profileRoleKind: stTr,
    profileLine1: (u.department || '-') + ' · ' + (u.bolum || '-'),
    profileLine2: u.email || ''
  };
}

/** Öğrenciler / Personel sayfası D sütunu (0-based index 3) — telefon. */
function lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(userKey) {
  var key = String(userKey || '').trim();
  if (!key) return '';
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
  var stu = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT);
  if (stu) {
    var d = stu.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var i = 1; i < d.length; i++) {
      if (String(d[i][0] || '').trim() === key) return String(d[i][3] || '').trim();
      if (String(d[i][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return String(d[i][3] || '').trim();
    }
  }
  var stf = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
  if (stf) {
    var d2 = stf.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (var j = 1; j < d2.length; j++) {
      if (String(d2[j][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase() === key.toLowerCase()) return String(d2[j][3] || '').trim();
      if (String(d2[j][0] || '').trim() === key) return String(d2[j][3] || '').trim();
    }
  }
  return '';
}

function fmtAdminPendingDt_(v) {
  if (v == null || v === '') return '';
  try {
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul';
    if (Object.prototype.toString.call(v) === '[object Date]') {
      if (isNaN(v.getTime())) return String(v);
      return Utilities.formatDate(v, tz, 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm');
    }
    var dt = new Date(v);
    if (!isNaN(dt.getTime())) return Utilities.formatDate(dt, tz, 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm');
    return String(v);
  } catch (e) {
    return String(v);
  }
}

function getPendingRequests(adminToken) {
  try {
    var uGate = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!uGate) return { list: [], duplicateEqWarnings: [], error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    const full = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const colAd = full.length >= 1 ? _reservationSheetColIxs_(full) : { group: 9, status: 7, student: 3, studentName: 4, handover: 5, ret: 6, eqId: 0, name: 1, category: 2, purpose: 10 };
    const hdr = full.length ? full[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); }) : [];
    var pdfCol = -1;
    for (var hi = 0; hi < hdr.length; hi++) {
      if (hdr[hi].indexOf('pdf') >= 0 && (hdr[hi].indexOf('student') >= 0 || hdr[hi].indexOf('document') >= 0)) {
        pdfCol = hi;
        break;
      }
    }
    const data = full.length > 1 ? full.slice(1) : [];
    const pendingRows = data.filter(function(r) { return String(r[colAd.status] || '').trim() === 'Pending'; });
    const grouped = {};
    pendingRows.forEach(r => {
      const resId = String(r[colAd.group] || '').trim();
      if (!resId) return;
      if (!grouped[resId]) {
        grouped[resId] = {
          id: resId,
          kind: 'equipment',
          userName: r[colAd.studentName],
          email: r[colAd.student],
          handoverLabel: '',
          returnLabel: '',
          purpose: String((colAd.purpose >= 0 ? r[colAd.purpose] : '') || ''),
          studentPdfUrl: '',
          items: []
        };
      }
      var hFmt = fmtAdminPendingDt_(r[colAd.handover]);
      var rFmt = fmtAdminPendingDt_(r[colAd.ret]);
      if (hFmt) grouped[resId].handoverLabel = hFmt;
      if (rFmt) grouped[resId].returnLabel = rFmt;
      grouped[resId].items.push({ eqId: r[colAd.eqId], name: r[colAd.name], eqType: String(r[colAd.category] || '') });
      if (!grouped[resId].purpose && colAd.purpose >= 0 && r[colAd.purpose]) grouped[resId].purpose = String(r[colAd.purpose] || '');
      if (pdfCol >= 0 && r[pdfCol]) {
        var pu = String(r[pdfCol]).trim();
        if (pu && (!grouped[resId].studentPdfUrl || grouped[resId].studentPdfUrl.length < pu.length)) grouped[resId].studentPdfUrl = pu;
      }
    });
    var out = Object.values(grouped).map(function(g) {
      var pr = pendingRequestUserProfile_(g.email);
      g.profileRoleKind = pr.profileRoleKind;
      g.profileLine1 = pr.profileLine1;
      g.profileLine2 = pr.profileLine2;
      g.phone = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(String(g.email || '').trim());
      return g;
    });
    try {
      var stRows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
      stRows.filter(function(r) { return String(r.status || '').toLowerCase() === STATUS.PENDING; }).forEach(function(r) {
        var emailDisp = lookupUserEmailById_(r.user_id) || '';
        var purposeParts = [];
        if (r.studio_name) purposeParts.push(String(r.studio_name));
        if (r.request_type) purposeParts.push(String(r.request_type));
        if (r.purpose) purposeParts.push(String(r.purpose));
        try {
          if (r.start_dt && r.end_dt) {
            purposeParts.push(
              Utilities.formatDate(new Date(r.start_dt), 'GMT+3', 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm') +
                ' → ' +
                Utilities.formatDate(new Date(r.end_dt), 'GMT+3', 'dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm')
            );
          }
        } catch (e4) {}
        var g = {
          id: r.id,
          kind: 'studio',
          studio_id: String(r.studio_id || ''),
          studio_name: String(r.studio_name || ''),
          userName: String(r.user_name || ''),
          email: emailDisp,
          handoverLabel: '',
          returnLabel: '',
          phone: '',
          purpose: purposeParts.join(' · '),
          studentPdfUrl: String(r.pdf_url || '').trim(),
          items: [{ eqId: String(r.key_id || 'STUDIO'), name: (String(r.studio_name || 'Stüdyo')) + ' · ' + String(r.key_id || '') + ' (anahtar)' }]
        };
        try {
          if (r.start_dt && r.end_dt) {
            g.handoverLabel = fmtAdminPendingDt_(r.start_dt);
            g.returnLabel = fmtAdminPendingDt_(r.end_dt);
          }
        } catch (eSt) {}
        var pr2 = pendingRequestUserProfile_(r.user_id);
        g.profileRoleKind = pr2.profileRoleKind;
        g.profileLine1 = pr2.profileLine1;
        g.profileLine2 = pr2.profileLine2;
        g.phone = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(String(r.user_id || '').trim()) || (emailDisp ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emailDisp) : '');
        out.push(g);
      });
    } catch (e3) {}

    var eqToRes = {};
    out.forEach(function(g) {
      if (g.kind === 'studio') return;
      (g.items || []).forEach(function(it) {
        var eid = String(it.eqId || '').trim();
        if (!eid) return;
        if (!eqToRes[eid]) eqToRes[eid] = [];
        if (eqToRes[eid].indexOf(g.id) < 0) eqToRes[eid].push(g.id);
      });
    });
    var duplicateEqWarnings = [];
    Object.keys(eqToRes).forEach(function(eid) {
      if (eqToRes[eid].length > 1) duplicateEqWarnings.push({ eqId: eid, reservationIds: eqToRes[eid] });
    });

    if (uGate && isIiwAdminRole_(uGate.role)) {
      out = out.filter(function(x) {
        return x.kind === 'studio' && _isPodcastStudioByFields_(x.studio_id, x.studio_name);
      });
      duplicateEqWarnings = [];
    }

    return { list: out, duplicateEqWarnings: duplicateEqWarnings };
  } catch (e) { return { list: [], duplicateEqWarnings: [], error: e.message }; }
}

function processRequest(resId, action, selectedItemIds, rejectReason, adminToken) {
  try {
    var actor = null;
    var actorEmail = '';
    if (adminToken) {
      actor = resolveCurrentUser(adminToken);
      if (!actor || !canAccessAdminWeb_(actor.role)) {
        throw new Error('Yetkisiz veya oturum geçersiz.');
      }
      actorEmail = String(actor.email || '').trim();
    } else {
      actorEmail = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || '';
      var sessionActor = resolveCurrentUser('');
      if (sessionActor && canAccessAdminWeb_(sessionActor.role)) {
        actor = sessionActor;
        if (!actorEmail) actorEmail = String(sessionActor.email || '').trim();
      }
    }

    var ssReq = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    // Stüdyo kaydı: Supabase-only modda sheet’te satır olmayabilir; findRow yerine canlı listeden ID eşleştir.
    var studioResById = null;
    try {
      studioResById = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) {
        return String(r.id || '').trim() === String(resId || '').trim();
      }) || null;
    } catch (_eStudioLookup) {}
    if (studioResById) {
      if (!actor) {
        throw new Error('Stüdyo onayı için tanınmış admin oturumu gerekli. Ana sayfadan OTP ile giriş yapıp üstteki Admin linkini kullanın; sayfayı ?at= olmadan açtıysanız bir kez yenileyin.');
      }
      if (isIiwAdminRole_(actor.role)) {
        if (!_isPodcastStudioByFields_(studioResById.studio_id, studioResById.studio_name)) {
          throw new Error('IIW Admin yalnız Podcast stüdyo taleplerini onaylayabilir.');
        }
      }
      if (action === 'Approved') {
        var approvedStudio = studioReservationsApprove({ id: resId }, actor);
        return { success: true, studioFormUrl: String(approvedStudio.studio_usage_form_url || '') };
      }
      studioReservationsReject({ id: resId, reason: String(rejectReason || '') }, actor);
      return { success: true };
    }

    if (actor && isIiwAdminRole_(actor.role)) {
      throw new Error('Bu işlem için yetkiniz yok (iiw_admin yalnızca stüdyo onayı).');
    }

    const sheet = ssReq.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colP = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var resIdTrim = String(resId || '').trim();
    var adminRejectNote = String(rejectReason || '').trim();
    var firstUserId = '';
    var firstUserName = '';
    var approvedItems = [];
    var rejectedItems = [];
    
    var existingEqIdSet = {};
    var firstTemplate = null;
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][colP.group] || '').trim() !== resIdTrim) continue;
      if (!firstUserId) firstUserId = String(data[i][colP.student] || '').trim();
      if (!firstUserName) firstUserName = String(data[i][colP.studentName] || '').trim();
      const eqId = String(data[i][colP.eqId] || '').trim();
      if (eqId) existingEqIdSet[eqId] = true;
      if (!firstTemplate) {
        firstTemplate = {
          reservation_group_id: String(data[i][colP.group] || '').trim(),
          student_id: String(data[i][colP.student] || '').trim(),
          student_name: String(data[i][colP.studentName] || '').trim(),
          handover_date: String(data[i][colP.handover] || '').trim(),
          return_date: String(data[i][colP.ret] || '').trim(),
          purpose: String(colP.purpose >= 0 ? (data[i][colP.purpose] || '') : '').trim()
        };
      }
      var dispName = String(data[i][colP.name] || eqId || '').trim();
      if (action === 'Approved') {
        if (selectedItemIds && selectedItemIds.includes(eqId)) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colP.status + 1).setValue('Approved');
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colP.approver + 1).setValue(actorEmail);
          approvedItems.push(dispName || eqId);
        } else {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colP.status + 1).setValue('Rejected (Removed)');
          rejectedItems.push(dispName || eqId);
        }
      } else {
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, colP.status + 1).setValue('Rejected');
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, colP.approver + 1).setValue(actorEmail);
        rejectedItems.push(dispName || eqId);
      }
    }
    if (action === 'Approved' && selectedItemIds && selectedItemIds.length && firstTemplate) {
      var invRows = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY));
      var invById = {};
      for (var ii = 0; ii < invRows.length; ii++) {
        var ir = invRows[ii];
        var iid = String(ir.id || ir['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim();
        if (iid) invById[iid] = ir;
      }
      var toAppend = [];
      for (var si = 0; si < selectedItemIds.length; si++) {
        var selId = String(selectedItemIds[si] || '').trim();
        if (!selId || existingEqIdSet[selId]) continue;
        var inv = invById[selId];
        if (!inv) throw new Error('Ekipman bulunamadı: ' + selId);
        var stInv = String(inv.status || inv['Status'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
        if (stInv === 'MÜSAİT' || stInv === 'UYGUN') stInv = 'AVAILABLE';
        if (stInv !== 'AVAILABLE') throw new Error('Ekipman müsait değil: ' + selId);
        var eqName = String(inv.name || inv['Equipment_Name'] || selId).trim();
        var eqType = String(inv.type_desc || inv['Ekipman Türü'] || '').trim();
        toAppend.push({
          reservation_group_id: firstTemplate.reservation_group_id,
          equipment_id: selId,
          equipment_name: eqName,
          equipment_category: eqType,
          student_id: firstTemplate.student_id,
          student_name: firstTemplate.student_name,
          handover_date: firstTemplate.handover_date,
          return_date: firstTemplate.return_date,
          status: 'Approved',
          approver_email: actorEmail,
          purpose: firstTemplate.purpose,
          created_at: now(),
          updated_at: now()
        });
        approvedItems.push(eqName || selId);
      }
      for (var ta = 0; ta < toAppend.length; ta++) {
        addRow(sheet, toAppend[ta], RESH);
      }
    }
    if (!actorEmail) {
      throw new Error('Onaylayan e-posta bulunamadı. Ana sayfadan admin paneline tekrar girin.');
    }
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(resIdTrim); } catch (_pm) {}
    var u = _mailUserByReservationId(firstUserId);
    if (u.email) {
      if (action === 'Approved') {
        var note = '';
        if (approvedItems.length) note += 'Onaylanan: ' + approvedItems.join(', ') + '. ';
        if (rejectedItems.length) note += 'Reddedilen: ' + rejectedItems.join(', ') + '.';
        sendReservationDecisionMail_(u.email, firstUserName || u.name, String(resId), true, note, '');
      } else {
        var note2 = rejectedItems.length ? ('Kalemler / Items: ' + rejectedItems.join(', ')) : '';
        sendReservationDecisionMail_(u.email, firstUserName || u.name, String(resId), false, note2, adminRejectNote);
      }
    }
    return { success: true };
  } catch(e) { throw new Error(e.message); }
}

function adminPendingLookupInventoryItem(equipmentId, adminToken) {
  try {
    var actor = resolveCurrentUser(adminToken);
    if (!actor || !canAccessAdminWeb_(actor.role)) return { error: 'Unauthorized.' };
    var eqId = String(equipmentId || '').trim();
    if (!eqId) return { error: 'Equipment ID required.' };
    var invRows = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY));
    var row = null;
    for (var i = 0; i < invRows.length; i++) {
      var r = invRows[i];
      if (String(r.id || r['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === eqId.toUpperCase()) { row = r; break; }
    }
    if (!row) return { error: 'Equipment not found.' };
    var st = String(row.status || row['Status'] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
    if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
    return {
      ok: true,
      item: {
        eqId: String(row.id || row['Equipment_ID'] || '').trim(),
        name: String(row.name || row['Equipment_Name'] || '').trim(),
        eqType: String(row.type_desc || row['Ekipman Türü'] || '').trim(),
        status: st
      }
    };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}

function getIIWTasks() {
  try {
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.ASSIGNMENTS);
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues().slice(1);
    return data.filter(r => r[9] === 'pending' || r[9] === 'completed').map(r => ({ id: r[0], studentId: r[1], studentName: r[1], jobDetail: r[3] }));
  } catch(e) { return []; }
}

function saveIIWHours(taskId, studentEmail, hours) {
  try {
    const h = parseFloat(hours);
    if (isNaN(h) || h < 0) return { success: false, error: 'Geçersiz saat.' };
    const em = String(studentEmail || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (!em || em.indexOf('@') < 0) return { success: false, error: 'Geçersiz e-posta.' };
    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT);
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    for (let i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][2] || '').trim().toLowerCase() === em) {
        const current = parseFloat(data[i][9] || 0);
        sheet.getRange(i + 1, 10).setValue(current + h);
        return { success: true, total: current + h };
      }
    }
    return { success: false, error: 'Öğrenci e-postası bulunamadı.' };
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message || String(e) }; }
}



function readInventoryPhysicalFields_(itemId) {
  var out = { locationText: '', responsibleText: '', conditionIn: '', conditionOut: '', rawStatus: '' };
  var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
  var invSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
  var data = invSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  if (data.length < 2) return out;
  var headers = data[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
  var idxId = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('equipment_id') >= 0 || h === 'id' || h.indexOf('ekipman_id') >= 0; });
  if (idxId === -1) idxId = 1;
  var idxLoc = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h === 'location' || h.indexOf('konum') >= 0; });
  if (idxLoc === -1 && headers.length > 11) idxLoc = 11;
  var idxResp = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('responsible') >= 0 || h.indexOf('sorumlu') >= 0; });
  if (idxResp === -1 && headers.length > 17) idxResp = 17;
  var idxCondIn = headers.findIndex(function(h) {
    return h.indexOf('condition_in') >= 0 || (h.indexOf('condition') >= 0 && h.indexOf('in') >= 0) || (h.indexOf('kondisyon') >= 0 && h.indexOf('iade') >= 0);
  });
  var idxCondOut = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('condition_out') >= 0 || (h.indexOf('condition') >= 0 && h.indexOf('out') >= 0); });
  var idxStatus = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('status') >= 0 || h.indexOf('durum') >= 0; });
  var search = String(itemId).trim().toUpperCase();
  for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
    var row = data[i];
    var cellId = String(idxId >= 0 ? row[idxId] : row[1]).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (cellId !== search) continue;
    if (idxLoc >= 0) out.locationText = String(row[idxLoc] || '').trim();
    if (idxResp >= 0) out.responsibleText = String(row[idxResp] || '').trim();
    if (idxCondIn >= 0) out.conditionIn = String(row[idxCondIn] || '').trim();
    if (idxCondOut >= 0) out.conditionOut = String(row[idxCondOut] || '').trim();
    if (idxStatus >= 0) out.rawStatus = String(row[idxStatus] || '').trim();
    return out;
  }
  return out;
}

function normalizeInventoryStatusEnglish_(st) {
  var u = String(st || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (u === 'MÜSAİT' || u === 'UYGUN' || u === 'AVAILABLE') return 'Available';
  if (u.indexOf('DAMAGE') >= 0 || u === 'HASARLI' || u === 'BOZUK') return 'Damaged';
  if (u === 'IN_USE' || u === 'IN USE' || u === 'KULLANIMDA' || u === 'DIŞARIDA' || u === 'DISARIDA' || u === 'TAKEN') return 'In Use';
  if (!u) return 'Unknown';
  return st;
}

function getInventoryDetail(itemId, adminToken) {
  return _legacyBridgeDisabled_('getInventoryDetail');
}

function adminCheckItemAvailabilityBridge(itemId, startIso, endIso, testToken) {
  try {
    var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!u || !canAccessAdminWeb_(u.role)) return { error: 'Unauthorized.' };
    var av = reservationsCheckAvailability({ item_id: String(itemId || '').trim(), start_dt: startIso, end_dt: endIso });
    return { available: !!av.available, conflict: av.conflict || null };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function adminUpdateInventoryMetaBridge(itemId, payload, testToken) {
  return _legacyBridgeDisabled_('adminUpdateInventoryMetaBridge');
}

// =================================================================
// 🔄 GÜNCELLENMİŞ TRAFİK VE PDF MOTORU (KESİN ÇÖZÜM)
// =================================================================

/** Günlük trafik: stüdyo anahtarı teslim (approved + teslim günü) / iade (checked_out + bitiş günü). */
function getStudioTrafficForDate_(dateStr) {
  var targetDate = new Date(dateStr).toDateString();
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
  var out = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    var r = rows[i];
    var st = normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(r.status);
    if (st === STATUS.CANCELLED || st === STATUS.REJECTED || st === STATUS.PENDING || isStudioReturnedStatus_(st)) continue;
    var pickupDay;
    try {
      pickupDay = r.key_pickup_dt ? new Date(r.key_pickup_dt).toDateString() : new Date(r.start_dt).toDateString();
    } catch (e) {
      continue;
    }
    var endDay;
    try {
      endDay = new Date(r.end_dt).toDateString();
    } catch (e2) {
      continue;
    }
    if (st === STATUS.APPROVED && pickupDay === targetDate) {
      var pdt = r.key_pickup_dt || r.start_dt;
      var uidS = String(r.user_id || '').trim();
      var emS = lookupUserEmailById_(r.user_id) || '';
      var phS = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(uidS) || (emS ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emS) : '');
      var sidPick = '';
      try {
        if (emS) {
          var uPick = getUserByEmail(String(emS).toLowerCase());
          if (uPick && uPick.student_no) sidPick = String(uPick.student_no).trim();
        }
      } catch (eSidP) {}
      out.push({
        kind: 'studio',
        id: r.id,
        userName: r.user_name || '',
        email: emS,
        phone: phS,
        studentId: sidPick,
        purpose: String(r.purpose || '').trim(),
        handoverLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(pdt),
        returnLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(r.end_dt),
        type: 'pickup',
        time: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(pdt), 'GMT+3', 'HH:mm'),
        items: [{ id: r.key_id, name: (r.studio_name || 'Stüdyo') + ' · ' + r.key_id, invStatus: 'AVAILABLE', kind: 'studio_key' }]
      });
      continue;
    }
    if (isStudioCheckedOutStatus_(st) && endDay === targetDate) {
      var uidR = String(r.user_id || '').trim();
      var emR = lookupUserEmailById_(r.user_id) || '';
      var phR = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(uidR) || (emR ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emR) : '');
      var sidRet = '';
      try {
        if (emR) {
          var uRet = getUserByEmail(String(emR).toLowerCase());
          if (uRet && uRet.student_no) sidRet = String(uRet.student_no).trim();
        }
      } catch (eSidR) {}
      out.push({
        kind: 'studio',
        id: r.id,
        userName: r.user_name || '',
        email: emR,
        phone: phR,
        studentId: sidRet,
        purpose: String(r.purpose || '').trim(),
        handoverLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(r.key_pickup_dt || r.start_dt),
        returnLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(r.end_dt),
        type: 'return',
        time: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(r.end_dt), 'GMT+3', 'HH:mm'),
        items: [{ id: r.key_id, name: (r.studio_name || 'Stüdyo') + ' · ' + r.key_id, invStatus: 'IN_USE', kind: 'studio_key' }]
      });
    }
  }
  return out;
}

function _isPodcastStudioTrafficRow_(r) {
  var sid = String((r && r.studio_id) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (sid === 'PODCAST') return true;
  var sn = String((r && r.studio_name) || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  return sn.indexOf('PODCAST') >= 0;
}

function getTrafficData(dateStr, adminToken) {
  var t0Traffic = Date.now();
  try {
    var adminUser = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!adminUser) return [];
    var iiwOnlyTraffic = !!(adminUser && isIiwAdminRole_(adminUser.role));
    var kTraffic = _cacheKey_('trafficData', [String(dateStr || ''), iiwOnlyTraffic ? 'iiw' : 'full', 'v1']);
    var cTraffic = _cacheGetJson_(kTraffic);
    if (cTraffic) {
      _debugSourceLog_('getTrafficData', 'cache', t0Traffic, { date: String(dateStr || '') });
      return cTraffic;
    }
    const invRows = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
    const invStatusMap = {};
    invRows.forEach(function(r) {
      var id = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['id', 'equipment_id'], '')).trim();
      var status = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (id) invStatusMap[id] = status;
    });

    const resData = _supaSelectAllEquipmentReservationLines_().rows || [];
    const targetDate = new Date(dateStr).toDateString();
    const groupedTraffic = {};

    resData.forEach(function(r) {
      const startIso = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '') || '');
      const endIso = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '') || '');
      const start = startIso ? new Date(startIso).toDateString() : '';
      const end = endIso ? new Date(endIso).toDateString() : '';
      const resId = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['reservation_group_id', 'group_id', 'reservation_id', 'res_id', 'id'], '')).trim();
      const status = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim();
      const eqId = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim();

      // MANTIK: Onaylıları (Approved) çıkışa, Çıkış yapılanları (Picked Up) iadeye koy.
      let isPickup = (start === targetDate && status === "Approved");
      let isReturn = (end === targetDate && status === "Picked Up");

      if (isPickup || isReturn) {
        var gk = String(resId) + '|' + (isPickup ? 'pickup' : 'return');
        if (!groupedTraffic[gk]) {
          var custKey = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_id', 'user_id'], '')).trim();
          var luT = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(custKey);
          var emailDisp = (luT && luT.ok && luT.email) ? String(luT.email).trim() : (custKey.indexOf('@') >= 0 ? custKey : '');
          var phoneT = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(custKey) || (emailDisp ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emailDisp) : '');
          groupedTraffic[gk] = {
            id: resId,
            userName: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_name', 'user_name'], '') || ''),
            email: emailDisp || custKey,
            phone: phoneT,
            studentId: custKey,
            handoverLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(startIso),
            returnLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(endIso),
            type: isPickup ? 'pickup' : 'return',
            time: startIso ? Utilities.formatDate(new Date(startIso), "GMT+3", "HH:mm") : '',
            items: []
          };
        }
        
        let currentInvStatus = invStatusMap[eqId] || 'UNKNOWN';
        if(currentInvStatus === 'MÜSAİT' || currentInvStatus === 'UYGUN') currentInvStatus = 'AVAILABLE';
        if(currentInvStatus === 'KULLANIMDA' || currentInvStatus === 'DIŞARIDA') currentInvStatus = 'IN_USE';

        groupedTraffic[gk].items.push({ id: eqId, name: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_name', 'item_name', 'name'], '') || eqId), invStatus: currentInvStatus });
      }
    });
    var eqList = Object.values(groupedTraffic);
    var stList = [];
    try {
      stList = getStudioTrafficForDate_(dateStr);
    } catch (e2) {
      stList = [];
    }
    if (iiwOnlyTraffic) {
      // IIW admin paneli: sadece Podcast stüdyo anahtar teslim/iade trafiği.
      stList = (stList || []).filter(function(x) { return _isPodcastStudioTrafficRow_(x); });
      eqList = [];
    }
    var out = eqList.concat(stList);
    _cachePutJson_(kTraffic, out, 12);
    _debugSourceLog_('getTrafficData', 'supabase-only', t0Traffic, { date: String(dateStr || ''), count: out.length });
    return out;
  } catch (e) { return []; }
}

function getTrafficDataByNameOrStudent(query, adminToken) {
  var t0TrafficQ = Date.now();
  try {
    var adminUser = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!adminUser) return [];
    var q = String(query || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!q || q.length < 2) return [];
    var iiwOnlyTraffic = !!(adminUser && isIiwAdminRole_(adminUser.role));
    var kTrafficQ = _cacheKey_('trafficDataQuery', [q, iiwOnlyTraffic ? 'iiw' : 'full', 'v1']);
    var cTrafficQ = _cacheGetJson_(kTrafficQ);
    if (cTrafficQ) {
      _debugSourceLog_('getTrafficDataByNameOrStudent', 'cache', t0TrafficQ, { q: q, count: cTrafficQ.length || 0 });
      return cTrafficQ;
    }

    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var resSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var resFullTf = resSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colTf = resFullTf.length >= 1 ? _reservationSheetColIxs_(resFullTf) : { group: 9, status: 7, student: 3, studentName: 4, handover: 5, ret: 6, eqId: 0, name: 1 };
    var resData = resFullTf.slice(1);

    var invSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    var invData = invSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var invHeaders = invData[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var idxInvID = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes('equipment_id') || h === 'id' || h.includes('ekipman_id'); });
    var idxInvStatus = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes('status') || h.includes('durum'); });
    var invStatusMap = {};
    for (var iInv = 1; iInv < invData.length; iInv++) {
      var iid = idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[iInv][idxInvID] : invData[iInv][1];
      var ist = idxInvStatus !== -1 ? invData[iInv][idxInvStatus] : invData[iInv][4];
      if (iid) invStatusMap[String(iid).trim()] = String(ist).trim().toUpperCase();
    }

    var groupedTraffic = {};
    resData.forEach(function(r) {
      var status = String(r[colTf.status] || '').trim();
      var isPickup = (status === 'Approved');
      var isReturn = (status === 'Picked Up');
      if (!isPickup && !isReturn) return;

      var studentId = String(r[colTf.student] || '').trim();
      var studentName = String(r[colTf.studentName] || '').trim();
      var hay = (studentName + ' ' + studentId).toLowerCase();
      if (hay.indexOf(q) === -1) return;

      var resId = String(r[colTf.group] || '').trim();
      var eqId = String(r[colTf.eqId] || '').trim();
      if (!resId || !eqId) return;

      var gk = resId + '|' + (isPickup ? 'pickup' : 'return');
      if (!groupedTraffic[gk]) {
        var custKey = studentId;
        var luT = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(custKey);
        var emailDisp = (luT && luT.ok && luT.email) ? String(luT.email).trim() : (custKey.indexOf('@') >= 0 ? custKey : '');
        var phoneT = lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(custKey) || (emailDisp ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emailDisp) : '');
        groupedTraffic[gk] = {
          id: resId,
          userName: studentName,
          email: emailDisp || custKey,
          phone: phoneT,
          studentId: studentId,
          handoverLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(r[colTf.handover]),
          returnLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(r[colTf.ret]),
          type: isPickup ? 'pickup' : 'return',
          time: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(isPickup ? r[colTf.handover] : r[colTf.ret]), 'GMT+3', 'HH:mm'),
          items: []
        };
      }

      var currentInvStatus = invStatusMap[eqId] || 'UNKNOWN';
      if (currentInvStatus === 'MÜSAİT' || currentInvStatus === 'UYGUN') currentInvStatus = 'AVAILABLE';
      if (currentInvStatus === 'KULLANIMDA' || currentInvStatus === 'DIŞARIDA') currentInvStatus = 'IN_USE';
      groupedTraffic[gk].items.push({ id: eqId, name: r[colTf.name], invStatus: currentInvStatus });
    });

    var out = Object.values(groupedTraffic);
    if (iiwOnlyTraffic) {
      out = [];
      try {
        var stRows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
        for (var si = 0; si < stRows.length; si++) {
          var rs = stRows[si];
          if (!_isPodcastStudioTrafficRow_(rs)) continue;
          var st = normalizeStudioStatusForDb_(rs.status);
          var isPickupS = (st === STATUS.APPROVED);
          var isReturnS = isStudioCheckedOutStatus_(st);
          if (!isPickupS && !isReturnS) continue;
          var uidS = String(rs.user_id || '').trim();
          var emS = lookupUserEmailById_(uidS) || '';
          var sidS = '';
          try {
            if (emS) {
              var uPick = getUserByEmail(String(emS).toLowerCase());
              if (uPick && uPick.student_no) sidS = String(uPick.student_no).trim();
            }
          } catch (_eSidS) {}
          var keyText = [
            String(rs.user_name || ''),
            String(uidS || ''),
            String(sidS || ''),
            String(emS || ''),
            String(rs.studio_name || ''),
            String(rs.key_id || '')
          ].join(' ').toLowerCase();
          if (keyText.indexOf(q) === -1) continue;
          out.push({
            kind: 'studio',
            id: rs.id,
            userName: rs.user_name || '',
            email: emS,
            phone: lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(uidS) || (emS ? lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(emS) : ''),
            studentId: sidS,
            handoverLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(rs.key_pickup_dt || rs.start_dt),
            returnLabel: fmtAdminPendingDt_(rs.end_dt),
            type: isPickupS ? 'pickup' : 'return',
            time: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(isPickupS ? (rs.key_pickup_dt || rs.start_dt) : rs.end_dt), 'GMT+3', 'HH:mm'),
            items: [{ id: rs.key_id, name: (rs.studio_name || 'Stüdyo') + ' · ' + rs.key_id, invStatus: isPickupS ? 'AVAILABLE' : 'IN_USE', kind: 'studio_key' }]
          });
        }
      } catch (_eStSearch) {}
    }
    out.sort(function(a, b) {
      var an = String(a.userName || '').toLowerCase();
      var bn = String(b.userName || '').toLowerCase();
      if (an !== bn) return an.localeCompare(bn);
      return String(a.id || '').localeCompare(String(b.id || ''));
    });
    _cachePutJson_(kTrafficQ, out, 20);
    _debugSourceLog_('getTrafficDataByNameOrStudent', 'sheet', t0TrafficQ, { q: q, count: out.length || 0 });
    return out;
  } catch (e) {
    return [];
  }
}

function adminStudioGenerateUsagePdfOnly_(resId, itemIds, studioHandoverNote) {
  var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
  var row = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i].id) === String(resId)) { row = rows[i]; break; }
  }
  if (!row) throw new Error('Kayıt bulunamadı.');
  if (String(row.status).toLowerCase() !== STATUS.APPROVED) throw new Error('Form yalnızca onaylı stüdyo rezervasyonları için basılır.');
  var kid = String(row.key_id || '').trim();
  var ok = false;
  var ids = itemIds || [];
  for (var j = 0; j < ids.length; j++) {
    if (String(ids[j]).trim() === kid) { ok = true; break; }
  }
  if (!ok) throw new Error('Anahtar seçimi eşleşmedi.');
  var pdfUrl = generateDeliveryPDF(CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID, buildStudioUsageFormMergeData_(row, studioHandoverNote));
  return { success: true, url: pdfUrl };
}

function adminStudioProcessKeyHandover_(resId, itemIds, studioHandoverNote) {
  var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  var rn = findRow(sheet, resId);
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
  var row = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i].id) === String(resId)) { row = rows[i]; break; }
  }
  if (!row) throw new Error('Kayıt bulunamadı.');
  if (String(row.status).toLowerCase() !== STATUS.APPROVED) throw new Error('Sadece onaylı rezervasyonlarda anahtar teslim edilebilir.');
  var kid = String(row.key_id || '').trim();
  var ok = false;
  var ids = itemIds || [];
  for (var j = 0; j < ids.length; j++) {
    if (String(ids[j]).trim() === kid) { ok = true; break; }
  }
  if (!ok) throw new Error('Anahtar seçimi eşleşmedi.');
  var pdfUrl = generateDeliveryPDF(CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID, buildStudioUsageFormMergeData_(row, studioHandoverNote));
  var up = Object.assign({}, row, {
    status: STUDIO_STATUS_CHECKED_OUT,
    studio_handover_note: studioHandoverNote,
    studio_usage_form_url: pdfUrl,
    updated_at: now()
  });
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(up);
  } else {
    if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Kayıt bulunamadı.');
    setRow(sheet, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
    trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  }
  try {
    mailDeliveryPdfCopyToBorrower_(row.user_id || '', row.user_name || '', pdfUrl, 'Stüdyo teslim formu', {
      resId: row.id || '',
      handoverDate: row.start_dt || '',
      returnDate: row.end_dt || ''
    });
  } catch (_eMailStudio) {}
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  return { success: true, url: pdfUrl };
}

function adminStudioProcessKeyReturn_(resId, itemIds, returnNote) {
  var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.STUDIO_RES);
  var rn = findRow(sheet, resId);
  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_();
  var row = null;
  for (var i = 0; i < rows.length; i++) {
    if (String(rows[i].id) === String(resId)) { row = rows[i]; break; }
  }
  if (!row) throw new Error('Kayıt bulunamadı.');
  if (!isStudioCheckedOutStatus_(row.status)) throw new Error('Anahtar henüz teslim edilmemiş veya zaten iade alınmış.');
  var kid = String(row.key_id || '').trim();
  var ok = false;
  var ids = itemIds || [];
  for (var j = 0; j < ids.length; j++) {
    if (String(ids[j]).trim() === kid) { ok = true; break; }
  }
  if (!ok) throw new Error('Anahtar seçimi eşleşmedi.');
  var up = Object.assign({}, row, {
    status: STUDIO_STATUS_RETURNED,
    return_handover_note: returnNote,
    updated_at: now()
  });
  if (_supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()) {
    _upsertStudioReservationDirect_(up);
  } else {
    if (rn === -1) throw new Error('Kayıt bulunamadı.');
    setRow(sheet, rn, studioSheetRowFromCanonical_(up), SRSH);
    trySupabaseMirrorStudioRow_(up);
  }
  SpreadsheetApp.flush();
  return { success: true };
}


var ADMIN_RETURN_EQUIP_CONDITIONS_ = ['Excellent', 'Minor Scratch', 'Damaged'];
var ADMIN_RETURN_STUDIO_NOTES_ = [
  'Sorunsuz-No Issues',
  'Duzensiz-Disorganized',
  'Eksik Ekipman-Missing Equipment',
  'Hasarli Alan-Needs Repair',
  'Kullanilamaz Durumda-Damaged Area',
  // Backward compatibility for older rows/UI labels
  'Studio Clean',
  'Studio Disorganized',
  'Studio Equipment Damaged',
  'Studio Facility Damaged'
];

function adminProcessPartialCheckin(resId, itemIds, handoverStatus, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) throw new Error('Yetkisiz.');
    var statusStr = handoverStatus != null ? String(handoverStatus).trim() : '';
    if (!statusStr) throw new Error('İade teslim durumu seçilmelidir.');
    var ss0 = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var studioRow0 = null;
    try {
      studioRow0 = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) {
        return String(r.id || '').trim() === String(resId || '').trim();
      }) || null;
    } catch (_eSt0) {}
    if (studioRow0) {
      if (ADMIN_RETURN_STUDIO_NOTES_.indexOf(statusStr) < 0) {
        throw new Error('Stüdyo anahtar iadesi için geçerli teslim durumu seçin.');
      }
      return adminStudioProcessKeyReturn_(resId, itemIds, statusStr);
    }
    if (ADMIN_RETURN_EQUIP_CONDITIONS_.indexOf(statusStr) < 0) {
      throw new Error('Ekipman iadesi için: Excellent / Minor Scratch / Damaged seçin.');
    }
    const ss = ss0;
    const resSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    const invSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    
    const resData = resSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colRetSt = _reservationSheetColIxs_(resData);
    const invData = invSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    const invHeaders = invData[0].map(h => String(h).trim().toLowerCase());
    const idxInvID = invHeaders.findIndex(h => h.includes("equipment_id") || h === "id" || h.includes("ekipman_id"));
    const idxInvStatus = invHeaders.findIndex(h => h.includes("status") || h.includes("durum"));
    var idxCondIn = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) {
      return h.indexOf('condition_in') >= 0 || (h.indexOf('condition') >= 0 && h.indexOf('in') >= 0 && h.indexOf('out') < 0);
    });
    if (idxCondIn < 0) {
      idxCondIn = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('kondisyon') >= 0 && (h.indexOf('iade') >= 0 || h.indexOf('giriş') >= 0 || h.indexOf('giris') >= 0); });
    }
    var resIdTrimCi = String(resId || '').trim();
    var resIdUpCi = resIdTrimCi.toUpperCase();

    itemIds.forEach(itemId => {
       var itemUpCi = String(itemId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
       // 1. Rezervasyonu "Returned" yap (Listeden düşer)
       for(let i=1; i<resData.length; i++) {
         if(String(resData[i][colRetSt.group]).trim().toUpperCase() === resIdUpCi && String(resData[i][colRetSt.eqId]).trim().toUpperCase() === itemUpCi) {
           resSheet.getRange(i+1, colRetSt.status + 1).setValue("Returned");
         }
       }
       // 2. Envanteri "AVAILABLE" yap + Condition In
       for(let i=1; i<invData.length; i++) {
         let currentId = idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[i][idxInvID] : invData[i][1];
         if(String(currentId || '').trim().toUpperCase() === itemUpCi) {
            let sCol = idxInvStatus !== -1 ? idxInvStatus + 1 : 5;
            let cell = invSheet.getRange(i+1, sCol);
            cell.clearDataValidations();
            cell.setValue("AVAILABLE");
            if (idxCondIn >= 0) {
              invSheet.getRange(i+1, idxCondIn+1).setValue(statusStr);
            }
            try { trySupabaseMirrorInventorySheetRow_(i + 1); } catch (_eInvMirrorRet) {}
         }
       }
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(resIdTrimCi); } catch (_eRet) {}
    return { success: true };
  } catch(e) { throw new Error(e.message); }
}

/** Tekrar bitiş: yyyy-MM-dd veya ISO; o günün sonu (yerel) dahil kabul edilir. */
function adminParseRepeatEndInclusive_(raw) {
  var s = String(raw || '').trim();
  if (!s) return null;
  var m = s.match(/^(\d{4})-(\d{2})-(\d{2})/);
  if (m) {
    var y = parseInt(m[1], 10), mo = parseInt(m[2], 10) - 1, day = parseInt(m[3], 10);
    if (isNaN(y) || isNaN(mo) || isNaN(day)) return null;
    return new Date(y, mo, day, 23, 59, 59, 999);
  }
  var d = new Date(s);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return null;
  d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  return d;
}

function adminCreateStudioReservation(payload, adminToken) {
  var adminActor = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
  if (!adminActor) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
  var emailNorm = String(payload.email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  var userNameFromEmail = String(emailNorm.split('@')[0] || '').trim();
  var user = { id: emailNorm, name: userNameFromEmail, role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN, email: emailNorm };
  try {
    var foundUser = getUserByEmail(emailNorm);
    if (foundUser) {
      user = {
        id: String(foundUser.student_no || foundUser.id || emailNorm).trim(),
        name: String(foundUser.name || userNameFromEmail || emailNorm).trim(),
        role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN,
        email: emailNorm
      };
    }
  } catch (_eLookupUser) {}
  
  var results = [];
  var errors = [];
  var currentStart = new Date(payload.start_dt);
  var currentEnd = new Date(payload.end_dt);
  if (isNaN(currentStart.getTime()) || isNaN(currentEnd.getTime())) return { success: false, error: 'Geçersiz tarih.' };
  if (currentEnd.getTime() <= currentStart.getTime()) return { success: false, error: 'Bitiş saati başlangıçtan sonra olmalı.' };
  var period = String(payload.period || 'once');
  var withEquipment = !!payload.with_equipment;
  var equipmentIds = (payload.equipment_ids || []).map(function(x) { return String(x || '').trim(); }).filter(function(x) { return !!x; });
  var invMap = {};
  if (withEquipment) {
    var inv = _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_();
    for (var ii = 0; ii < inv.length; ii++) {
      invMap[String(inv[ii].id || '').trim()] = inv[ii];
    }
  }
  var endPeriod = null;
  if (period !== 'once') {
    endPeriod = adminParseRepeatEndInclusive_(payload.end_period_dt);
    if (!endPeriod) return { success: false, error: 'Tekrarlı rezervasyonda tekrar bitiş tarihi zorunlu.' };
    if (endPeriod.getTime() < currentStart.getTime()) return { success: false, error: 'Tekrar bitiş tarihi başlangıçtan önce olamaz.' };
  }
  var guard = 0;
  var eqCreated = 0;
  var skippedHolidayDates = [];
  var actorEmail = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || 'admin';
  var resSheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  while (true) {
    guard++;
    if (guard > 400) return { success: false, error: 'Tekrar limiti aşıldı (400).' };
    var hInfo = _holidayConflictInfo_(currentStart, currentEnd);
    if (hInfo.blocked) {
      if (period === 'once') {
        return { success: false, error: 'Resmi tatilde stüdyo teslim/iade yapılamaz: ' + hInfo.dates.join(', ') };
      }
      skippedHolidayDates.push(_ymdInTz_(currentStart));
    } else {
    try {
      var p = {
        studio_id: payload.studio_id,
        start_dt: currentStart.toISOString(),
        end_dt: currentEnd.toISOString(),
        purpose: String(payload.purpose || ''),
        pdf_url: 'ADMIN_RESERVATION',
        request_type: String(payload.request_type || '').trim(),
        admin_approved_by: String(adminActor.id || adminActor.email || Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || 'admin_web').trim(),
        _bookdeck_admin_direct_studio: true
      };
      results.push(studioReservationsCreate(p, user));
      if (withEquipment && equipmentIds.length) {
        var eqGroupId = 'RES-ADM-ST-' + Utilities.getUuid().substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
        var sStr = Utilities.formatDate(currentStart, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm");
        var eStr = Utilities.formatDate(currentEnd, Session.getScriptTimeZone(), "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm");
        var eqRows = [];
        for (var ei = 0; ei < equipmentIds.length; ei++) {
          var eid = equipmentIds[ei];
          var av = reservationsCheckAvailability({ item_id: eid, start_dt: sStr, end_dt: eStr });
          if (!av || !av.available) {
            errors.push('Ekipman çakışması (' + eid + ') - ' + currentStart.toLocaleDateString('tr-TR'));
            continue;
          }
          var it = invMap[eid] || {};
          var tsBund = now();
          var eqPayload = {
            reservation_group_id: eqGroupId,
            equipment_id: eid,
            equipment_name: String(it.name || ''),
            equipment_category: String(it.type || it.type_desc || ''),
            student_id: String(payload.email || ''),
            student_name: String(user.name || ''),
            handover_date: sStr,
            return_date: eStr,
            status: 'Approved',
            approver_email: actorEmail,
            purpose: 'Studio bundled equipment',
            created_at: tsBund,
            updated_at: tsBund
          };
          eqRows.push(eqPayload);
          try { addRow(resSheet, eqPayload, RESH); } catch (_sheetBundledErr) {}
        }
        if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_() && eqRows.length) {
          _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsPrimary_(eqRows);
        } else {
          for (var em = 0; em < eqRows.length; em++) trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_(eqRows[em]);
        }
        eqCreated += eqRows.length;
      }
    } catch(e) {
      errors.push('Tarih ' + currentStart.toLocaleDateString('tr-TR') + ': ' + e.message);
    }
    }
    if (period === 'once') break;
    
    if (period === 'daily') {
      currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 1);
      currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 1);
      // Hafta sonunu atla
      if (currentStart.getDay() === 6) { currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 2); currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 2); }
      if (currentStart.getDay() === 0) { currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 1); currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 1); }
    } else if (period === 'weekly') {
      currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 7);
      currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 7);
    } else if (period === 'monthly') {
      currentStart.setMonth(currentStart.getMonth() + 1);
      currentEnd.setMonth(currentEnd.getMonth() + 1);
    } else {
      return { success: false, error: 'Geçersiz period.' };
    }
    if (endPeriod && currentStart.getTime() > endPeriod.getTime()) break;
  }
  
  var response = { success: true, count: results.length };
  if (withEquipment) response.equipmentCount = eqCreated;
  if (errors.length) response.warnings = errors.join(' | ');
  if (skippedHolidayDates.length) {
    var uniq = Array.from(new Set(skippedHolidayDates)).sort();
    response.skipped_holiday_dates = uniq;
    response.warnings = (response.warnings ? (response.warnings + ' | ') : '') + ('Resmi tatil nedeniyle atlandı: ' + uniq.join(', '));
  }
  return response;
}

function getStudioData(testToken) {
  var baseList;
  if (testToken === undefined || testToken === null || testToken === '') {
    baseList = Object.values(STUDIOS).map(function(s) {
      return { id: s.id, name: s.name, weekendOk: s.weekendOk, keyCount: s.keyCount, formUrl: 'https://docs.google.com/document/d/' + CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID };
    });
  } else {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return [];
    baseList = studiosListForUser(user);
  }
  var isUserSession = !!(testToken !== undefined && testToken !== null && String(testToken).trim() !== '');
  return baseList.map(function(s) {
    var embedUrl = buildStudioCalendarEmbedUrl(s.id);
    return {
      id: s.id,
      name: s.name,
      weekendOk: !!s.weekendOk,
      desc: s.name + ' — Google Calendar',
      image: STUDIO_CARD_IMAGES[s.id] || ('https://via.placeholder.com/1200x600?text=' + encodeURIComponent(s.name)),
      calendarUrl: embedUrl,
      // Always prefer native Google Calendar iframe (month/week/day controls + real-time sync).
      calendarBusyOnly: false
    };
  });
}

/**
 * BRIDGE 5: Admin Onay (admin arayüzü doğrudan processRequest kullanır; jeton zorunlu.)
 */
function approveReservation(resId, adminToken) {
  return processRequest(resId, 'Approved', null, '', adminToken);
}

/**
 * BRIDGE 6: Admin Red
 */
function rejectReservation(resId, adminToken) {
  return processRequest(resId, 'Rejected', null, '', adminToken);
}

/** Supabase’ten admin rezervasyon geçmişi (ekipman satırları); kapalıysa null. */
function tryGetAdminReservationHistoryFromSupabase_() {
  if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_()) return null;
  function toIso_(v) {
    if (v === '' || v === null || v === undefined) return '';
    var d = new Date(v);
    if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return '';
    return d.toISOString();
  }
  var resRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(_supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_(), { select: '*' }).rows || [];
  var out = [];
  for (var i = 0; i < resRows.length; i++) {
    var r = resRows[i];
    var eqId = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim();
    if (!eqId) continue;
    var handover = supaRowPick_(r, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '');
    var ret = supaRowPick_(r, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '');
    out.push({
      eqId: eqId,
      eqName: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_name', 'item_name', 'name'], '')).trim(),
      userId: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_id', 'user_id'], '')).trim(),
      userName: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_name', 'user_name'], '')).trim(),
      startDt: toIso_(handover),
      endDt: toIso_(ret),
      status: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim(),
      resId: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['reservation_group_id', 'res_id', 'reservation_id', 'id'], '')).trim()
    });
  }
  out.sort(function(a, b) {
    return new Date(b.startDt || 0) - new Date(a.startDt || 0);
  });
  return out.slice(0, 200);
}

/**
 * BRIDGE 7: Admin Geçmiş Tablosu
 */
function getAdminReservationHistory(adminToken) {
  var t0Hist = Date.now();
  try {
    var adminUser = requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken);
    if (!adminUser) return [];
    var kHist = _cacheKey_('adminResHistory', ['v1']);
    var cHist = _cacheGetJson_(kHist);
    if (cHist) {
      _debugSourceLog_('getAdminReservationHistory', 'cache', t0Hist, { count: cHist.length || 0 });
      return cHist;
    }
    try {
      var sbHist = tryGetAdminReservationHistoryFromSupabase_();
      if (sbHist != null) {
        if (_supabaseStrictReadEnabled_()) {
          _cachePutJson_(kHist, sbHist, 20);
          _debugSourceLog_('getAdminReservationHistory', 'supabase-strict', t0Hist, { count: sbHist.length || 0 });
          return sbHist;
        }
        if (!sbHist.length && !_allowEmptySupabaseRead_()) {
          _debugSourceLog_('getAdminReservationHistory', 'supabase-empty-fallback-sheet', t0Hist, {});
        } else {
          _cachePutJson_(kHist, sbHist, 20);
          _debugSourceLog_('getAdminReservationHistory', 'supabase', t0Hist, { count: sbHist.length });
          return sbHist;
        }
      }
    } catch (_sbAdmHist) {}

    const sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    const data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return [];
    var colHist = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    
    var out = data.slice(1)
      .filter(r => r[colHist.eqId])
      .map(r => ({
        eqId:     String(r[colHist.eqId] || ''),
        eqName:   String(r[colHist.name] || ''),
        userId:   String(r[colHist.student] || ''),
        userName: String(r[colHist.studentName] || ''),
        startDt:  r[colHist.handover] ? new Date(r[colHist.handover]).toISOString() : '',
        endDt:    r[colHist.ret] ? new Date(r[colHist.ret]).toISOString() : '',
        status:   String(r[colHist.status] || ''),
        resId:    String(r[colHist.group] || '')
      }))
      .reverse()
      .slice(0, 200);
    _cachePutJson_(kHist, out, 20);
    _debugSourceLog_('getAdminReservationHistory', 'sheet', t0Hist, { count: out.length });
    return out;
  } catch(e) {
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Web istemcisi / dağıtım kontrolü: Apps Script editöründe bu fonksiyonu çalıştırıp
 * { ok: true, ... } döndüğünü doğrulayın. Tarayıcıda takılı kalıyorsa önce burayı test edin.
 */
function bookdeckClientPing() {
  try {
    var recaptcha = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('RECAPTCHA_SITE_KEY') ? true : false;
    return { ok: true, otpMode: true, recaptchaConfigured: recaptcha };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

function _otpHash(email, code) {
  var raw = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim() + '|' + String(code || '').trim();
  var dig = Utilities.computeDigest(Utilities.DigestAlgorithm.SHA_256, raw, Utilities.Charset.UTF_8);
  return dig.map(function(b) {
    var v = (b < 0 ? b + 256 : b).toString(16);
    return v.length === 1 ? '0' + v : v;
  }).join('');
}

function _isAllowedLoginEmail(email) {
  var e = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  return /@bilgiedu\.net$/.test(e) || /@bilgi\.edu\.tr$/.test(e);
}

function _profileTypeFromEmail(email) {
  var e = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  if (/@bilgiedu\.net$/.test(e)) return 'student';
  if (/@bilgi\.edu\.tr$/.test(e)) return 'staff';
  return '';
}

function _isFacultyOfCommunication(unitName) {
  var u = String(unitName || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  return u === 'faculty of communication' || u === 'iletişim fakültesi' || u === 'iletisim fakultesi';
}

function _verifyRecaptchaToken(token, actionName) {
  try {
    var secret = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().getProperty('RECAPTCHA_SECRET_KEY') || '';
    if (!secret) return { ok: true, skipped: true };
    if (!token) return { ok: false, error: 'Captcha token missing.' };
    var resp = _urlFetchWithTelemetry_('https://www.google.com/recaptcha/api/siteverify', {
      method: 'post',
      payload: { secret: secret, response: token },
      muteHttpExceptions: true
    }, 'recaptcha.verify');
    var out = JSON.parse(resp.getContentText() || '{}');
    var score = Number(out.score || 0);
    if (!out.success) return { ok: false, error: 'Captcha failed.' };
    if (out.action && actionName && out.action !== actionName) return { ok: false, error: 'Captcha action mismatch.' };
    if (score && score < 0.4) return { ok: false, error: 'Captcha score too low.' };
    return { ok: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { ok: false, error: 'Captcha verify error: ' + e.message };
  }
}

function _sessionUserSnapshot_(u) {
  if (!u) return null;
  return {
    id: String(u.id || '').trim(),
    name: String(u.name || '').trim(),
    email: String(u.email || '').trim(),
    role: String(u.role || '').trim(),
    staff_status: String(u.staff_status || '').trim(),
    department: String(u.department || '').trim(),
    bolum: String(u.bolum || '').trim(),
    level: String(u.level || '').trim(),
    yetkiRaw: String(u.yetkiRaw || '').trim(),
    student_no: String(u.student_no || '').trim(),
    yetkiRaw: String(u.yetkiRaw || '').trim(),
    status: String(u.status || '').trim(),
    isComm: !!u.isComm,
    isApplied: !!u.isApplied
  };
}

function _saveAuthSession(email, ttlSec, userSnapshot) {
  _authSessionPeriodicSweep_();
  var normalizedEmail = String(email || '').toLowerCase();
  _authSessionCleanupForEmail_(normalizedEmail, 3);
  var token = Utilities.getUuid().replace(/-/g, '');
  var exp = Date.now() + Math.max(60, Number(ttlSec || 3600)) * 1000;
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  p.setProperty('SESSION_' + token, JSON.stringify({
    email: normalizedEmail,
    exp: exp,
    created: Date.now(),
    user: _sessionUserSnapshot_(userSnapshot)
  }));
  return token;
}

function _authSessionParseSafe_(raw) {
  try {
    var obj = JSON.parse(String(raw || ''));
    if (!obj || !obj.email || !obj.exp) return null;
    return obj;
  } catch (_e) { return null; }
}

function _authSessionPeriodicSweep_(force) {
  try {
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var lastSweep = Number(p.getProperty('SESSION_LAST_SWEEP_MS') || 0);
    // Her kayıtta tam tarama pahalı olmasın: en fazla saatte bir.
    if (!force && (nowMs - lastSweep < 60 * 60 * 1000)) return;
    var all = p.getProperties();
    var del = [];
    for (var k in all) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all, k)) continue;
      if (k.indexOf('SESSION_') !== 0) continue;
      var rec = _authSessionParseSafe_(all[k]);
      if (!rec || Number(rec.exp) < nowMs) del.push(k);
    }
    if (del.length) p.deleteAllProperties(del);
    p.setProperty('SESSION_LAST_SWEEP_MS', String(nowMs));
  } catch (_e2) {}
}

function _authSessionCleanupForEmail_(email, maxKeep) {
  try {
    var em = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!em) return;
    var keep = Math.max(1, parseInt(maxKeep || 3, 10) || 3);
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var all = p.getProperties();
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var mine = [];
    var del = [];
    for (var k in all) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all, k)) continue;
      if (k.indexOf('SESSION_') !== 0) continue;
      var rec = _authSessionParseSafe_(all[k]);
      if (!rec) { del.push(k); continue; }
      var exp = Number(rec.exp) || 0;
      var recEmail = String(rec.email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
      if (exp < nowMs) { del.push(k); continue; }
      if (recEmail === em) {
        mine.push({ key: k, created: Number(rec.created || 0), exp: exp });
      }
    }
    mine.sort(function(a, b) { return b.created - a.created; });
    if (mine.length > keep) {
      for (var i = keep; i < mine.length; i++) del.push(mine[i].key);
    }
    if (del.length) p.deleteAllProperties(del);
  } catch (_e3) {}
}

function _authSessionCompactAll_(maxKeepPerEmail) {
  try {
    var keep = Math.max(1, parseInt(maxKeepPerEmail || 3, 10) || 3);
    var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
    var all = p.getProperties();
    var nowMs = Date.now();
    var byEmail = {};
    var del = [];
    for (var k in all) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all, k)) continue;
      if (k.indexOf('SESSION_') !== 0) continue;
      if (k === 'SESSION_LAST_SWEEP_MS') continue;
      var rec = _authSessionParseSafe_(all[k]);
      if (!rec) { del.push(k); continue; }
      var exp = Number(rec.exp) || 0;
      if (exp < nowMs) { del.push(k); continue; }
      var em = String(rec.email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
      if (!em) { del.push(k); continue; }
      if (!byEmail[em]) byEmail[em] = [];
      byEmail[em].push({ key: k, created: Number(rec.created || 0), exp: exp });
    }
    for (var emk in byEmail) {
      if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(byEmail, emk)) continue;
      var arr = byEmail[emk];
      arr.sort(function(a, b) { return b.created - a.created; });
      if (arr.length > keep) {
        for (var i = keep; i < arr.length; i++) del.push(arr[i].key);
      }
    }
    if (del.length) p.deleteAllProperties(Array.from(new Set(del)));
  } catch (_e4) {}
}

function authSessionsCleanupNow() {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var all = p.getProperties();
  var before = 0;
  for (var k in all) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all, k) && k.indexOf('SESSION_') === 0) before++;
  }
  _authSessionPeriodicSweep_(true);
  _authSessionCompactAll_(3);
  var all2 = p.getProperties();
  var after = 0;
  for (var k2 in all2) {
    if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all2, k2) && k2.indexOf('SESSION_') === 0) after++;
  }
  return { ok: true, before: before, after: after, removed: Math.max(0, before - after) };
}

/**
 * Bakım: Script Properties içindeki SESSION_* ve mail_overdue_* kayıtlarını toplu temizler.
 * DİKKAT: Aktif oturumları da kapatır (yeniden login gerekir).
 */
function authCleanupSessionsAndOverdueMailPropsNow() {
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var all = p.getProperties();
  var toDelete = [];
  var counts = { session: 0, overdueMail: 0 };
  for (var k in all) {
    if (!Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(all, k)) continue;
    if (k.indexOf('SESSION_') === 0) {
      toDelete.push(k);
      counts.session++;
      continue;
    }
    if (k.indexOf('mail_overdue_') === 0) {
      toDelete.push(k);
      counts.overdueMail++;
      continue;
    }
  }
  if (toDelete.length) {
    var uniq = Array.from(new Set(toDelete));
    for (var i = 0; i < uniq.length; i++) {
      p.deleteProperty(uniq[i]);
    }
  }
  return {
    ok: true,
    deleted: counts.session + counts.overdueMail,
    deletedSessions: counts.session,
    deletedOverdueMail: counts.overdueMail
  };
}

function _readAuthSession(token) {
  var t = String(token || '').trim();
  if (!t) return null;
  var p = PropertiesService.getScriptProperties();
  var raw = p.getProperty('SESSION_' + t);
  if (!raw) return null;
  try {
    var obj = JSON.parse(raw);
    if (!obj || !obj.email || !obj.exp) return null;
    if (Date.now() > Number(obj.exp)) {
      p.deleteProperty('SESSION_' + t);
      return null;
    }
    return obj;
  } catch (e) {
    return null;
  }
}

function _deleteAuthSession(token) {
  try {
    if (!token) return;
    PropertiesService.getScriptProperties().deleteProperty('SESSION_' + String(token).trim());
  } catch (e) {}
}

function authRequestOtp(email, captchaToken) {
  try {
    var em = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!_isAllowedLoginEmail(em)) return { error: 'Use a valid @bilgiedu.net or @bilgi.edu.tr address.' };
    var cp = _verifyRecaptchaToken(captchaToken, 'otp_request');
    if (!cp.ok) return { error: cp.error };
    var rl = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    var lockKey = 'OTP_RL_' + em;
    if (rl.get(lockKey)) return { error: 'Please wait 60 seconds before requesting a new code.' };
    var code = String(Math.floor(100000 + Math.random() * 900000));
    var rec = { h: _otpHash(em, code), attempts: 0, exp: Date.now() + 5 * 60 * 1000 };
    rl.put('OTP_CODE_' + em, JSON.stringify(rec), 300);
    rl.put(lockKey, '1', 60);
    var mailBody =
      '<p><strong>TR</strong></p>' +
      '<p>İletişim Fakültesi rezervasyon sistemini kullanabilmek için geçerli tek kullanımlık şifreniz:</p>' +
      '<p style="font-size:24px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:2px;">' + code + '</p>' +
      '<p>Güvenlik için bu şifreyi 5 dakika içinde giriniz. Başarılı girişten sonra oturumunuz (hesap türüne göre) en fazla 24 saat boyunca kullanımlarınızda geçerlidir.</p>' +
      '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
      '<p><strong>EN</strong></p>' +
      '<p>To use the Faculty of Communication reservation system, your valid one-time password is:</p>' +
      '<p style="font-size:24px;font-weight:700;letter-spacing:2px;">' + code + '</p>' +
      '<p>For security, enter this password within 5 minutes. After a successful sign-in, your session remains valid for your usage for up to 24 hours, depending on account type.</p>';
    var mailRes = sendMail(
      em,
      '[Bilgi Booking] One-Time Password / Tek Kullanımlık Şifre',
      mailBody
    );
    if (!mailRes || !mailRes.ok) {
      var detail = mailRes && mailRes.error ? String(mailRes.error) : '';
      return {
        error: detail
          ? ('OTP email could not be delivered: ' + detail)
          : 'OTP email could not be delivered. Check Apps Script mail quota, authorization, and Execution log.'
      };
    }
    return { ok: true, expiresSec: 300 };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function authRegisterByEmail(email, payload, captchaToken) {
  try {
    var em = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    if (!_isAllowedLoginEmail(em)) return { error: 'Only @bilgiedu.net or @bilgi.edu.tr emails are allowed.' };
    var cp = _verifyRecaptchaToken(captchaToken, 'register');
    if (!cp.ok) return { error: cp.error };
    var existing = getUserByEmail(em);
    if (existing) return { error: 'This account already exists. Please request OTP.' };
    var verified = CacheService.getScriptCache().get('OTP_VERIFIED_' + em);
    if (!verified) return { error: 'Please verify OTP first.' };

    var kind = _profileTypeFromEmail(em);
    payload = payload || {};

    function normalizePersonNameTitleCaseServer_(raw) {
      var s = String(raw || '').trim().replace(/\s+/g, ' ');
      if (!s) return '';
      return s.split(' ').map(function(part) {
        var low = part.toLocaleLowerCase('tr-TR');
        return low.charAt(0).toLocaleUpperCase('tr-TR') + low.slice(1);
      }).join(' ');
    }

    if (kind === 'student') {
      var sid = String(payload.student_no || '').replace(/\D/g, '');
      var name = normalizePersonNameTitleCaseServer_(payload.name || '');
      if (!name) return { error: 'Full name is required.' };
      if (sid.length < 6) return { error: 'Valid student number is required.' };
      var st = resolveStudentLevel(sid, '');
      var insertStudent = {
        id: sid,
        email: em,
        full_name: name,
        user_type: 'student',
        role: 'student',
        student_number: sid,
        department_code: String(st.abbr || ''),
        department_name: String(st.deptName || ''),
        access_override_level: String(st.level || '1'),
        senior_flag: String(st.level || '') === '5',
        is_active: true,
        onboarding_completed: true,
        updated_at: now()
      };
      var insSt = supabaseRequest_('post', 'profiles', { select: '*' }, [insertStudent]);
      if (!insSt || !insSt.length) return { error: 'Student profile create failed.' };
      try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove('OTP_VERIFIED_' + em); } catch (eR) {}
      var newUserSt = getUserByEmail(em);
      if (!newUserSt) return { ok: true, profileType: 'student' };
      var uSt = enrichUserMatrix(newUserSt) || newUserSt;
      var ttlSt = isAppAdminRole_(uSt.role) ? (8 * 3600) : (12 * 3600);
      var tokSt = _saveAuthSession(em, ttlSt, uSt);
      return { ok: true, profileType: 'student', token: tokSt, ttlSec: ttlSt, user: uSt };
    }

    if (kind === 'staff') {
      var staffName = normalizePersonNameTitleCaseServer_(payload.name || '');
      var staffStatusRaw = String(payload.staff_status || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var unit = String(payload.unit || '').trim();
      var commDept = String(payload.comm_dept || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!staffName) return { error: 'Full name is required.' };
      if (staffStatusRaw !== 'akademik' && staffStatusRaw !== 'idari') return { error: 'Staff type must be akademik or idari.' };
      if (!unit) return { error: 'Unit is required.' };
      var isCommUnit = _isFacultyOfCommunication(unit);
      if (staffStatusRaw === 'akademik' && isCommUnit && !commDept) {
        return { error: 'Department is required for Faculty of Communication.' };
      }
      var role = 'instructor';
      var sf = resolveStaffLevel(staffStatusRaw, unit, commDept, role);
      var insertStaff = {
        id: genId('STF'),
        email: em,
        full_name: staffName,
        user_type: 'staff',
        role: role,
        staff_type: staffStatusRaw === 'idari' ? 'administrative' : 'academic',
        faculty_name: unit,
        department_code: commDept,
        department_name: unit,
        access_override_level: String(sf.level || '1'),
        senior_flag: String(sf.level || '') === '5',
        is_active: true,
        onboarding_completed: true,
        updated_at: now()
      };
      var insSf = supabaseRequest_('post', 'profiles', { select: '*' }, [insertStaff]);
      if (!insSf || !insSf.length) return { error: 'Staff profile create failed.' };
      try { CacheService.getScriptCache().remove('OTP_VERIFIED_' + em); } catch (eRf) {}
      var newUserSf = getUserByEmail(em);
      if (!newUserSf) return { ok: true, profileType: 'staff' };
      var uSf = enrichUserMatrix(newUserSf) || newUserSf;
      var ttlSf = isAppAdminRole_(uSf.role) ? (8 * 3600) : (12 * 3600);
      var tokSf = _saveAuthSession(em, ttlSf, uSf);
      return { ok: true, profileType: 'staff', token: tokSf, ttlSec: ttlSf, user: uSf };
    }

    return { error: 'Unsupported email domain.' };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function authVerifyOtp(email, code, remember, captchaToken) {
  try {
    var em = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
    var cd = String(code || '').trim();
    if (!_isAllowedLoginEmail(em)) return { error: 'Invalid email domain.' };
    if (!/^\d{6}$/.test(cd)) return { error: 'Invalid OTP code.' };
    var cp = _verifyRecaptchaToken(captchaToken, 'otp_verify');
    if (!cp.ok) return { error: cp.error };
    var cache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    var key = 'OTP_CODE_' + em;
    var raw = cache.get(key);
    if (!raw) return { error: 'OTP expired or not found. Request a new code.' };
    var rec = JSON.parse(raw);
    if (!rec || Date.now() > Number(rec.exp || 0)) {
      cache.remove(key);
      return { error: 'OTP expired. Request a new code.' };
    }
    if (_otpHash(em, cd) !== String(rec.h || '')) {
      rec.attempts = Number(rec.attempts || 0) + 1;
      if (rec.attempts >= 5) {
        cache.remove(key);
        return { error: 'Too many attempts. Request a new code.' };
      }
      cache.put(key, JSON.stringify(rec), Math.max(30, Math.floor((Number(rec.exp) - Date.now()) / 1000)));
      return { error: 'Incorrect OTP.' };
    }
    cache.remove(key);
    var user = getUserByEmail(em);
    if (!user) {
      CacheService.getScriptCache().put('OTP_VERIFIED_' + em, '1', 900);
      return { ok: true, needsOnboarding: true, profileType: _profileTypeFromEmail(em), email: em };
    }
    var u = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
    var isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(u.role);
    var ttl = isAdmin ? (8 * 3600) : (12 * 3600);
    var token = _saveAuthSession(em, ttl, u);
    return { ok: true, token: token, ttlSec: ttl, user: u, remember: !!remember };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function authGetSession(token) {
  try {
    var s = _readAuthSession(token);
    if (!s) return { error: 'Session expired.' };
    var user = (s && s.user) ? s.user : getUserByEmail(s.email);
    if (user && s && s.email) {
      var isStaffLike = (user.role === ROLES.INSTRUCTOR) || (user.email && String(user.email).toLowerCase().indexOf('@bilgi.edu.tr') >= 0);
      if (isStaffLike && (user.yetkiRaw === undefined || user.yetkiRaw === null || user.yetkiRaw === '')) {
        var freshUser = getUserByEmail(s.email);
        if (freshUser) user = freshUser;
      }
    }
    if (!user) return { error: 'User not found.' };
    var u = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
    return { ok: true, user: u, email: s.email, expiresAt: s.exp };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function authLogout(token) {
  _deleteAuthSession(token);
  return { ok: true };
}

/**
 * Ortak yardımcı: Test token veya Session email'den kullanıcı çözer.
 * Tüm bridge fonksiyonları bunu kullanacak.
 */
function resolveCurrentUser(testToken) {
  var u = null;
  if (testToken) {
    var s = _readAuthSession(testToken);
    if (s && s.user) {
      u = s.user;
      var isStaffLike = (u.role === ROLES.INSTRUCTOR) || (u.email && String(u.email).toLowerCase().indexOf('@bilgi.edu.tr') >= 0);
      if (isStaffLike && (u.yetkiRaw === undefined || u.yetkiRaw === null || u.yetkiRaw === '')) {
        var fresh = getUserByEmail(s.email);
        if (fresh) u = fresh;
      }
    } else if (s && s.email) {
      u = getUserByEmail(s.email);
    }
  } else {
    var email = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail();
    if (!email) return null;
    u = getUserByEmail(email);
  }
  return u ? enrichUserMatrix(u) : null;
}

/** Admin web / google.script.run: OTP veya (nadir) Script oturumu ile çözülmüş kullanıcı admin rollerinden biri olmalı. */
function requireAdminWebUser_(testToken) {
  var u = testToken ? resolveCurrentUser(testToken) : resolveCurrentUser('');
  if (!u || !canAccessAdminWeb_(u.role)) return null;
  return u;
}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// ADIM 2: MEVCUT 4 BRIDGE FONKSİYONUNU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// Her fonksiyona testToken parametresi eklendi.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────


/**
 * Kullanıcının Rezervasyonları (testToken destekli)
 */
function tryGetUserBookingsFromSupabase_(user) {
  if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_() || !user) return null;
  var searchId = String(user.id || '');
  var searchStudentNo = String(user.student_no || '');
  var searchEmail = user.email ? String(user.email).toLowerCase() : '';
  if (!searchId && !searchEmail) return [];

  var eqRes = [];
  var resRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(_supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_(), { select: '*' }).rows || [];
  resRows.forEach(function(r) {
    var sid = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['student_id', 'user_id', 'email'], '')).trim();
    var sidLower = sid.toLowerCase();
    var isMatch = false;
    if (searchId && sid === searchId) isMatch = true;
    if (searchStudentNo && sid === searchStudentNo) isMatch = true;
    if (searchEmail && sidLower === searchEmail) isMatch = true;
    if (!isMatch) return;
    eqRes.push({
      id: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['reservation_group_id', 'res_id', 'reservation_id', 'id'], '')).trim(),
      eqId: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim(),
      item: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_name', 'item_name', 'name'], '')).trim(),
      type: 'Equipment',
      start: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '') || ''),
      end: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '') || ''),
      status: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], 'Pending')).trim()
    });
  });

  var stRes = [];
  try {
    var stRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['studio_reservations'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
    stRows.forEach(function(r) {
      var uid = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['user_id', 'email'], '')).trim();
      var uLower = uid.toLowerCase();
      if (uid !== searchId && uLower !== searchEmail) return;
      stRes.push({
        id: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['id'], '')).trim(),
        item: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['studio_name', 'name'], '')).trim(),
        type: 'Studio',
        start: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['start_dt', 'start_date'], '') || ''),
        end: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['end_dt', 'end_date'], '') || ''),
        status: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], 'pending')).trim()
      });
    });
  } catch (_eSt) {}

  var all = eqRes.concat(stRes);
  all.sort(function(a, b) { return new Date(b.start || 0) - new Date(a.start || 0); });
  return all;
}

function getUserBookings(testToken) {
  var t0Bookings = Date.now();
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return [];
    var kBookings = _cacheKey_('userBookings', [String(user.id || ''), String(user.student_no || ''), String(user.email || '').toLowerCase()]);
    var cBookings = _cacheGetJson_(kBookings);
    if (cBookings) {
      _debugSourceLog_('getUserBookings', 'cache', t0Bookings, { uid: String(user.id || ''), count: cBookings.length || 0 });
      return cBookings;
    }
    var sbBookings = tryGetUserBookingsFromSupabase_(user) || [];
    if (sbBookings.error) return [];
    _cachePutJson_(kBookings, sbBookings, 15);
