    _debugSourceLog_('getUserBookings', 'supabase-only', t0Bookings, { uid: String(user.id || ''), count: sbBookings.length || 0 });
    return sbBookings;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getUserBookings error: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

function formatBanStageForUser(level) {
  var L = String(level || '');
  if (L.indexOf('yellow') >= 0) return 'Yellow warning';
  if (L.indexOf('15_day') >= 0 || L.indexOf('DAY15') >= 0) return '15-day suspension';
  if (L.indexOf('SEMESTER') >= 0) return 'Semester suspension';
  if (L.indexOf('PERMANENT') >= 0) return 'Permanent ban';
  if (L === 'manual') return 'Manual / other';
  return L || 'Record';
}

function formatBanStageAdmin(level) {
  var L = String(level || '');
  if (L.indexOf('yellow') >= 0) return 'Sarı uyarı';
  if (L.indexOf('15_day') >= 0 || L.indexOf('DAY15') >= 0) return '15 gün askı';
  if (L.indexOf('SEMESTER') >= 0) return 'Dönem uzaklaştırma';
  if (L.indexOf('PERMANENT') >= 0) return 'Kalıcı';
  if (L === 'manual') return 'Manuel';
  return L || '—';
}

function getUserDashboardExtrasForUser_(user) {
  try {
    if (!user) return { error: 'Not signed in.', loans: [], penalties: [], appBlocked: false, blockReason: '' };
    var uid = String(user.id || '');
    var em = user.email ? String(user.email).toLowerCase() : '';
    var now = Date.now();
    var loans = [];
    try {
      var invRows = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
      invRows.forEach(function(r) {
        var sidCell = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['assigned_to', 'student_id', 'user_id', 'email'], '')).trim();
        var okUser = (uid && sidCell === uid) || (em && sidCell.toLowerCase() === em);
        if (!okUser) return;
        var st = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
        var onLoan = st === 'IN_USE' || st === 'IN USE' || st === 'TAKEN' || st === 'KULLANIMDA' || st === 'DIŞARIDA' || st === 'OVERDUE';
        if (!onLoan) return;
        var dueRaw = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['due_date', 'return_date'], '') || '');
        var dueMs = dueRaw ? new Date(dueRaw).getTime() : NaN;
        loans.push({
          eqId: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['id', 'equipment_id'], '')).trim(),
          name: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['name', 'equipment_name'], '')).trim(),
          due: dueRaw,
          overdue: !isNaN(dueMs) && dueMs < now,
          msLeft: isNaN(dueMs) ? null : (dueMs - now),
          resGroupId: '',
          handover: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['checked_out_at', 'handover_date'], '') || ''),
          resEnd: dueRaw
        });
      });
    } catch (_eLoan) {}
    var banRows = [];
    try {
      banRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['bans'], { select: '*', user_id: 'eq.' + uid, order: 'banned_at.desc', limit: 200 }).rows || [];
    } catch (_eBan) { banRows = []; }
    var penalties = banRows.map(function(b) {
      var active = String(supaRowPick_(b, ['active'], 'false')).toLowerCase() === 'true';
      var expRaw = String(supaRowPick_(b, ['expires_at'], '') || '');
      var expMs = expRaw ? new Date(expRaw).getTime() : NaN;
      var remainingMs = !isNaN(expMs) ? Math.max(0, expMs - Date.now()) : null;
      var bl = String(supaRowPick_(b, ['ban_level'], '') || '');
      var isYellow = bl.indexOf('yellow') >= 0;
      return {
        id: String(supaRowPick_(b, ['id'], '') || ''),
        ban_level: bl,
        stageLabel: formatBanStageForUser(bl),
        reason: String(supaRowPick_(b, ['reason'], '') || ''),
        banned_at: String(supaRowPick_(b, ['banned_at'], '') || ''),
        expires_at: expRaw,
        active: active,
        remainingMs: remainingMs,
        isYellowWarning: isYellow,
        isHardBan: active && !isYellow
      };
    });
    var hasOverdue = loans.some(function(L) { return L.overdue; });
    var hasBlockingPenalty = penalties.some(function(p) { return p.active && !p.isYellowWarning; });
    var appBlocked = hasOverdue || hasBlockingPenalty;
    var blockReason = '';
    if (hasOverdue && hasBlockingPenalty) blockReason = 'overdue_and_penalty';
    else if (hasOverdue) blockReason = 'overdue';
    else if (hasBlockingPenalty) blockReason = 'penalty';
    if (isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) {
      appBlocked = false;
      blockReason = '';
    }
    return { loans: loans, penalties: penalties, appBlocked: appBlocked, blockReason: blockReason };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message, loans: [], penalties: [], appBlocked: false, blockReason: '' };
  }
}

function getUserDashboardExtras(testToken) {
  var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
  return getUserDashboardExtrasForUser_(user);
}

function _assertUserNotAppBlocked_(user) {
  if (!user) throw new Error('User not found.');
  if (isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) return;
  var ex = getUserDashboardExtrasForUser_(user);
  if (ex && ex.appBlocked) {
    throw new Error('Your account is restricted (overdue equipment or an active non-warning penalty). Please visit the equipment desk. New bookings are disabled until this is resolved.');
  }
}

function getAdminOverdueEquipmentListCore_() {
  try {
    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return [];
    var headers = data[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var ixId = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('equipment_id') >= 0; });
    if (ixId === -1) ixId = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h === 'id'; });
    var ixName = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('equipment_name') >= 0; });
    if (ixName === -1) ixName = 2;
    var ixSt = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('status') >= 0 || h.indexOf('durum') >= 0; });
    var ixRet = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('return_date') >= 0; });
    var ixSid = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('student_id') >= 0; });
    var ixSname = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('student_name') >= 0; });
    var ixMail = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('email') >= 0 && h.indexOf('student') < 0; });
    var now = Date.now();
    var out = [];
    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      var id = String(ixId >= 0 ? row[ixId] : row[0]).trim();
      if (!id) continue;
      var st = String(ixSt >= 0 ? row[ixSt] : '').toUpperCase();
      if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
      var outSt = st === 'IN_USE' || st === 'IN USE' || st === 'TAKEN' || st === 'KULLANIMDA' || st === 'DIŞARIDA' || st === 'OVERDUE';
      if (!outSt) continue;
      var dueRaw = ixRet >= 0 ? row[ixRet] : '';
      if (!dueRaw) continue;
      var dueMs = new Date(dueRaw).getTime();
      if (isNaN(dueMs) || dueMs >= now) continue;
      out.push({
        id: id,
        name: String(ixName >= 0 ? row[ixName] : row[2]).trim(),
        studentId: String(ixSid >= 0 ? row[ixSid] : '').trim(),
        studentName: String(ixSname >= 0 ? row[ixSname] : '').trim(),
        due: String(dueRaw),
        emailHint: String(ixMail >= 0 ? row[ixMail] : '').trim()
      });
    }
    return out;
  } catch (e) {
    Logger.log('getAdminOverdueEquipmentListCore_: ' + e.message);
    return [];
  }
}

function getAdminOverdueEquipmentList(adminToken) {
  if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return [];
  return getAdminOverdueEquipmentListCore_();
}

function adminSendOverdueReminderEmails(equipmentIds, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var ids = equipmentIds || [];
    if (!ids.length) return { success: false, error: 'Seçim yok.' };
    var list = getAdminOverdueEquipmentListCore_();
    var map = {};
    list.forEach(function(x) { map[x.id] = x; });
    var sent = 0;
    var skipped = [];
    ids.forEach(function(id) {
      var item = map[String(id).trim()];
      if (!item) { skipped.push(id); return; }
      var email = item.emailHint;
      if (!email || email.indexOf('@') < 0) {
        var lu = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(item.studentId);
        if (lu && lu.ok && lu.email && lu.email.indexOf('@') >= 0) email = lu.email;
      }
      if (!email || email.indexOf('@') < 0) { skipped.push(id); return; }
      var subj = '[' + CONFIG.APP_NAME + '] Iade hatirlatmasi / Equipment return reminder';
      var body = '<p><strong>TR</strong></p><p>Merhaba,</p><p>Asagidaki ekipmanin iade suresi <strong>gecmistir</strong>:</p><p><strong>' + item.name + '</strong> (' + item.id + ')<br>Son iade: ' + item.due + '</p><p>Lutfen en kisa surede ekipman ofisine iade ediniz.</p>' +
        '<hr style="border:none;border-top:1px solid #ddd;margin:12px 0;">' +
        '<p><strong>EN</strong></p><p>Hello,</p><p>This is a reminder that the following depot item is <strong>overdue</strong> for return:</p><p><strong>' + item.name + '</strong> (' + item.id + ')<br>Due: ' + item.due + '</p><p>Please return it to the equipment office as soon as possible.</p>';
      sendMail(email, subj, body);
      sent++;
    });
    return { success: true, sent: sent, skipped: skipped.length };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

function getAdminPenaltiesList(adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return [];
    var list = toObjs(getSheet(SHEETS.BANS));
    return list.sort(function(a, b) { return new Date(b.banned_at || 0) - new Date(a.banned_at || 0); }).map(function(b) {
      var active = b.active === true || String(b.active).toLowerCase() === 'true';
      var expMs = b.expires_at ? new Date(b.expires_at).getTime() : NaN;
      var remainingMs = !isNaN(expMs) ? Math.max(0, expMs - Date.now()) : null;
      var bl = String(b.ban_level || '');
      var isYellow = bl.indexOf('yellow') >= 0;
      return {
        id: String(b.id || ''),
        user_id: String(b.user_id || ''),
        user_name: String(b.user_name || ''),
        ban_level: bl,
        stageLabel: formatBanStageAdmin(bl),
        reason: String(b.reason || ''),
        banned_at: String(b.banned_at || ''),
        expires_at: String(b.expires_at || ''),
        active: active,
        remainingMs: remainingMs,
        isSuspended: active && !isYellow,
        isYellow: isYellow
      };
    });
  } catch (e) {
    return [];
  }
}

/**
 * Rezervasyon İptali (testToken destekli)
 */
function cancelBookingBridge(id, type, testToken) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'User not found.' };

    if (type === 'Studio') {
      studioReservationsCancel({ id: id }, user);
      _invalidateUserBookingsCache_(user);
    } else {
      var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
      var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
      var colCan = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
      var idTrim = String(id).trim();
      var changed = 0;
      for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][colCan.group]).trim() !== idTrim) continue;
        var currentStatus = String(data[i][colCan.status]).trim();
        var st = currentStatus.toLowerCase();
        if (st === 'pending' || st === 'approved') {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colCan.status + 1).setValue('Cancelled');
          changed++;
        }
      }
      if (changed === 0) {
        return { error: 'Reservation is not cancellable or already updated.' };
      }
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(idTrim); } catch (_sc) {}
      _invalidateUserBookingsCache_(user);
      audit('reservation.cancel', user.id, id, null, { status: 'Cancelled' });
    }
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

/**
 * Stüdyo Rezervasyonu (testToken destekli)
 */
function createStudioReservationBridge(studioId, startDt, endDt, purpose, pdfUrl, keyPickupDt, requestType, testToken) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) {
      var tt = String(testToken || '').trim();
      if (!tt) {
        return { error: 'Giriş gerekli. OTP ile oturum açın. / Please sign in with OTP.' };
      }
      var sess = _readAuthSession(tt);
      if (!sess) {
        return { error: 'Oturum süresi doldu veya geçersiz. Tekrar giriş yapın. / Session expired. Please sign in again.' };
      }
      return { error: 'E-posta sisteme kayıtlı değil (Personel / Öğrenci tablosu). Yönetimle iletişime geçin. / Email not found in staff/student directory.' };
    }
    try { _assertUserNotAppBlocked_(user); } catch (bx) { return { error: bx.message || String(bx) }; }
    var payload = {
      studio_id: studioId,
      start_dt: startDt,
      end_dt: endDt,
      purpose: purpose || '',
      pdf_url: String(pdfUrl || '').trim(),
      key_pickup_dt: keyPickupDt || '',
      request_type: requestType || ''
    };
    return studioReservationsCreate(payload, user);
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function checkEquipmentReservationConflictsBridge(itemIds, startDt, endDt, testToken) {
  try {
    var t0 = Date.now();
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'User not found.' };
    var ids = Array.isArray(itemIds) ? itemIds : [];
    if (!ids.length) return { ok: true, conflicts: [], availableIds: [] };
    var reqIds = [];
    var reqSet = {};
    for (var ri = 0; ri < ids.length; ri++) {
      var norm = String(ids[ri] || '').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!norm || reqSet[norm]) continue;
      reqSet[norm] = true;
      reqIds.push(norm);
    }
    if (!reqIds.length) return { ok: true, conflicts: [], availableIds: [] };
    reqIds.sort();

    // Hot path cache: same ID set + same range frequently rechecked by UI.
    var cacheKey = _cacheKey_('eqConflictBridge', [startDt, endDt, reqIds.join(',')]);
    var cached = _cacheGetJson_(cacheKey);
    if (cached && cached.ok === true) {
      cached.cache = 'hit';
      Logger.log('checkEquipmentReservationConflictsBridge ms=' + (Date.now() - t0) + ' req=' + reqIds.length + ' avail=' + ((cached.availableIds || []).length) + ' conflicts=' + ((cached.conflicts || []).length) + ' cache=hit');
      return cached;
    }
    try {
      assertDepotSlotCapacity_(startDt, endDt, '', {});
    } catch (se) {
      return { error: se.message || String(se) };
    }
    var startMs = new Date(startDt).getTime();
    var endMs = new Date(endDt).getTime();
    if (isNaN(startMs) || isNaN(endMs) || endMs <= startMs) {
      return { error: 'Invalid date range.' };
    }

    // 1) Inventory map (only requested IDs) from Supabase.
    var invData = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
    var invMap = {};
    for (var i = 0; i < invData.length; i++) {
      var rid = String(supaRowPick_(invData[i], ['id', 'equipment_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!rid || !reqSet[rid]) continue;
      invMap[rid] = {
        id: rid,
        name: String(supaRowPick_(invData[i], ['name', 'equipment_name'], '')).trim(),
        status: String(supaRowPick_(invData[i], ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase()
      };
    }

    // 2) Reservation overlap index from Supabase.
    var overlapByEq = {};
    var resData = _supaSelectAllEquipmentReservationLines_().rows || [];
    for (var r = 0; r < resData.length; r++) {
      var row = resData[r];
      var eqId = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!eqId || !reqSet[eqId]) continue;
      if (!_reservationRowCountsAsBlocking_(supaRowPick_(row, ['status'], ''))) continue;
      var rs = new Date(supaRowPick_(row, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '')).getTime();
      var re = new Date(supaRowPick_(row, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '')).getTime();
      if (isNaN(rs) || isNaN(re)) continue;
      if (startMs < re && endMs > rs) overlapByEq[eqId] = true;
    }

    var conflicts = [];
    var available = [];
    reqIds.forEach(function(cid) {
      var inv = invMap[cid];
      if (!inv) {
        conflicts.push({ id: cid, name: cid, reason: 'Not found in inventory.' });
        return;
      }
      var st = inv.status;
      if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
      if (st !== 'AVAILABLE') {
        conflicts.push({ id: cid, name: inv.name || cid, reason: 'IN_USE' });
        return;
      }
      if (overlapByEq[cid]) {
        conflicts.push({ id: cid, name: inv.name || cid, reason: 'SCHEDULING_CONFLICT' });
        return;
      }
      available.push(cid);
    });
    var out = { ok: true, conflicts: conflicts, availableIds: available, cache: 'miss' };
    _cachePutJson_(cacheKey, out, 45);
    Logger.log('checkEquipmentReservationConflictsBridge ms=' + (Date.now() - t0) + ' req=' + reqIds.length + ' avail=' + available.length + ' conflicts=' + conflicts.length + ' cache=miss');
    return out;
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function inventoryUpdateReturnDateForEquipment(equipmentId, newReturnIso, userId, studentNo) {
  try {
    var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    if (data.length < 2) return;
    var headers = data[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var colEq = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('equipment_id') >= 0; });
    if (colEq === -1) colEq = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h === 'id'; });
    var colRet = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('return_date') >= 0; });
    var colSid = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('student_id') >= 0; });
    if (colEq === -1 || colRet === -1) return;
    var eq = String(equipmentId).trim();
    var uid = String(userId || '').trim();
    var sno = String(studentNo || '').trim();
    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      if (String(data[i][colEq]).trim() !== eq) continue;
      if (colSid >= 0) {
        var cell = String(data[i][colSid] || '').trim();
        var match = (uid && cell === uid) || (sno && cell === sno);
        if (!match) continue;
      }
      sheet.getRange(i + 1, colRet + 1).setValue(newReturnIso);
      SpreadsheetApp.flush();
      return;
    }
  } catch (e) { Logger.log('inventoryUpdateReturnDateForEquipment: ' + e.message); }
}

function extendStudentEquipmentReservation(testToken, groupResId, equipmentId, newEndIso) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'User not found.' };
    var u = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
    if (u.role !== ROLES.STUDENT || parseInt(String(u.level || '0'), 10) !== 4) {
      return { error: 'Extension is only available for Level 4 students.' };
    }
    var gid = String(groupResId).trim();
    var eqId = String(equipmentId).trim();
    var searchId = String(u.id || '');
    var searchStudentNo = String(u.student_no || '');
    var searchEmail = String(u.email || '').toLowerCase();
    var sheet = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colEx = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var foundRow = -1;
    var startDt = '';
    var oldEnd = '';
    for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
      var row = data[i];
      if (String(row[colEx.group] || '').trim() !== gid) continue;
      if (String(row[colEx.eqId] || '').trim() !== eqId) continue;
      var sid = String(row[colEx.student] || '').trim();
      var okUser = (searchId && sid === searchId) || (searchStudentNo && sid === searchStudentNo) ||
        (searchEmail && sid.toLowerCase() === searchEmail);
      if (!okUser) return { error: 'Not your reservation.' };
      var st = String(row[colEx.status] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (st !== 'picked up' && st !== 'approved') {
        return { error: 'Extension is only available for approved or picked-up equipment.' };
      }
      foundRow = i + 1;
      startDt = row[colEx.handover] ? String(row[colEx.handover]) : '';
      oldEnd = row[colEx.ret] ? String(row[colEx.ret]) : '';
      break;
    }
    if (foundRow === -1) return { error: 'Reservation line not found.' };
    if (!startDt) return { error: 'Invalid reservation data.' };
    if (new Date(newEndIso).getTime() <= new Date(oldEnd).getTime()) {
      return { error: 'New return must be after your current due time.' };
    }
    validateEquipmentExtendReturn(startDt, newEndIso, u);
    try {
      assertDepotSlotCapacity_(startDt, newEndIso, gid, { checkStart: false, checkEnd: true });
    } catch (se) {
      return { error: se.message || String(se) };
    }
    var chk = reservationsCheckAvailabilityExcludingGroup({
      item_id: eqId,
      start_dt: startDt,
      end_dt: newEndIso,
      exclude_group_id: gid
    });
    if (!chk.available) return { error: 'That equipment is already booked for part of the time you selected.' };
    sheet.getRange(foundRow, colEx.ret + 1).setValue(newEndIso);
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    inventoryUpdateReturnDateForEquipment(eqId, newEndIso, searchId, searchStudentNo);
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(gid); } catch (_se2) {}
    audit('reservation.extend', u.id, gid, { end: oldEnd }, { end: newEndIso, equipment_id: eqId });
    return { success: true, new_end: newEndIso };
  } catch (e) {
    var msg = e.message || String(e);
    if (msg.indexOf('EXTEND_MAX_DAYS:') === 0) return { error: 'EXTEND_MAX_DAYS' };
    return { error: msg };
  }
}

function extendEquipmentReservationBridge(groupResId, equipmentId, newEndIso, testToken) {
  return extendStudentEquipmentReservation(testToken, groupResId, equipmentId, newEndIso);
}

/**
 * Öğrenci numarasından bölüm kodunu çıkarır.
 * Önce 3 haneli istisnaları kontrol eder (156, 305),
 * sonra standart 2 haneli kodu dener.
 * 
 * @param {string} studentId - Öğrenci numarası (ör: "12334001")
 * @returns {object|null} - { abbr, name, baseLevel, isApplied } veya null
 */
function parseDeptFromStudentId(studentId) {
  var sid = String(studentId || '').replace(/\D/g, '');
  if (sid.length < 5) return null;
  
  // Önce 3 haneli istisnaları dene (156, 305)
  var code3 = sid.substring(3, 6);
  if (DEPT_CODE_MAP[code3]) return DEPT_CODE_MAP[code3];
  
  // Sonra standart 2 haneli kodu dene
  var code2 = sid.substring(3, 5);
  if (DEPT_CODE_MAP[code2]) return DEPT_CODE_MAP[code2];
  
  return null; // İletişim Fakültesi dışı
}

/**
 * Öğrenci için nihai yetki seviyesini belirler.
 * 
 * Öncelik sırası:
 *   1. Sheet'te manuel override (Yetki kolonu) varsa → onu kullan
 *   2. Yoksa → bölüm taban yetkisini kullan
 *   3. Bölüm bulunamazsa (diğer fakülte) → 1
 * 
 * @param {string} studentId - Öğrenci numarası
 * @param {string} sheetOverride - Sheet'teki Yetki kolonundaki değer
 * @returns {object} - { level, dept, isComm, isApplied }
 */
function resolveStudentLevel(studentId, sheetOverride) {
  var dept = parseDeptFromStudentId(studentId);
  var override = String(sheetOverride || '').trim();
  var facultyName = 'Faculty of Communication';
  
  // Diğer fakülte (kod eşleşmedi)
  if (!dept) {
    return {
      level: (override === '5' || override === '4') ? override : '1',
      dept: null,
      deptName: 'Non-Faculty',
      isComm: false,
      isApplied: false
    };
  }
  
  // İletişim Fakültesi — override kontrolü
  var finalLevel = dept.baseLevel;
  var sid = String(studentId || '').replace(/\D/g, '');
  var entryYY = NaN;
  if (sid.length >= 3) {
    entryYY = parseInt(sid.substring(1, 3), 10); // 2. ve 3. hane
  }
  // Uygulamali bolumlerde (TVRP/MED/FTV/VCD), giris yili <=22 ise otomatik en az Level 4.
  if (dept.isApplied && !isNaN(entryYY) && entryYY <= 22) {
    finalLevel = Math.max(finalLevel, 4);
  }
  
  if (override && !isNaN(parseInt(override))) {
    var overrideNum = parseInt(override);
    // Override ancak taban yetkiden yüksekse veya 4/5 ise geçerli
    if (overrideNum > finalLevel || overrideNum === 4 || overrideNum === 5) {
      finalLevel = overrideNum;
    }
  }
  
  return {
    level: String(finalLevel),
    dept: dept,
    deptName: facultyName,
    abbr: dept.abbr,
    isComm: true,
    isApplied: dept.isApplied
  };
}

// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// DEĞİŞİKLİK 4/6: canUserAccessStudio — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// studiosListForUser da güncelleniyor.
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 
/**
 * Kullanıcının belirli bir stüdyoya erişim hakkını kontrol eder.
 * 
 * MATRIS:
 *   - Diğer fakülte öğrenci → Stüdyo erişimi YOK
 *   - İletişim öğrenci/personel → A seviye (GREEN, PODCAST, DUBBING)
 *   - İdari/diğer personel → A seviye
 *   - SENIOR (level 5) → A + B seviye (tüm stüdyolar)
 *   - Admin/Technician → tüm stüdyolar
 */
function canUserAccessStudio(user, studioId) {
  var isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role);
  var userLevel = parseInt(user.level || '1');
  var studioLevel = STUDIO_LEVELS[studioId] || 'A';
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  
  // Admin/Technician → her şeye erişim
  if (isAdmin) return { ok: true };
  if (_hasActiveSpecialStudioAccess_(user, sid)) return { ok: true };
  
  // SENIOR (level 5) → A + B tüm stüdyolar
  if (userLevel === 5) return { ok: true };
  
  // B seviye stüdyolar (RED, BLUE) → sadece level 5 ve admin
  if (studioLevel === 'B') {
    return { ok: false, reason: 'Bu stüdyo Senior (Seviye 5) yetkisi gerektirir.' };
  }
  
  // A seviye stüdyolar (GREEN, PODCAST, DUBBING)
  if (user.role === ROLES.STUDENT) {
    // Öğrenci — İletişim Fakültesi mi?
    var isComm = user.isComm;
    
    // isComm bilgisi yoksa student_no'dan tekrar hesapla
    if (isComm === undefined || isComm === null) {
      var stuInfo = parseDeptFromStudentId(user.student_no || user.id);
      isComm = !!stuInfo;
    }
    
    if (!isComm) {
      return { ok: false, reason: 'Studio access is limited to Communication Faculty students.' };
    }
    
    // İletişim öğrenci → A seviye OK
    return { ok: true };
  }
  
  // Personel → A seviye stüdyolara her zaman erişim
  return { ok: true };
}
 
/**
 * Kullanıcının erişebildiği stüdyoları listeler.
 * Yetkisiz stüdyolar listede GÖRÜNMEZ.
 */
function studiosListForUser(user) {
  var isAdmin = isAppAdminRole_(user.role);
  
  return Object.values(STUDIOS).filter(function(s) {
    if (isAdmin) return true;
    if (s.adminOnly) return false;
    return canUserAccessStudio(user, s.id).ok;
  }).map(function(s) {
    return {
      id: s.id,
      name: s.name,
      weekendOk: s.weekendOk,
      keyCount: s.keyCount,
      formUrl: 'https://docs.google.com/document/d/' + CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID
    };
  });
}

function _specialStudioAccessSet_(raw) {
  var s = String(raw || '').toUpperCase();
  var tokens = s.split(/[^A-Z]+/).filter(function(x) { return !!x; });
  var allow = {};
  tokens.forEach(function(t) {
    if (t === 'GREEN' || t === 'RED' || t === 'PODCAST' || t === 'DUBBING') {
      allow[t] = true;
    }
  });
  return allow;
}

function _isSpecialStudioAccessActiveUntil_(rawUntil) {
  var txt = String(rawUntil || '').trim();
  if (!txt) return true;
  var d = new Date(txt);
  if (isNaN(d.getTime())) return false;
  // Tarih girildiyse o gün sonuna kadar geçerli kabul et.
  if (/^\d{4}-\d{2}-\d{2}$/.test(txt)) d.setHours(23, 59, 59, 999);
  return d.getTime() >= Date.now();
}

function _hasActiveSpecialStudioAccess_(user, studioId) {
  if (!user) return false;
  var sid = String(studioId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (!sid) return false;
  var allow = _specialStudioAccessSet_(user.special_access || '');
  if (!allow[sid]) return false;
  return _isSpecialStudioAccessActiveUntil_(user.special_access_until || '');
}

/**
 * Sheet Yetki ham değeri + öğrenci no ile matris; sepet/stüdyo listesi bayrakları.
 */
function enrichUserMatrix(user) {
  if (!user) return null;
  var u = Object.assign({}, user);
  if (u.role === ROLES.STUDENT && u.student_no) {
    // Öğrenci override yalnızca sheet'teki Yetki(F) hücresinden gelsin.
    // Session/user objesindeki stale `level` değeri override gibi kullanılmamalı.
    var raw = (u.yetkiRaw === undefined || u.yetkiRaw === null) ? '' : String(u.yetkiRaw).trim();
    var st = resolveStudentLevel(String(u.student_no), raw);
    u.level = st.level;
    u.isComm = st.isComm;
    u.isApplied = st.isApplied;
    if (st.deptName) u.department = st.deptName;
    if (st.abbr) u.bolum = st.abbr;
  } else if (u.role === ROLES.INSTRUCTOR || (u.email && String(u.email).toLowerCase().indexOf('@bilgi.edu.tr') >= 0)) {
    var staffYetkiRaw = (u.yetkiRaw === undefined || u.yetkiRaw === null) ? '' : String(u.yetkiRaw).trim();
    var stf = resolveStaffLevel(String(u.staff_status || 'akademik'), String(u.department || ''), String(u.bolum || ''), staffYetkiRaw);
    // Personel için nihai seviye mutlaka matristen gelsin; eski/stale level değeri eq_level filtrelerini bozmasın.
    u.level = String(stf.level || u.level || '1');
    u.yetkiRaw = staffYetkiRaw;
    if (u.isApplied === undefined) u.isApplied = stf.isApplied;
    if (u.isComm === undefined) u.isComm = stf.isComm;
  }
  u.showStudiosTab = studiosListForUser(u).length > 0;
  u.levelLabel = ({ '1': 'TEMEL', '2': 'ORTA', '3': 'İLERİ', '4': 'PRO', '5': 'SENIOR' })[String(u.level || '1')] || ('Level ' + u.level);
  return u;
}

function getAllowedEqLevelStrings(user) {
  if (!user) return LEVEL_ACCESS['1'];
  if (isAppAdminRole_(user.role)) {
    return ['1', '2', '3', '4', '5'];
  }
  var lv = String(user.level || '1').replace(/[^0-9]/g, '') || '1';
  return LEVEL_ACCESS[lv] || LEVEL_ACCESS['1'];
}

function buildStudioCalendarEmbedUrl(studioId) {
  var meta = STUDIO_CALENDAR_EMBEDS[studioId];
  if (!meta || !meta.calId) return '';
  var tz = 'Europe/Istanbul';
  // Tek encode (# → %23). Eski %23… değerleri çift encode ile Google 500 verebiliyordu; dates= bazı hesaplarda da hata üretiyordu.
  var q = 'src=' + encodeURIComponent(meta.calId) +
    '&ctz=' + encodeURIComponent(tz) + '&mode=WEEK&wkst=2&showTitle=0&showNav=1&showDate=1&showPrint=0&showTabs=1&showCalendars=0&showTz=0';
  if (meta.color) q += '&color=' + encodeURIComponent(String(meta.color).indexOf('#') === 0 ? meta.color : ('#' + String(meta.color).replace(/^#/, '')));
  return 'https://calendar.google.com/calendar/embed?' + q;
}

/**
 * Kullanıcı arayüzü: etkinlik başlığı/detayı gönderilmez; yalnızca meşgul zaman aralıkları (ms).
 * CalendarApp için takvim, scripti çalıştıran Google hesabıyla paylaşılmış olmalı (salt okunur yeterli).
 */
function getStudioCalendarBusyBlocksPublic(studioId, testToken) {
  try {
    var u = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!u) return { error: 'Not signed in.' };
    var acc = canUserAccessStudio(u, studioId);
    if (!acc || acc.ok !== true) return { error: 'Access denied.' };
    // Google Calendar integration disabled.
    return { ok: true, blocks: [], rangeStartMs: 0, rangeEndMs: 0, noCalendar: true, skipped: true };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message || String(e) };
  }
}
 
 
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// DEĞİŞİKLİK 5/6: getEquipmentData — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// testToken parametresi eklendi, kullanıcı seviyesine göre filtreleme
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 
function _equipmentUiCategoryMatchWords_(category, catMap, catMapUi) {
  var cat = String(category || '');
  var seen = {};
  var out = [];
  function pushArr(arr) {
    for (var i = 0; i < arr.length; i++) {
      var w = String(arr[i] || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!w || seen[w]) continue;
      seen[w] = true;
      out.push(w);
    }
  }
  pushArr(catMapUi[cat] || []);
  pushArr(catMap[cat] || []);
  var low = cat.toLowerCase();
  if (low && !seen[low]) out.push(low);
  return out;
}

function _equipmentLooksLikeOptics_(searchableText, id) {
  var txt = String(searchableText || '').toLowerCase();
  var eid = String(id || '').trim().toUpperCase();
  if (/^(LEN|LENS|OPT)/.test(eid)) return true;
  var opticsWords = ['lens', 'optik', 'optics', 'objektif', 'mercek', 'filtre', 'filter'];
  for (var i = 0; i < opticsWords.length; i++) {
    if (txt.indexOf(opticsWords[i]) >= 0) return true;
  }
  return false;
}

/**
 * Envanter kart gruplaması: "Ekipman türü" doluysa onunla; boşsa Equipment_ID harf öneki (SOUND40 → sound, CAM09 → cam).
 * Böylece tür hücresi boş kalsa da aynı kod ailesi tek kartta toplanır.
 */
function _equipmentGroupKeyAndTypeLabel_(rawTypeDisplay, equipmentId, equipmentName) {
  var raw = String(rawTypeDisplay || '').trim();
  var id = String(equipmentId || '').trim();
  var nm = String(equipmentName || '').trim();
  if (raw) {
    return { gkey: raw.toLowerCase(), typeLabel: raw };
  }
  var m = id.match(/^([A-Za-z]{2,24})/);
  if (m) {
    var letters = m[1];
    return { gkey: letters.toLowerCase(), typeLabel: letters.toUpperCase() };
  }
  var slug = nm.toLowerCase().replace(/\s+/g, '_').replace(/[^a-z0-9_]/g, '');
  return { gkey: slug ? ('__n__' + slug) : '__n__unknown', typeLabel: nm || id || 'Item' };
}

function tryGetEquipmentDataFromSupabase_(category, user) {
  if (!isSupabaseReadEnabled_()) return null;
  var isAdmin = !!(user && isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
  var allowedLevels = user ? getAllowedEqLevelStrings(enrichUserMatrix(user) || user) : LEVEL_ACCESS['1'];
  var invRes = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*' });
  var rows = invRes.rows || [];
  if (!rows.length) return [];
  var livePickupByEq = {};
  try {
    var rsSel = 'equipment_id,status,return_date,handover_date,updated_at,created_at';
    var rsRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(_supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_(), { select: rsSel, limit: 1000000 }).rows || [];
    function _isLivePickupStatus_(st) {
      var raw = String(st || '').trim();
      if (!raw) return false;
      var s = raw.toLowerCase();
      if (s.indexOf('cancel') >= 0 || s.indexOf('reject') >= 0 || s.indexOf('return') >= 0 || s.indexOf('complete') >= 0) return false;
      if (s === 'picked_up' || s === 'picked up' || s === 'picked') return true;
      if (s.indexOf('picked') >= 0 || s.indexOf('teslim al') >= 0 || s.indexOf('handover done') >= 0) return true;
      return false;
    }
    rsRows.forEach(function(r) {
      var eqId = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!eqId) return;
      var st = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim();
      if (!_isLivePickupStatus_(st)) return;
      var ret = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '')).trim();
      var ho = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['handover_date', 'start_dt', 'start_date'], '')).trim();
      var upd = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['updated_at', 'created_at'], '')).trim();
      var prev = livePickupByEq[eqId];
      if (!prev) {
        livePickupByEq[eqId] = { status: st, returnDate: ret, handoverDate: ho, updatedAt: upd };
        return;
      }
      var prevMs = Date.parse(String(prev.updatedAt || '')) || 0;
      var curMs = Date.parse(upd) || 0;
      if (curMs >= prevMs) livePickupByEq[eqId] = { status: st, returnDate: ret, handoverDate: ho, updatedAt: upd };
    });
  } catch (_rsJoinErr) {}

  var groupedItems = {};
  var catMap = {
    'Cameras': ['cam','kamera','camera','dslr','video'],
    'Optics': ['opt','lens','optik','optics','filtre','filter'],
    'Mic': ['mic','mikrofon','yaka','boom'],
    'Sound': ['snd','sound','ses','audio','recorder','mikser'],
    'Lighting': ['lgh','light','ışık','isik','lighting','led'],
    'Grip': ['grp','grip','tripod','ayak','stand','gimbal']
  };
  var catMapUi = {
    'Cam': ['cam','kamera','camera','dslr','video','sinema','ayna'],
    'Ops': ['opt','lens','optik','optics','filtre','filter','objektif','mercek'],
    'Sound': ['mic','mikrofon','yaka','boom','snd','sound','ses','audio','recorder','mikser','hoparlör','hoparlor'],
    'Light': ['lgh','light','ışık','isik','lighting','led','aydın','aydin'],
    'Grip': ['grp','grip','tripod','ayak','stand','gimbal','monopod','slider']
  };
  var EQ_LBL = {'TEMEL':'1','ORTA':'2','İLERİ':'3','ILERI':'3','PRO':'4','SENIOR':'5'};

  rows.forEach(function(row) {
    var id = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_id', 'id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim();
    var name = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_name', 'name'], '')).trim();
    if (!name && id) name = id;
    var rawTypeDisplay = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['equipment_type', 'type_desc', 'category', 'type'], '')).trim();
    var statusRaw = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['status'], 'AVAILABLE')).trim().toUpperCase();
    var photo = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['photo', 'image', 'photo_url'], '')).trim();
    var rDateVal = supaRowPick_(row, ['return_date', 'due_date', 'due_dt', 'return_dt'], '');
    var lvlCellFull = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['eq_level', 'equipment_level', 'level'], 'TEMEL')).trim();
    var conditionInVal = String(supaRowPick_(row, ['condition_in', 'condition'], '')).trim();
    var itemCat = rawTypeDisplay.toLowerCase();
    var searchableBlob = (rawTypeDisplay + ' ' + name + ' ' + id).toLowerCase();
    var lvlParsedRow = parseEquipmentLevelCell_(lvlCellFull);
    var eqLvl = EQ_LBL[lvlParsedRow.levelToken] || lvlParsedRow.levelToken || '1';

    if (!id || statusRaw === 'DELETED' || statusRaw === 'DAMAGED' || statusRaw === 'HIDDEN') return;
    if (isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)) return;
    if (!isAdmin && !allowedLevels.includes(String(eqLvl))) return;
    var livePickup = livePickupByEq[String(id).trim().toUpperCase()] || null;
    if (livePickup) {
      statusRaw = 'IN_USE';
      if (!rDateVal && livePickup.returnDate) rDateVal = livePickup.returnDate;
    }

    if (category && category !== 'All') {
      if (category === 'Light') {
        if (!/^LIGHT/i.test(id) || isLightingStandInventoryRow_(name, rawTypeDisplay, id)) return;
      } else if (category === 'Cam') {
        var camWords = _equipmentUiCategoryMatchWords_('Cam', catMap, catMapUi);
        var isCam = camWords.some(function(w) { return w && searchableBlob.indexOf(w) >= 0; });
        if (!isCam) return;
        if (_equipmentLooksLikeOptics_(searchableBlob, id)) return;
      } else if (category === 'Grip') {
        var matchWordsG = catMapUi['Grip'] || [];
        var isGrip = matchWordsG.some(function(w) { return searchableBlob.indexOf(w) >= 0; });
        if (!isGrip && !isLightingStandInventoryRow_(name, rawTypeDisplay, id)) return;
      } else {
        var matchWords = _equipmentUiCategoryMatchWords_(category, catMap, catMapUi);
        var isMatch = matchWords.some(function(w) { return w && searchableBlob.indexOf(w) >= 0; });
        if (!isMatch) return;
      }
    }

    var gkSupa = _equipmentGroupKeyAndTypeLabel_(rawTypeDisplay, id, name);
    var gkey = gkSupa.gkey;
    if (!groupedItems[gkey]) {
      groupedItems[gkey] = {
        id: id, groupKey: gkey, name: name, typeLabel: gkSupa.typeLabel, modelNames: [name],
        category: itemCat || category, status: 'Checked Out',
        image: photo || ("https://via.placeholder.com/400x200?text=" + encodeURIComponent(rawTypeDisplay || name)),
        stock: 0, outCount: 0, totalCount: 0, returnDate: '', returnSchedule: [], availableIds: [], eq_level: eqLvl, eq_max_per_reservation: null, details: [],
        earliestReturnMs: null, earliestReturnLabel: '', earliestReturnDateOnly: ''
      };
    } else if (groupedItems[gkey].modelNames.indexOf(name) < 0) {
      groupedItems[gkey].modelNames.push(name);
    }
    groupedItems[gkey].totalCount += 1;
    var tzInv = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul';
    var retParsed = null;
    if (rDateVal) {
      var dr0 = new Date(rDateVal);
      if (!isNaN(dr0.getTime())) retParsed = dr0;
    }
    var detailReturn = retParsed ? Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy / HH:mm') : (rDateVal ? String(rDateVal) : '');
    var detailStatus = (statusRaw === 'AVAILABLE' || statusRaw === 'MÜSAİT' || statusRaw === 'UYGUN') ? 'Available' : 'In Use';
    var hideConditionOnly = detailStatus === 'In Use' && (!user || !isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
    groupedItems[gkey].details.push({
      equipment_id: id,
      name: name,
      photo: (photo && photo !== groupedItems[gkey].image) ? photo : '',
      status: detailStatus,
      returnDate: detailReturn || '–',
      returnDateMs: retParsed ? retParsed.getTime() : null,
      conditionIn: hideConditionOnly ? '–' : (conditionInVal || '–')
    });
    if (detailStatus === 'Available') {
      groupedItems[gkey].stock += 1;
      groupedItems[gkey].availableIds.push(id);
      groupedItems[gkey].status = 'Available';
    } else {
      groupedItems[gkey].outCount += 1;
      if (retParsed) {
        var ms = retParsed.getTime();
        if (groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs == null || ms < groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs) {
          groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs = ms;
          groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnLabel = Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy / HH:mm');
          groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnDateOnly = Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy');
        }
      }
      if (detailReturn) {
        if (!groupedItems[gkey].returnDate) groupedItems[gkey].returnDate = detailReturn;
        groupedItems[gkey].returnSchedule.push(detailReturn);
      }
    }
  });
  return Object.values(groupedItems);
}

function getEquipmentData(category, testToken) {
  var t0Eq = Date.now();
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    var uid = String((user && user.id) || '');
    var role = String((user && user.role) || '');
    var lvlSig = user ? String(getAllowedEqLevelStrings(user).join(',')) : '1';
    var kEq = _cacheKey_('equipmentData', [String(category || 'All'), uid, role, lvlSig]);
    var cEq = _cacheGetJson_(kEq);
    if (cEq) {
      _debugSourceLog_('getEquipmentData', 'cache', t0Eq, { category: String(category || 'All'), uid: uid || '-', count: cEq.length || 0 });
      return cEq;
    }
    try {
      var sbEq = tryGetEquipmentDataFromSupabase_(category, user);
      if (sbEq && !sbEq.error) {
        if (_supabaseStrictReadEnabled_()) {
          _cachePutJson_(kEq, sbEq, 180);
          _debugSourceLog_('getEquipmentData', 'supabase-strict', t0Eq, { category: String(category || 'All'), uid: uid || '-', count: sbEq.length || 0 });
          return sbEq;
        }
        // Inventory ekranında boş liste yerine her zaman Sheet fallback dene.
        // Bu sayede Supabase tablo/izin/şema boşsa kullanıcı "No items" görmez.
        if (!sbEq.length) {
          _debugSourceLog_('getEquipmentData', 'supabase-empty-fallback-sheet', t0Eq, {
            category: String(category || 'All'),
            uid: uid || '-',
            allowEmpty: _allowEmptySupabaseRead_()
          });
        } else {
          _cachePutJson_(kEq, sbEq, 180);
          _debugSourceLog_('getEquipmentData', 'supabase', t0Eq, { category: String(category || 'All'), uid: uid || '-', count: sbEq.length || 0 });
          return sbEq;
        }
      }
    } catch (_sbErrEq) {}
    var isAdmin = false;
    var allowedLevels = LEVEL_ACCESS['1'];
    var uEqFilter = user ? (enrichUserMatrix(user) || user) : null;
    if (user) {
      isAdmin = (isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
      allowedLevels = getAllowedEqLevelStrings(uEqFilter);
    }
    
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY); 
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var headers = data[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var rows = data.slice(1);
    
    var idxID = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_id") || h.includes("ekipman_id") || h === "id"; });
    var idxName = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("name") || h.includes("adı"); });
    var idxCat = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("türü") || h.includes("type") || h.includes("category"); });
    var idxStatus = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("status") || h.includes("durum"); });
    var idxPhoto = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("photo") || h.includes("foto"); });
    var idxReturn = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("return") || h.includes("due") || h.includes("iade"); });
    var idxLevel = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("ekipman seviyesi") || h.includes("seviye") || h.includes("eq_level"); });
    var idxConditionIn = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("condition_in") || h.includes("condition in") || h.includes("durum_in") || h.includes("giris_durum"); });
 
    var EQ_LBL = {'TEMEL':'1','ORTA':'2','İLERİ':'3','ILERI':'3','PRO':'4','SENIOR':'5'};
    var pickedByEq = {};
    function __isPickedLikeStatus_(st) {
      var s = String(st || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      if (!s) return false;
      if (s.indexOf('cancel') >= 0 || s.indexOf('reject') >= 0 || s.indexOf('return') >= 0 || s.indexOf('complete') >= 0) return false;
      return s === 'picked up' || s === 'picked_up' || s === 'picked' || s.indexOf('picked') >= 0 || s.indexOf('teslim al') >= 0;
    }
    try {
      if (isSupabaseReadEnabled_()) {
        var sbPickRows = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(_supaEquipmentReservationTableCandidates_(), {
          select: 'equipment_id,status,return_date,updated_at,created_at',
          limit: 1000000
        }).rows || [];
        sbPickRows.forEach(function(rr) {
          var eq = String(supaRowPick_(rr, ['equipment_id', 'item_id', 'eq_id'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
          if (!eq) return;
          var st = String(supaRowPick_(rr, ['status'], '')).trim();
          if (!__isPickedLikeStatus_(st)) return;
          var prev = pickedByEq[eq];
          var ret = String(supaRowPick_(rr, ['return_date', 'end_dt', 'end_date'], '')).trim();
          var upd = String(supaRowPick_(rr, ['updated_at', 'created_at'], '')).trim();
          if (!prev || (Date.parse(upd) || 0) >= (Date.parse(String(prev.updatedAt || '')) || 0)) {
            pickedByEq[eq] = { returnDate: ret, updatedAt: upd };
          }
        });
      }
    } catch (_sbPickErr) {}
    var groupedItems = {};
    var catMap = { 
      'Cameras': ['cam','kamera','camera','dslr','video'], 
      'Optics': ['opt','lens','optik','optics','filtre','filter'], 
      'Mic': ['mic','mikrofon','yaka','boom'], 
      'Sound': ['snd','sound','ses','audio','recorder','mikser'], 
      'Lighting':['lgh','light','ışık','isik','lighting','led'], 
      'Grip': ['grp','grip','tripod','ayak','stand','gimbal'] 
    };
    /** index.html filter-btn data-category ile aynı anahtarlar */
    var catMapUi = {
      'Cam': ['cam','kamera','camera','dslr','video','sinema','ayna'],
      'Ops': ['opt','lens','optik','optics','filtre','filter','objektif','mercek'],
      'Sound': ['mic','mikrofon','yaka','boom','snd','sound','ses','audio','recorder','mikser','hoparlör','hoparlor'],
      'Light': ['lgh','light','ışık','isik','lighting','led','aydın','aydin'],
      'Grip': ['grp','grip','tripod','ayak','stand','gimbal','monopod','slider']
    };
    
    rows.forEach(function(row) {
      var name = String(idxName !== -1 ? row[idxName] : row[2]).trim(); 
      var rawTypeDisplay = String(idxCat !== -1 ? row[idxCat] : row[3]).trim();
      var itemCat = rawTypeDisplay.toLowerCase(); 
      var statusRaw = String(idxStatus !== -1 ? row[idxStatus] : row[4]).trim().toUpperCase(); 
      var id = String(idxID !== -1 ? row[idxID] : row[1]).trim(); 
      var pickedMeta = pickedByEq[String(id || '').trim().toUpperCase()] || null;
      if (pickedMeta) statusRaw = 'IN_USE';
      var photo = String(idxPhoto !== -1 ? row[idxPhoto] : row[15] || '').trim();
      var lvlCellFull = String(idxLevel !== -1 ? row[idxLevel] : row[16] || 'TEMEL').trim();
      var lvlParsedRow = parseEquipmentLevelCell_(lvlCellFull);
      var eqLvl = EQ_LBL[lvlParsedRow.levelToken] || lvlParsedRow.levelToken || '1';
      
      if (!name || statusRaw === 'DELETED' || statusRaw === 'DAMAGED' || statusRaw === 'HIDDEN') return;
      if (isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)) return;
      
      // ═══ SEVİYE FİLTRESİ ═══
      // Admin olmayan kullanıcılar: seviye 5 ekipmanları göremez (sheet'te 5 yoksa)
      // Kendi seviyesinin üstündeki ekipmanları göremez
      if (!isAdmin) {
        if (!allowedLevels.includes(eqLvl) && !_hasActiveSpecialEquipmentAccessForItem_(uEqFilter, id)) return;
      }
      
      // Kategori filtresi (All = tüm satırlar; Light = yalnızca Equipment_ID "LIGHT…" ve sehpa değil; Grip = sehpa dahil)
      if (category && category !== "All") {
        if (category === 'Light') {
          if (!/^LIGHT/i.test(String(id).trim()) || isLightingStandInventoryRow_(name, rawTypeDisplay, id)) return;
        } else if (category === 'Cam') {
          var camWords2 = _equipmentUiCategoryMatchWords_('Cam', catMap, catMapUi);
          var hay2 = (itemCat + ' ' + String(name || '').toLowerCase() + ' ' + String(id || '').toLowerCase());
          var isCam2 = camWords2.some(function(w) { return hay2.indexOf(w) >= 0; });
          if (!isCam2) return;
          if (_equipmentLooksLikeOptics_(hay2, id)) return;
        } else if (category === 'Grip') {
          var matchWordsG = catMapUi['Grip'] || [];
          var isGrip = matchWordsG.some(function(w) { return itemCat.includes(w) || id.toLowerCase().includes(w); });
          if (!isGrip && !isLightingStandInventoryRow_(name, rawTypeDisplay, id)) return;
        } else {
          var matchWords = catMap[category] || catMapUi[category] || [String(category).toLowerCase()];
          var isMatch = matchWords.some(function(w) { return itemCat.includes(w) || id.toLowerCase().includes(w); });
          if (!isMatch) return;
        }
      }
      
      var gkSh = _equipmentGroupKeyAndTypeLabel_(rawTypeDisplay, id, name);
      var gkey = gkSh.gkey;
      if (!groupedItems[gkey]) { 
        groupedItems[gkey] = { 
          id: id,
          groupKey: gkey,
          name: name,
          typeLabel: gkSh.typeLabel,
          modelNames: [name],
          category: itemCat || category, 
          status: 'Checked Out', 
          image: photo || "https://via.placeholder.com/400x200?text=" + encodeURIComponent(rawTypeDisplay || name), 
          stock: 0, outCount: 0, totalCount: 0, returnDate: '', returnSchedule: [], availableIds: [], eq_level: eqLvl, eq_max_per_reservation: null, details: [],
          earliestReturnMs: null, earliestReturnLabel: '', earliestReturnDateOnly: ''
        }; 
      } else if (groupedItems[gkey].modelNames.indexOf(name) < 0) {
        groupedItems[gkey].modelNames.push(name);
      }
      if (lvlParsedRow.maxN != null) {
        if (groupedItems[gkey].eq_max_per_reservation == null) groupedItems[gkey].eq_max_per_reservation = lvlParsedRow.maxN;
        else groupedItems[gkey].eq_max_per_reservation = Math.min(groupedItems[gkey].eq_max_per_reservation, lvlParsedRow.maxN);
      }
      groupedItems[gkey].totalCount += 1; 
      var rDateVal = idxReturn !== -1 ? row[idxReturn] : row[8];
      if ((!rDateVal || String(rDateVal).trim() === '') && pickedMeta && pickedMeta.returnDate) rDateVal = pickedMeta.returnDate;
      var tzInv = Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul';
      var retParsed = null;
      if (rDateVal) {
        var dr0 = new Date(rDateVal);
        if (!isNaN(dr0.getTime())) retParsed = dr0;
      }
      var detailReturn = '';
      var detailReturnMs = NaN;
      if (retParsed) {
        detailReturnMs = retParsed.getTime();
        detailReturn = Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy / HH:mm');
      } else if (rDateVal) {
        detailReturn = String(rDateVal);
      }
      var detailStatus = (statusRaw === 'AVAILABLE' || statusRaw === 'MÜSAİT' || statusRaw === 'UYGUN') ? 'Available' : 'In Use';
      var conditionInVal = String(idxConditionIn !== -1 ? row[idxConditionIn] : '').trim();
      var hideConditionOnly = detailStatus === 'In Use' && (!user || !isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
      groupedItems[gkey].details.push({
        equipment_id: id,
        name: name,
        photo: (photo && photo !== groupedItems[gkey].image) ? photo : '',
        status: detailStatus,
        returnDate: detailReturn || '–',
        returnDateMs: !isNaN(detailReturnMs) ? detailReturnMs : null,
        conditionIn: hideConditionOnly ? '–' : (conditionInVal || '–')
      });
      
      if (statusRaw === 'AVAILABLE' || statusRaw === 'MÜSAİT' || statusRaw === 'UYGUN') { 
        groupedItems[gkey].stock += 1; 
        groupedItems[gkey].availableIds.push(id);
        groupedItems[gkey].status = 'Available'; 
      } else if (statusRaw === 'IN_USE' || statusRaw === 'IN USE' || statusRaw === 'KULLANIMDA' || statusRaw === 'DIŞARIDA') { 
        groupedItems[gkey].outCount += 1; 
        if (retParsed) {
          var ms = retParsed.getTime();
          if (groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs == null || ms < groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs) {
            groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnMs = ms;
            groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnLabel = Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy / HH:mm');
            groupedItems[gkey].earliestReturnDateOnly = Utilities.formatDate(retParsed, tzInv, 'dd.MM.yyyy');
          }
        }
        if (detailReturn) {
          if (!groupedItems[gkey].returnDate) groupedItems[gkey].returnDate = detailReturn;
          groupedItems[gkey].returnSchedule.push(detailReturn);
        } else if (rDateVal) {
          groupedItems[gkey].returnSchedule.push(String(rDateVal));
        }
      }
    });
    var outEq = Object.values(groupedItems);
    _cachePutJson_(kEq, outEq, 180);
    _debugSourceLog_('getEquipmentData', 'sheet', t0Eq, { category: String(category || 'All'), uid: uid || '-', count: outEq.length || 0 });
    return outEq;
  } catch (e) { 
    return { error: e.message }; 
  }
}
 
 
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// DEĞİŞİKLİK 6/6: createEquipmentReservation — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// Eklenen: sepetteki her ekipmanın seviyesini kullanıcı yetkisiyle kontrol
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function mapInventoryTypeToBookingCategory(typeRaw, equipmentId, equipmentName) {
  var id = String(equipmentId || '').toLowerCase();
  var nm = String(equipmentName || '').toLowerCase();
  var t = String(typeRaw || '').toLowerCase();
  if (isLightingStandInventoryRow_(nm, t, id)) return 'Grip';
  if (/cam|kamera|dslr|video|sinema|ayna/.test(t)) return 'Camera';
  if (/opt|lens|filtre|filter|objektif|mercek/.test(t)) return 'Optics';
  if (/mic|mikrofon|yaka|boom|snd|sound|ses|audio|recorder|mikser|hoparlör|hoparlor/.test(t)) return 'Sound';
  if (/light|led|ışık|isik|lgh|aydın|aydin/.test(t)) return 'Lighting';
  if (/grip|tripod|ayak|stand|gimbal|grp|monopod|slider/.test(t)) return 'Grip';
  return 'General';
}
 
function createEquipmentReservation(cartIds, startDt, endDt, testToken, purpose) {
  try {
    var user = resolveCurrentUser(testToken);
    if (!user) return { error: 'User not found. Please sign in.' };
    try { _assertUserNotAppBlocked_(user); } catch (bx) { return { error: bx.message || String(bx) }; }
    var purposeTrim = String(purpose || '').trim();
    if (!purposeTrim) return { error: 'Project description is required.' };
    
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var userId = user.id || user.email;
    var userName = user.name || user.email.split('@')[0].toUpperCase();
    var isAdmin = (isAppAdminRole_(user.role));
    var uEq = enrichUserMatrix(user) || user;
    var allowedLevels = getAllowedEqLevelStrings(uEq);
 
    var resSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var invData = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY).getDataRange().getValues();
    var invHeaders = invData[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var idxInvID = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_id") || h === "id"; });
    var idxInvName = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_name") || h.includes("name"); });
    var idxInvType = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("ekipman türü") || h.includes("type"); });
    var idxInvStatus = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("status") || h.includes("durum"); });
    var idxInvLevel = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("ekipman seviyesi") || h.includes("seviye") || h.includes("eq_level"); });
    var idxInvSid = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("student_id"); });
    
    var EQ_LBL = {'TEMEL':'1','ORTA':'2','İLERİ':'3','ILERI':'3','PRO':'4','SENIOR':'5'};
    var resGroupId = 'RES-' + Utilities.getUuid().substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
    var errors = [];
    var nameCartCaps = {};
 
    // ═══ SEPET KONTROLÜ ═══
    cartIds.forEach(function(id) {
      var eqRow = null;
      var searchId = String(id).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (!isAdmin && isStudioKeyEquipmentId(searchId)) {
        errors.push(searchId + ': Stüdyo anahtarları bu ekrandan rezerve edilemez.');
        return;
      }
      for (var i = 1; i < invData.length; i++) {
        var cellId = String(idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[i][idxInvID] : invData[i][1]).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (cellId === searchId) { eqRow = invData[i]; break; }
      }
      
      if (!eqRow) {
        errors.push(searchId + ': Equipment not found.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Availability check
      var eqStatus = String(idxInvStatus !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvStatus] : eqRow[4]).trim().toUpperCase();
      if (eqStatus !== 'AVAILABLE' && eqStatus !== 'MÜSAİT' && eqStatus !== 'UYGUN') {
        var eqName = String(idxInvName !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvName] : eqRow[2]).trim();
        errors.push(eqName + ': Not available right now.');
        return;
      }
      
      // Access level check
      if (!isAdmin) {
        var lvlCellCart = String(idxInvLevel !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvLevel] : eqRow[16] || 'TEMEL').trim();
        var lvlParsedCart = parseEquipmentLevelCell_(lvlCellCart);
        var eqLvl = EQ_LBL[lvlParsedCart.levelToken] || lvlParsedCart.levelToken || '1';
        
        if (!allowedLevels.includes(eqLvl) && !_hasActiveSpecialEquipmentAccessForItem_(uEq, searchId)) {
          var eqNameLvl = String(idxInvName !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvName] : eqRow[2]).trim();
          var levelNames = {'1':'Basic','2':'Intermediate','3':'Advanced','4':'Pro','5':'Senior'};
          var userLevelNum = parseInt(String(user.level || '1'), 10) || 1;
          errors.push(eqNameLvl + ': You are not authorized for Level ' + (levelNames[eqLvl]||eqLvl) + ' equipment. (Your current level: ' + userLevelNum + ')');
          return;
        }
        var nmKey = String(idxInvName !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvName] : eqRow[2]).trim().toLowerCase();
        var capN = perReservationNameCapFromLevelParsed_(lvlParsedCart);
        if (!nameCartCaps[nmKey]) nameCartCaps[nmKey] = { count: 0, caps: [] };
        nameCartCaps[nmKey].count++;
        if (capN != null) nameCartCaps[nmKey].caps.push(capN);
      }
    });
    
    // Hata varsa durdur
    if (errors.length > 0) {
      return { error: errors.join(' | ') };
    }

    if (!isAdmin) {
      for (var nk in nameCartCaps) {
        var ng = nameCartCaps[nk];
        if (ng.caps.length) {
          var minC = Math.min.apply(null, ng.caps);
          if (ng.count > minC) {
            return { error: 'Equipment "' + nk + '": at most ' + minC + ' unit(s) per reservation (Ekipman Seviyesi MAX:N). You have ' + ng.count + ' in the cart.' };
          }
        }
      }
      var loanByCat = countUserOnHandLoansByBookingCategory_(user, invData, idxInvID, idxInvName, idxInvType, idxInvStatus, idxInvSid);
      var catMax = equipmentReservationCategoryMax_();
      var cartByCat = { Camera: 0, Optics: 0, Sound: 0, Lighting: 0, Grip: 0, General: 0 };
      for (var cc = 0; cc < cartIds.length; cc++) {
        var cid0 = String(cartIds[cc]).trim().toUpperCase();
        var eqRow0 = null;
        for (var ii = 1; ii < invData.length; ii++) {
          var cId = String(idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[ii][idxInvID] : invData[ii][1]).trim().toUpperCase();
          if (cId === cid0) { eqRow0 = invData[ii]; break; }
        }
        if (!eqRow0) continue;
        var tyC = String(idxInvType >= 0 ? eqRow0[idxInvType] : eqRow0[3]).trim();
        var nmC = String(idxInvName >= 0 ? eqRow0[idxInvName] : eqRow0[2]).trim();
        var catC = mapInventoryTypeToBookingCategory(tyC, cid0, nmC);
        cartByCat[catC] = (cartByCat[catC] || 0) + 1;
      }
      var catKeys = ['Camera', 'Optics', 'Sound', 'Lighting', 'Grip', 'General'];
      for (var ckI = 0; ckI < catKeys.length; ckI++) {
        var ckk = catKeys[ckI];
        var maxK = catMax[ckk] != null ? catMax[ckk] : 5;
        var have = loanByCat[ckk] || 0;
        var add = cartByCat[ckk] || 0;
        if (have + add > maxK) {
          return { error: 'Category limit: you already have ' + have + ' ' + ckk + ' item(s) on loan. With this cart (' + add + ' new), the maximum is ' + maxK + '. Return items or reduce the cart.' };
        }
      }
    }

    try {
      validateBookingDateTime('equipment', startDt, endDt, user);
    } catch (ve) {
      var vm = ve.message || String(ve);
      if (vm.indexOf('EQUIPMENT_MAX_DAYS:') === 0) {
        var md = vm.split(':')[1] || '2';
        return { error: 'EQUIPMENT_MAX_DAYS:' + md };
      }
      return { error: vm };
    }

    for (var c = 0; c < cartIds.length; c++) {
      var cid = String(cartIds[c]).trim().toUpperCase();
      var av = reservationsCheckAvailability({ item_id: cid, start_dt: startDt, end_dt: endDt });
      if (!av.available) return { error: 'Scheduling conflict for ' + cid + '.' };
    }
 
    // ═══ REZERVASYON OLUŞTUR ═══
    var reservedNames = [];
    var upsertRows = [];
    var tsRes = now();
    cartIds.forEach(function(id) {
      var eqRow = null;
      var searchId = String(id).trim().toUpperCase();
      for (var i = 1; i < invData.length; i++) {
        var cellId = String(idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[i][idxInvID] : invData[i][1]).trim().toUpperCase();
        if (cellId === searchId) { eqRow = invData[i]; break; }
      }
      var eqName = eqRow ? String(idxInvName !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvName] : eqRow[2]).trim() : 'Bilinmeyen';
      var eqType = eqRow ? String(idxInvType !== -1 ? eqRow[idxInvType] : eqRow[3]).trim() : '';

      var rowGuest = {
        reservation_group_id: resGroupId,
        equipment_id: searchId,
        equipment_name: eqName,
        equipment_category: eqType,
        student_id: userId,
        student_name: userName,
        handover_date: startDt,
        return_date: endDt,
        status: 'Pending',
        approver_email: '',
        purpose: purposeTrim,
        created_at: tsRes,
        updated_at: tsRes
      };
      upsertRows.push({
        equipment_id: searchId,
        equipment_name: eqName,
        equipment_category: eqType,
        student_id: userId,
        student_name: userName,
        handover_date: startDt,
        return_date: endDt,
        status: 'Pending',
        approver_email: '',
        reservation_group_id: resGroupId,
        purpose: purposeTrim
      });
      reservedNames.push(eqName + ' (' + searchId + ')');
      try { addRow(resSheet, rowGuest, RESH); } catch (_sheetWriteErr) {}
    });

    if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_()) {
      var primaryUp = _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsPrimary_(upsertRows);
      if (!primaryUp || !primaryUp.ok) {
        return { error: 'Supabase reservation write failed.' };
      }
    } else {
      for (var su = 0; su < upsertRows.length; su++) {
        trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_(upsertRows[su]);
      }
    }
 
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    if (user.email && String(user.email).indexOf('@') >= 0) {
      sendReservationCreatedMail_(String(user.email), userName, resGroupId, startDt, endDt, reservedNames);
    }
    return { success: true, resId: resGroupId };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: 'İşlem hatası: ' + e.message };
  }
}

function _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_() {
  try {
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var headers = data[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var rows = data.slice(1);

    var idxID = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_id") || h === "id" || h.includes("ekipman_id"); });
    var idxName = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_name") || h.includes("name") || h.includes("ekipman adı"); });
    var idxType = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("ekipman türü") || h.includes("type_desc") || h.includes("kategori"); });
    var idxStatus = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("status") || h.includes("durum"); });
    var idxPhoto = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("photo") || h.includes("foto"); });
    var idxLevel = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("ekipman seviyesi") || h.includes("seviye") || h.includes("eq_level"); });
    var idxLoc = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h === 'location' || h.indexOf('konum') >= 0; });
    if (idxLoc === -1 && headers.length > 11) idxLoc = 11;
    var idxResp = headers.findIndex(function(h) { return h.indexOf('responsible') >= 0 || h.indexOf('sorumlu') >= 0; });
    if (idxResp === -1 && headers.length > 17) idxResp = 17;

    return rows.filter(function(r) { 
      var idVal = idxID !== -1 ? r[idxID] : r[1]; 
      return idVal && String(idVal).trim() !== ''; 
    }).map(function(r) {
      var rawStatus = idxStatus !== -1 ? r[idxStatus] : r[4];
      var st = String(rawStatus || 'AVAILABLE').trim().toUpperCase();
      if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
      if (st === 'KULLANIMDA' || st === 'DIŞARIDA') st = 'IN_USE';

      return { 
        id: String(idxID !== -1 ? r[idxID] : r[1]).trim(), 
        name: String(idxName !== -1 ? r[idxName] : r[2]).trim(), 
        type: String(idxType !== -1 ? r[idxType] : r[3]).trim(), 
        status: st, 
        photo: String(idxPhoto !== -1 ? r[idxPhoto] : r[15] || '').trim(), 
        level: String(idxLevel !== -1 ? r[idxLevel] : r[16] || '1').trim(),
        locationText: idxLoc >= 0 ? String(r[idxLoc] || '').trim() : '',
        responsibleText: idxResp >= 0 ? String(r[idxResp] || '').trim() : ''
      };
    });
  } catch(e) { return []; }
}

/** Tam envanter — yalnızca yetkili admin çağrısı (google.script.run). Sunucu içi: _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_(). */
function getAdminEquipmentData(adminToken) {
  if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return [];
  return _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_();
}

/**
 * Admin arayüzü: envanter sekmesinde stüdyo anahtarları listelenmez; Hızlı Çıkış’ta isStudioKey ile gelir.
 */
function getAdminEquipmentDataForUi(adminToken) {
  if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return [];
  var rows = supabaseSelectFirstNonEmptyTable_(['inventory_items', 'inventory', 'equipment_inventory'], { select: '*' }).rows || [];
  return rows.map(function(r) {
    var id = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['id', 'equipment_id'], '')).trim();
    var st = String(supaRowPick_(r, ['status'], '')).trim().toUpperCase();
    if (st === 'MÜSAİT' || st === 'UYGUN') st = 'AVAILABLE';
    return {
      id: id,
      name: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['name', 'equipment_name'], '')).trim(),
      type: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['type_desc', 'equipment_type', 'category'], '')).trim(),
      status: st,
      locationText: '',
      responsibleText: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['assigned_name', 'assigned_to'], '')).trim(),
      level: String(supaRowPick_(r, ['eq_level', 'required_level'], '1')).trim(),
      isStudioKey: isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)
    };
  });
}
