// CODE.GS — PDF TABLO DEĞİŞİKLİKLERİ (3 FONKSİYON)
// Her birini Code.gs'de bulup DEĞİŞTİRİN.
// ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 1/3: generateDeliveryPDF — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function generateDeliveryPDF(templateId, dataObj) {
  try {
    var folder;
    try { folder = DriveApp.getFolderById(CONFIG.STUDIO_PDF_FOLDER_ID); } catch(e) { folder = DriveApp.getRootFolder(); }
    var template = DriveApp.getFileById(templateId);
    var fileName = 'TeslimFormu_' + (dataObj.Student_Name || 'Bilinmiyor') + '_' + Utilities.formatDate(new Date(), "GMT+3", "ddMMyy");
    
    var copy = template.makeCopy(fileName, folder);
    var doc = DocumentApp.openById(copy.getId());
    var body = doc.getBody();

    function _placeholderVariantsForKey_(key) {
      var raw = String(key || '').trim();
      if (!raw) return [];
      var out = {};
      function add(v) { if (v) out[v] = true; }
      var spaceVer = raw.replace(/_/g, ' ');
      var underVer = raw.replace(/\s+/g, '_');
      add(raw);
      add(spaceVer);
      add(underVer);
      // Türkçe karakter toleransı (şablonda ASCII yazılmış olabilir)
      function trToAscii(s) {
        return String(s || '')
          .replace(/İ/g, 'I').replace(/İ/g, 'I')
          .replace(/ı/g, 'i').replace(/Ş/g, 'S').replace(/ş/g, 's')
          .replace(/Ğ/g, 'G').replace(/ğ/g, 'g').replace(/Ü/g, 'U').replace(/ü/g, 'u')
          .replace(/Ö/g, 'O').replace(/ö/g, 'o').replace(/Ç/g, 'C').replace(/ç/g, 'c');
      }
      add(trToAscii(raw));
      add(trToAscii(spaceVer));
      add(trToAscii(underVer));
      return Object.keys(out);
    }

    // Standart alanları değiştir (Equipment_List hariç)
    for (var key in dataObj) {
     if (key === 'Equipment_Items' || key === 'Equipment_List') continue;
      var val = String(dataObj[key] || '-');
      var vars = _placeholderVariantsForKey_(key);
      for (var vi = 0; vi < vars.length; vi++) {
        body.replaceText('\\{\\{' + vars[vi] + '\\}\\}', val);
      }
    }

    // ═══ EKİPMAN TABLOSU OLUŞTUR ═══
    var eqListPattern = '(?i)\\{\\{\\s*\\(?\\s*equipment[ _]list\\s*\\)?\\s*\\}\\}';
    var sr = body.findText(eqListPattern);
    var parentIndex = -1;
    if (sr) {
      try {
        var element = sr.getElement();
        var p = element ? element.getParent() : null;
        parentIndex = p ? body.getChildIndex(p) : -1;
      } catch (_eIx) { parentIndex = -1; }
    }
    // Placeholder temizliği ({{Equipment_List}}, {{Equipment List}}, {{(Equipment_List)}} vb.)
    body.replaceText(eqListPattern, '');

    var items = Array.isArray(dataObj.Equipment_Items) ? dataObj.Equipment_Items.slice() : [];
    if (!items.length) {
      var rawList = String(dataObj.Equipment_List || '').trim();
      if (rawList) {
        rawList.split(/\r?\n|,/).forEach(function(line) {
          var t = String(line || '').trim();
          if (!t) return;
          items.push({ id: '', name: t, conditionOut: 'Excellent' });
        });
      }
    }

    if (items.length > 0) {
      // Tablo oluştur: başlık + veri satırları
      var tableData = [];
      tableData.push(['Ekipman ID', 'Ekipman Adı', 'Çıkış Durumu', 'İade Durumu']);
      items.forEach(function(item) {
        tableData.push([
          item.id || '',
          item.name || '',
          item.conditionOut || 'Excellent',
          '' // condition_in (boş)
        ]);
      });

      // Placeholder yeri bulunamazsa tabloyu sona ekle
      var table = (parentIndex >= 0) ? body.insertTable(parentIndex + 1, tableData) : body.appendTable(tableData);

      // Tablo stili
      var headerRow = table.getRow(0);
      for (var h = 0; h < headerRow.getNumCells(); h++) {
        var headerCell = headerRow.getCell(h);
        headerCell.setBackgroundColor('#333333');
        var headerText = headerCell.editAsText();
        headerText.setBold(true);
        headerText.setForegroundColor('#FFFFFF');
        headerText.setFontSize(9);
        headerText.setFontFamily('Inter');
      }
      for (var r = 1; r < table.getNumRows(); r++) {
        var row = table.getRow(r);
        var bgColor = (r % 2 === 0) ? '#F9FAFB' : '#FFFFFF';
        for (var c = 0; c < row.getNumCells(); c++) {
          var cell = row.getCell(c);
          cell.setBackgroundColor(bgColor);
          var cellText = cell.editAsText();
          cellText.setFontSize(9);
          cellText.setFontFamily('Inter');
          if (c === 3) {
            cell.setText('________________');
            cell.editAsText().setForegroundColor('#CCCCCC');
          }
        }
      }
      var tableWidth = 500;
      table.setColumnWidth(0, Math.round(tableWidth * 0.15));
      table.setColumnWidth(1, Math.round(tableWidth * 0.40));
      table.setColumnWidth(2, Math.round(tableWidth * 0.20));
      table.setColumnWidth(3, Math.round(tableWidth * 0.25));
      table.setBorderColor('#E5E7EB');
      table.setBorderWidth(1);
    }

    doc.saveAndClose();
    Utilities.sleep(2000);

    var pdfBlob = copy.getAs('application/pdf');
    var pdfFile = folder.createFile(pdfBlob);
    pdfFile.setSharing(DriveApp.Access.ANYONE_WITH_LINK, DriveApp.Permission.VIEW);
    copy.setTrashed(true);

    return pdfFile.getUrl();
  } catch (e) { 
    throw new Error("PDF Hatası: " + e.message); 
  }
}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 2/3: adminProcessPartialCheckout — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

/** Sayfa1 / envanter başlığından Condition-Out sütununu bulur (condition_in ile karışmaz). */
function findInventoryConditionOutColumnIndex_(invHeaders) {
  var i, h;
  for (i = 0; i < invHeaders.length; i++) {
    h = String(invHeaders[i] || '').toLowerCase().replace(/-/g, '_');
    if (h.indexOf('condition_out') >= 0) return i;
  }
  for (i = 0; i < invHeaders.length; i++) {
    h = String(invHeaders[i] || '').toLowerCase();
    if (h.indexOf('condition') >= 0 && h.indexOf('out') >= 0 && h.indexOf('in') < 0) return i;
  }
  for (i = 0; i < invHeaders.length; i++) {
    h = String(invHeaders[i] || '').toLowerCase();
    if (h.indexOf('durum') >= 0 && (h.indexOf('cik') >= 0 || h.indexOf('çık') >= 0)) return i;
  }
  return -1;
}

function normalizeAdminCheckoutCondition_(raw) {
  var s = String(raw || '').trim();
  if (s === 'Excellent' || s === 'Minor Scratch' || s === 'Missing Part') return s;
  var low = s.toLowerCase();
  if (low.indexOf('minor') >= 0 && low.indexOf('scratch') >= 0) return 'Minor Scratch';
  if (low.indexOf('missing') >= 0) return 'Missing Part';
  return 'Excellent';
}

function adminProcessPartialCheckout(resId, itemIds, studioHandoverNote, checkoutConditionMap, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) throw new Error('Yetkisiz.');
    var handoverTxt = studioHandoverNote != null ? String(studioHandoverNote).trim() : '';
    if (!handoverTxt) handoverTxt = 'Sorunsuz-No Issues';
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var studioRow = null;
    try {
      studioRow = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) {
        return String(r.id || '').trim() === String(resId || '').trim();
      }) || null;
    } catch (_eSt1) {}
    if (studioRow) {
      return adminStudioProcessKeyHandover_(resId, itemIds, handoverTxt);
    }
    var resSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var invSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.INVENTORY);

    var resData = resSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colCo = _reservationSheetColIxs_(resData);
    var invData = invSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var invHeaders = invData[0].map(function(h) { return String(h).trim().toLowerCase(); });
    var idxInvID = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_id") || h === "id" || h.includes("ekipman_id"); });
    var idxInvName = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("equipment_name") || h.includes("name") || h.includes("adı"); });
    var idxInvType = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("type_desc") || h.includes("type") || h.includes("kategori") || h.includes("ekipman türü"); });
    var idxInvStatus = invHeaders.findIndex(function(h) { return h.includes("status") || h.includes("durum"); });
    var idxCondOut = findInventoryConditionOutColumnIndex_(invHeaders);
    var resIdTrimCo = String(resId || '').trim();

    var userEmail = "", userName = "", startDt = "", endDt = "";
    var equipmentItems = [];
    var hasStudioKey = false;
    var firstTemplate = null;
    for (var rt = 1; rt < resData.length; rt++) {
      if (String(resData[rt][colCo.group]).trim() === resIdTrimCo) {
        firstTemplate = {
          group: String(resData[rt][colCo.group] || '').trim(),
          student: String(resData[rt][colCo.student] || '').trim(),
          studentName: String(resData[rt][colCo.studentName] || '').trim(),
          handover: resData[rt][colCo.handover],
          ret: resData[rt][colCo.ret],
          approver: String(resData[rt][colCo.approver] || '').trim(),
          purpose: String(colCo.purpose >= 0 ? (resData[rt][colCo.purpose] || '') : '').trim()
        };
        userEmail = firstTemplate.student;
        userName = firstTemplate.studentName;
        startDt = firstTemplate.handover;
        endDt = firstTemplate.ret;
        break;
      }
    }

    itemIds.forEach(function(itemId) {
       var itemIdNorm = String(itemId || '').trim().toUpperCase();
       if (!itemIdNorm) return;
       var foundInReservation = false;
       var condVal = normalizeAdminCheckoutCondition_(checkoutConditionMap && checkoutConditionMap[itemId]);
       // 1. Rezervasyonu "Picked Up" yap
       for (var i = 1; i < resData.length; i++) {
         if (String(resData[i][colCo.group]).trim() === resIdTrimCo && String(resData[i][colCo.eqId] || '').trim().toUpperCase() === itemIdNorm) {
           foundInReservation = true;
           resSheet.getRange(i + 1, colCo.status + 1).setValue("Picked Up"); 
           userEmail = resData[i][colCo.student]; 
           userName = resData[i][colCo.studentName];
           startDt = resData[i][colCo.handover]; 
           endDt = resData[i][colCo.ret];
         }
       }
       // 1b) Admin checkout'a son anda eklenen kalemi aynı gruba satır olarak ekle
       if (!foundInReservation && firstTemplate) {
         var addName = String(itemId).trim();
         var addType = '';
         for (var ai = 1; ai < invData.length; ai++) {
           var invIdA = idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[ai][idxInvID] : invData[ai][1];
           if (String(invIdA || '').trim().toUpperCase() === itemIdNorm) {
             addName = String(idxInvName !== -1 ? invData[ai][idxInvName] : invData[ai][2]).trim() || addName;
             addType = String(idxInvType !== -1 ? invData[ai][idxInvType] : '').trim();
             break;
           }
         }
         var newRow = {};
         newRow[colCo.group] = firstTemplate.group;
         newRow[colCo.eqId] = String(itemId || '').trim();
         newRow[colCo.name] = addName;
         if (colCo.category >= 0) newRow[colCo.category] = addType;
         newRow[colCo.student] = firstTemplate.student;
         newRow[colCo.studentName] = firstTemplate.studentName;
         newRow[colCo.handover] = firstTemplate.handover;
         newRow[colCo.ret] = firstTemplate.ret;
         newRow[colCo.status] = 'Picked Up';
         if (colCo.approver >= 0) newRow[colCo.approver] = firstTemplate.approver;
         if (colCo.purpose >= 0) newRow[colCo.purpose] = firstTemplate.purpose;
         var appendArr = new Array(resData[0].length).fill('');
         for (var ci = 0; ci < appendArr.length; ci++) {
           if (Object.prototype.hasOwnProperty.call(newRow, ci)) appendArr[ci] = newRow[ci];
         }
         resSheet.appendRow(appendArr);
       }
       var foundInInventory = false;
       // 2. Envanteri "IN_USE" yap ve tablo verisini topla
       for (var j = 1; j < invData.length; j++) {
         var currentId = idxInvID !== -1 ? invData[j][idxInvID] : invData[j][1];
         if (String(currentId || '').trim().toUpperCase() === itemIdNorm) {
           foundInInventory = true;
            var sCol = idxInvStatus !== -1 ? idxInvStatus + 1 : 5;
            var cell = invSheet.getRange(j + 1, sCol);
            cell.clearDataValidations();
            cell.setValue("IN_USE");
            
            var eName = idxInvName !== -1 ? invData[j][idxInvName] : invData[j][2];
            if (idxCondOut !== -1) {
              invSheet.getRange(j + 1, idxCondOut + 1).setValue(condVal);
            }
           try { trySupabaseMirrorInventorySheetRow_(j + 1); } catch (_eInvMirrorChk) {}
            
            equipmentItems.push({
              id: String(itemId || '').trim(),
              name: String(eName).trim(),
              conditionOut: condVal
            });
            
            if (isStudioKeyEquipmentId(itemId)) hasStudioKey = true;
            break;
         }
       }
       if (!foundInInventory && foundInReservation) {
         for (var k = 1; k < resData.length; k++) {
           if (String(resData[k][colCo.group]).trim() !== resIdTrimCo) continue;
           if (String(resData[k][colCo.eqId] || '').trim().toUpperCase() !== itemIdNorm) continue;
           equipmentItems.push({
             id: String(resData[k][colCo.eqId] || '').trim(),
             name: String(resData[k][colCo.name] || '').trim(),
             conditionOut: condVal
           });
           break;
         }
       }
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(resIdTrimCo); } catch (_eChk) {}

    var templateId = hasStudioKey ? CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID : CONFIG.EQUIPMENT_FORM_DOC_ID;
    var pdfUrl = generateDeliveryPDF(templateId, {
      Student_Name: userName, 
      Student_ID: userEmail,
      Equipment_List: '',  // Eski metin formatı (artık kullanılmıyor, tablo var)
      Equipment_Items: equipmentItems,  // YENİ: Tablo verisi
      Handover_Date: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(startDt), "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm"),
      Return_Date: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(endDt), "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm")
    });

    try {
      var formLabel = hasStudioKey ? 'Stüdyo teslim formu' : 'Ekipman teslim formu';
      mailDeliveryPdfCopyToBorrower_(userEmail || '', userName || '', pdfUrl, formLabel, {
        resId: resIdTrimCo,
        handoverDate: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(startDt), "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm"),
        returnDate: Utilities.formatDate(new Date(endDt), "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm")
      });
    } catch (_eMailEq) {}

    return { success: true, url: pdfUrl };
  } catch(e) { 
    throw new Error(e.message); 
  }
}


// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// 3/3: processQuickCheckout — MEVCUT FONKSİYONU DEĞİŞTİRİN
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────

function processQuickCheckout(cartIds, email, returnDt, displayName, projectPurpose, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) throw new Error('Yetkisiz.');
    var purpose = String(projectPurpose || '').trim();
    if (purpose.length > 300) throw new Error('Proje açıklaması en fazla 300 karakter olabilir.');
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var sheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var invItems = _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_();
    var resId = 'QC-' + Utilities.getUuid().substring(0, 6).toUpperCase();
    var start = new Date();
    var who = String(displayName || '').trim();
    if (!who) who = (String(email).indexOf('@') >= 0 ? String(email).split('@')[0] : String(email));
    
    var end;
    if (returnDt) {
      end = new Date(returnDt);
    } else {
      end = new Date();
      end.setHours(17, 0, 0, 0);
    }
    
    var hasStudioKey = false;
    var equipmentItems = [];
    
    var tsQC = now();
    var approverQc = '';
    try { approverQc = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || ''; } catch (_eQC) {}
    cartIds.forEach(function(id) {
       var itm = invItems.find(function(i) { return i.id === id; });
       if (itm) {
         addRow(sheet, {
           reservation_group_id: resId,
           equipment_id: id,
           equipment_name: String(itm.name || ''),
           equipment_category: String(itm.type || ''),
           student_id: email,
           student_name: who,
           handover_date: start.toISOString(),
           return_date: end.toISOString(),
           status: 'Picked Up',
           approver_email: approverQc,
           purpose: purpose || 'Hızlı Çıkış',
           created_at: tsQC,
           updated_at: tsQC
         }, RESH);
         
         equipmentItems.push({
           id: String(id).trim(),
           name: String(itm.name).trim(),
           conditionOut: 'Excellent'
         });
         
         if (isStudioKeyEquipmentId(id)) hasStudioKey = true;
       }
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();

    // Envanter durumlarını güncelle
    adminProcessPartialCheckout(resId, cartIds, '', null, adminToken);

    var templateId = hasStudioKey ? CONFIG.STUDIO_FORM_DOC_ID : CONFIG.EQUIPMENT_FORM_DOC_ID;
    var pdfUrl = generateDeliveryPDF(templateId, {
      Student_Name: String(who).toUpperCase(),
      Student_ID: email,
      Equipment_List: '',
      Equipment_Items: equipmentItems,
      Handover_Date: Utilities.formatDate(start, "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm"),
      Return_Date: Utilities.formatDate(end, "GMT+3", "dd.MM.yyyy HH:mm")
    });

    return { success: true, url: pdfUrl };
  } catch(e) { 
    throw new Error("Hızlı Çıkış Hatası: " + e.message); 
  }
}

function lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(query) {
  return _legacyBridgeDisabled_('lookupQuickCheckoutUser_');
}

function lookupQuickCheckoutUser(query, adminToken) {
  if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { ok: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
  return lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(query);
}

function adminTrafficCancelDeliveries(resId, itemIds, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colAdT = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var ridT = String(resId).trim();
    itemIds.forEach(function(eqId) {
      var eqT = String(eqId).trim();
      for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][colAdT.group]).trim() === ridT && String(data[i][colAdT.eqId]).trim() === eqT) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colAdT.status + 1).setValue('Cancelled');
        }
      }
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(ridT); } catch (_eAT) {}
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message }; }
}

function adminTrafficExtendDeliveries(resId, itemIds, newEndDt, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    if (!newEndDt) throw new Error('Yeni iade tarihi gerekli.');
    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colExtD = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var ridX = String(resId).trim();
    itemIds.forEach(function(eqId) {
      var custodianId = '';
      var eqX = String(eqId).trim();
      for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][colExtD.group]).trim() === ridX && String(data[i][colExtD.eqId]).trim() === eqX) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colExtD.ret + 1).setValue(newEndDt);
          custodianId = String(data[i][colExtD.student] || '');
          break;
        }
      }
      if (custodianId) inventoryUpdateReturnDateForEquipment(eqId, newEndDt, custodianId, '');
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(ridX); } catch (_eAX) {}
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message }; }
}

function adminTrafficTransferDeliveries(resId, itemIds, newQuery, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var lu = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(newQuery);
    if (!lu || !lu.ok) throw new Error('Kullanıcı bulunamadı.');
    var sheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var data = sheet.getDataRange().getValues();
    var colTr = _reservationSheetColIxs_(data);
    var ridTr = String(resId).trim();
    var custodianName = lu.name || (lu.email && lu.email.indexOf('@') >= 0 ? lu.email.split('@')[0] : '') || String(lu.studentId || '');
    var custodianId = lu.studentId || lu.email || '';
    itemIds.forEach(function(eqId) {
      var eqTr = String(eqId).trim();
      for (var i = 1; i < data.length; i++) {
        if (String(data[i][colTr.group]).trim() === ridTr && String(data[i][colTr.eqId]).trim() === eqTr) {
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colTr.student + 1).setValue(custodianId);
          sheet.getRange(i + 1, colTr.studentName + 1).setValue(custodianName);
        }
      }
    });
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    try { trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationGroup_(ridTr); } catch (_eTR) {}
    return { success: true };
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message }; }
}

function adminTrafficPrintPdf(resId, itemIds, studioHandoverNote, checkoutConditionMap, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var note = studioHandoverNote != null ? String(studioHandoverNote).trim() : '';
    var studioRow = null;
    try {
      studioRow = toObjsStudioReservations_().find(function(r) {
        return String(r.id || '').trim() === String(resId || '').trim();
      }) || null;
    } catch (_eStP) {}
    if (studioRow) {
      return adminStudioGenerateUsagePdfOnly_(resId, itemIds || [], note);
    }
    return adminProcessPartialCheckout(resId, itemIds || [], note, checkoutConditionMap, adminToken);
  } catch (e) { return { success: false, error: e.message }; }
}

function _adminUserLookupBundleFromLu_(lu) {
  if (!lu || !lu.ok) return null;
  var em0 = String(lu.email || '').trim();
  if (!em0) return null;
  var profile = em0.indexOf('@') >= 0 ? getUserByEmail(em0) : null;
  if (!profile) {
    profile = {
      name: lu.name || '',
      email: em0,
      id: lu.studentId || '',
      student_no: lu.isStaffRow ? '' : (lu.studentId || ''),
      role: lu.isStaffRow ? ROLES.INSTRUCTOR : ROLES.STUDENT,
      level: lu.level || '1',
      department: '',
      yetkiRaw: lu.level || ''
    };
    if (lu.isStaffRow) profile.student_no = '';
  }
  var enriched = enrichUserMatrix(Object.assign({}, profile));
  var sid = String(lu.studentId || profile.student_no || profile.id || '');
  var em = String(lu.email || profile.email || '').toLowerCase();
  var phoneSheet = '';
  try {
    phoneSheet = (lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(em) || lookupPhoneFromDirectory_(sid) || '').trim();
  } catch (ePh) {}
  var profileForUi = Object.assign({}, enriched || profile, { phone: phoneSheet });
  var resSheet = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID).getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
  var r0 = resSheet.getDataRange().getValues();
  var colLk = r0.length >= 1 ? _reservationSheetColIxs_(r0) : { student: 3, eqId: 0, name: 1, handover: 5, ret: 6, status: 7, group: 9 };
  var eqHistory = [];
  var eqActive = [];
  for (var i = 1; i < r0.length; i++) {
    var row = r0[i];
    var uid = String(row[colLk.student] || '').trim();
    var ok = (sid && uid === sid) || (em && uid.toLowerCase() === em);
    if (!ok) continue;
    var rec = { eqId: row[colLk.eqId], eqName: row[colLk.name], start: row[colLk.handover], end: row[colLk.ret], status: row[colLk.status], resId: row[colLk.group] };
    if (/pending|approved|picked/i.test(String(row[colLk.status] || ''))) eqActive.push(rec);
    eqHistory.push(rec);
  }
  eqHistory = eqHistory.slice(-40).reverse();
  var stRes = [];
  try {
    toObjsStudioReservations_().forEach(function(r) {
      var su = String(r.user_id || '').trim();
      if ((sid && su === sid) || (em && su.toLowerCase() === em)) {
        stRes.push({ studio: r.studio_name, start: r.start_dt, end: r.end_dt, status: r.status });
      }
    });
  } catch (e0) {}
  var extras = getUserDashboardExtrasForUser_(profileForUi);
  var loans = extras && extras.loans ? extras.loans : [];
  var pens = extras && extras.penalties ? extras.penalties : [];
  var onHand = loans;
  var overdueOnHand = loans.filter(function(L) { return L.overdue; });
  var activePen = pens.filter(function(p) { return p.active; });
  var userTypeLabel = em.indexOf('@bilgi.edu.tr') >= 0 ? 'Personel' : 'Öğrenci';
  var pendingEquipmentApprovals = eqActive.filter(function(r) { return String(r.status || '').toLowerCase() === 'pending'; });
  var pendingStudioApprovals = [];
  try {
    toObjsStudioReservations_().forEach(function(r) {
      var su = String(r.user_id || '').trim();
      if (!((sid && su === sid) || (em && su.toLowerCase() === em))) return;
      if (String(r.status || '').toLowerCase() !== STATUS.PENDING) return;
      pendingStudioApprovals.push({ id: r.id, studio: r.studio_name, start: r.start_dt, end: r.end_dt, status: r.status });
    });
  } catch (eP) {}
  var cutoff15 = Date.now() - 15 * 86400000;
  var equipmentRecent15d = eqHistory.filter(function(r) {
    try {
      var t = new Date(r.end || r.start || 0).getTime();
      return !isNaN(t) && t >= cutoff15;
    } catch (e1) { return false; }
  });
  var invList = _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_();
  var responsibleForEquipment = [];
  var nameQ = String(profileForUi.name || '').trim().toLowerCase();
  for (var iq = 0; iq < invList.length; iq++) {
    var it = invList[iq];
    var rt = String(it.responsibleText || '').toLowerCase();
    if (!rt) continue;
    if ((nameQ && rt.indexOf(nameQ) >= 0) || (em && rt.indexOf(em) >= 0)) {
      responsibleForEquipment.push({ id: it.id, name: it.name, type: it.type, locationText: it.locationText || '' });
    }
  }
  return {
    profile: profileForUi,
    userTypeLabel: userTypeLabel,
    studentIdDisplay: sid,
    equipmentHistory: eqHistory,
    equipmentActive: eqActive,
    studioReservations: stRes,
    loansOnHand: onHand,
    overdueOnHand: overdueOnHand,
    penalties: activePen,
    pendingEquipmentApprovals: pendingEquipmentApprovals,
    pendingStudioApprovals: pendingStudioApprovals,
    equipmentRecent15d: equipmentRecent15d,
    responsibleForEquipment: responsibleForEquipment
  };
}

function adminUserLookup(query, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var q = String(query || '').trim();
    if (!q) return { error: 'Boş arama.' };
    if (q.length < 3) return { error: 'En az 3 karakter girin.' };
    var candidates = [];
    var ql = q.toLowerCase();
    if (q.indexOf('@') >= 0) {
      var luE = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(q);
      if (luE && luE.ok) candidates.push(luE);
    } else if (/^\d+$/.test(q.replace(/\s/g, ''))) {
      var luN = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(q);
      if (luN && luN.ok) candidates.push(luN);
    } else {
      var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
      var stu = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS_STUDENT);
      if (stu) {
        var d = stu.getDataRange().getValues();
        for (var i = 1; i < d.length; i++) {
          var nm = String(d[i][1] || '').trim();
          if (nm.toLowerCase().indexOf(ql) >= 0) {
            candidates.push({ ok: true, name: nm, email: String(d[i][2] || '').trim(), studentId: String(d[i][0] || '').trim(), level: String(d[i][5] || '') });
          }
        }
      }
      var stf = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.USERS);
      if (stf) {
        var d2 = stf.getDataRange().getValues();
        for (var j = 1; j < d2.length; j++) {
          var nm2 = String(d2[j][1] || '').trim();
          if (nm2.toLowerCase().indexOf(ql) >= 0) {
            candidates.push({ ok: true, name: nm2, email: String(d2[j][2] || '').trim(), studentId: String(d2[j][0] || '').trim(), isStaffRow: true });
          }
        }
      }
    }
    if (!candidates.length) return { error: 'Kullanıcı bulunamadı.' };
    var seen = {};
    var matches = [];
    var maxMatches = 10;
    var bundleCache = CacheService.getScriptCache();
    for (var c = 0; c < candidates.length; c++) {
      var lu = candidates[c];
      var emk = String(lu.email || '').trim().toLowerCase();
      var dedupe = emk || ('id:' + String(lu.studentId || '').trim());
      if (!dedupe || dedupe === 'id:') continue;
      if (seen[dedupe]) continue;
      seen[dedupe] = true;
      var b = null;
      var ck = 'adminUserLookupBundle:' + dedupe;
      try {
        var cr = bundleCache.get(ck);
        if (cr) b = JSON.parse(cr);
      } catch (_eCacheGet) {}
      if (!b) {
        b = _adminUserLookupBundleFromLu_(lu);
        try { if (b) bundleCache.put(ck, JSON.stringify(b), 45); } catch (_eCachePut) {}
      }
      if (b) matches.push(b);
      if (matches.length >= maxMatches) break;
    }
    if (!matches.length) return { error: 'Kullanıcı bulunamadı.' };
    return { matches: matches };
  } catch (e) {
    return { error: e.message };
  }
}

function adminCreateForwardEquipmentReservation(payload, adminToken) {
  try {
    if (!requireAdminWebUser_(adminToken)) return { success: false, error: 'Yetkisiz.' };
    var kind = String(payload.reservation_type || 'equipment').trim().toLowerCase();
    if (kind !== 'equipment') return { success: false, error: 'Bu akışta yalnızca ekipman desteklenir.' };
    var userKey = String(payload.user_key || payload.email || '').trim();
    var itemIds = payload.item_ids || [];
    var start = payload.start_dt;
    var end = payload.end_dt;
    var period = String(payload.period || 'once');
    var endPeriodDt = payload.end_period_dt;
    if (!userKey || !itemIds.length || !start || !end) throw new Error('E-posta/öğrenci no, ekipman ve teslim/iade tarihleri gerekli.');
    var lu = lookupQuickCheckoutUser_(userKey);
    var resolvedEmail = (lu && lu.email && lu.email.indexOf('@') >= 0) ? lu.email : (userKey.indexOf('@') >= 0 ? userKey : '');
    var studentId = (lu && lu.studentId) ? lu.studentId : (resolvedEmail || userKey);
    var studentName = (lu && lu.name) ? lu.name : String(userKey).split('@')[0];
    var ss = SpreadsheetApp.openById(CONFIG.SPREADSHEET_ID);
    var resSheet = ss.getSheetByName(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
    var inv = _adminEquipmentListFromSheet_();
    var currentStart = new Date(start);
    var currentEnd = new Date(end);
    if (isNaN(currentStart.getTime()) || isNaN(currentEnd.getTime())) throw new Error('Geçersiz tarih.');
    if (currentEnd.getTime() <= currentStart.getTime()) throw new Error('İade tarihi teslimden sonra olmalı.');
    var endPeriod = null;
    if (period !== 'once') {
      endPeriod = adminParseRepeatEndInclusive_(endPeriodDt);
      if (!endPeriod) throw new Error('Tekrarlı rezervasyon için tekrar bitiş tarihi gerekli.');
      if (endPeriod.getTime() < currentStart.getTime()) throw new Error('Tekrar bitiş tarihi teslim zamanından önce olamaz.');
    }
    var totalRows = 0;
    var errors = [];
    var skippedHolidayDates = [];
    var tz = Session.getScriptTimeZone();
    var occurrence = 0;
    var groupId = 'RES-ADM-' + Utilities.getUuid().substring(0, 8).toUpperCase();
    var actorEmail = Session.getActiveUser().getEmail() || '';
    if (!actorEmail) actorEmail = 'admin';
    function sheetDt(d) { return Utilities.formatDate(d, tz, "yyyy-MM-dd'T'HH:mm"); }
    while (true) {
      occurrence++;
      if (occurrence > 400) throw new Error('Tekrar limiti aşıldı (400). Tekrar bitiş tarihini kontrol edin.');
      var purpose = String(payload.purpose || 'Admin ileri tarihli rezervasyon');
      var sStr = sheetDt(currentStart);
      var eStr = sheetDt(currentEnd);
      var hInfo = _holidayConflictInfo_(currentStart, currentEnd);
      if (hInfo.blocked) {
        if (period === 'once') {
          throw new Error('Resmi tatilde ekipman teslim/iade yapılamaz: ' + hInfo.dates.join(', '));
        }
        skippedHolidayDates.push(_ymdInTz_(currentStart));
      } else {
      try {
        validateBookingDateTime('equipment', sStr, eStr, { role: ROLES.SUPER_ADMIN });
        assertDepotSlotCapacity_(sStr, eStr, '', {});
      } catch (eSl) {
        throw new Error(eSl.message || String(eSl));
      }
      var occurrenceRows = [];
      var tsFwd = now();
      itemIds.forEach(function(iid) {
        var itm = inv.find(function(x) { return x.id === iid; });
        var nm = itm ? itm.name : '';
        var ty = itm ? itm.type : '';
        try {
          var rowPayload = {
            reservation_group_id: groupId,
            equipment_id: String(iid || ''),
            equipment_name: String(nm || ''),
            equipment_category: String(ty || ''),
            student_id: String(studentId || resolvedEmail || ''),
            student_name: String(studentName || ''),
            handover_date: sStr,
            return_date: eStr,
            status: 'Approved',
            approver_email: actorEmail,
            purpose: purpose,
            created_at: tsFwd,
            updated_at: tsFwd
          };
          occurrenceRows.push(rowPayload);
          try { addRow(resSheet, rowPayload, RESH); } catch (_sheetOccErr) {}
        } catch (e1) {
          errors.push(String(iid) + ': ' + e1.message);
        }
      });
      if (_supabasePrimaryWriteEnabled_() && occurrenceRows.length) {
        try {
          _supaUpsertEquipmentReservationRowsPrimary_(occurrenceRows);
        } catch (eSupOcc) {
          throw new Error('Supabase write failed: ' + (eSupOcc.message || eSupOcc));
        }
      } else {
        for (var om = 0; om < occurrenceRows.length; om++) {
          trySupabaseMirrorEquipmentReservationRow_(occurrenceRows[om]);
        }
      }
      totalRows += occurrenceRows.length;
      }
      if (period === 'once') break;
      if (period === 'daily') {
        currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 1);
        currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 1);
      } else if (period === 'weekly') {
        currentStart.setDate(currentStart.getDate() + 7);
        currentEnd.setDate(currentEnd.getDate() + 7);
      } else if (period === 'monthly') {
        currentStart.setMonth(currentStart.getMonth() + 1);
        currentEnd.setMonth(currentEnd.getMonth() + 1);
      } else {
        throw new Error('Geçersiz period.');
      }
      if (endPeriod && currentStart.getTime() > endPeriod.getTime()) break;
    }
    SpreadsheetApp.flush();
    var warnings = errors.length ? errors.join(' | ') : '';
    var skipped = [];
    if (skippedHolidayDates.length) {
      skipped = Array.from(new Set(skippedHolidayDates)).sort();
      warnings = (warnings ? (warnings + ' | ') : '') + ('Resmi tatil nedeniyle atlandı: ' + skipped.join(', '));
    }
    return { success: true, count: totalRows, resId: groupId, groupIds: [groupId], warnings: warnings, skipped_holiday_dates: skipped, occurrences: occurrence };
  } catch (e) {
    return { success: false, error: e.message };
  }
}

function checkOfficialHolidayBridge(startDt, endDt, testToken) {
  try {
    var tok = String(testToken || '').trim();
    if (tok && !resolveCurrentUser(tok)) return { ok: false, error: 'Not signed in.' };
    if (!startDt || !endDt) return { ok: false, error: 'Dates required.' };
    var s = new Date(startDt);
    var e = new Date(endDt);
    if (isNaN(s.getTime()) || isNaN(e.getTime())) return { ok: false, error: 'Invalid format.' };
    var info = _holidayConflictInfo_(s, e);
    return { ok: true, blocked: !!info.blocked, dates: info.dates || [] };
  } catch (err) {
    return { ok: false, error: err.message || String(err) };
  }
}

function adminGetForwardAvailableEquipment(startDt, endDt, adminToken) {
  return _legacyBridgeDisabled_('adminGetForwardAvailableEquipment');
}

function getUserByEmail(email) {
  if (!email) return null;
  var normalizedEmail = String(email || '').toLowerCase().trim();
  if (!normalizedEmail) return null;
  var cached = _userCacheGet_(normalizedEmail);
  if (cached) return cached;
  try {
    var row = supabaseTrySelectFirstExisting_(['profiles'], {
      select: '*',
      email: 'eq.' + normalizedEmail,
      limit: 1
    }).rows;
    var p = (row && row.length) ? row[0] : null;
    if (!p) return null;
    if (String(supaRowPick_(p, ['is_active'], 'true')).toLowerCase() === 'false') return null;

    var role = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['role'], '') || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    var userType = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['user_type'], role === 'student' ? 'student' : 'staff')).trim().toLowerCase();
    var staffType = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['staff_type'], '') || '').trim().toLowerCase();
    var idVal = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['id', 'student_number'], '') || '').trim();
    var studentNo = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['student_number'], '') || '').trim();
    var deptName = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['department_name', 'faculty_name'], '') || '').trim();
    var deptCode = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['department_code'], '') || '').trim();
    var fullName = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['full_name'], '') || '').trim();
    var override = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['access_override_level'], '') || '').trim();
    var senior = String(supaRowPick_(p, ['senior_flag'], 'false')).toLowerCase() === 'true';
    var derivedLevel = '1';
    if (override && /^[1-5]$/.test(override)) derivedLevel = override;
    else if (senior) derivedLevel = '5';
    else if (role === 'super_admin' || role === 'technician' || role === 'iiw_instructor') derivedLevel = '5';
    else if (userType === 'student') {
      var st = resolveStudentLevel(studentNo || idVal, '');
      derivedLevel = String(st.level || '1');
      if (!deptName) deptName = String(st.deptName || '');
      if (!deptCode) deptCode = String(st.abbr || '');
    } else {
      var sf = resolveStaffLevel(staffType || 'akademik', deptName, deptCode, role);
      derivedLevel = String(sf.level || '1');
    }

    var user = {
      id: idVal || normalizedEmail,
      name: fullName || normalizedEmail.split('@')[0],
      email: normalizedEmail,
      role: role || (userType === 'student' ? 'student' : 'instructor'),
      staff_status: userType === 'staff' ? (staffType || 'akademik') : '',
      department: deptName,
      bolum: deptCode,
      level: derivedLevel,
      yetkiRaw: override || role,
      student_no: studentNo || '',
      status: 'active',
      isComm: String(deptName || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('communication') >= 0 || String(deptName || '').toLowerCase().indexOf('iletişim') >= 0,
      isApplied: ['MED', 'TVRP', 'FTV', 'VCD'].indexOf(String(deptCode || '').toUpperCase()) >= 0,
      special_access: String(supaRowPick_(p, ['special_access'], '') || '').trim(),
      special_access_until: String(supaRowPick_(p, ['special_access_until'], '') || '').trim(),
      special_equipment_access: String(supaRowPick_(p, ['special_equipment_access'], '') || '').trim(),
      special_equipment_access_until: String(supaRowPick_(p, ['special_equipment_access_until'], '') || '').trim()
    };
    _userCachePut_(normalizedEmail, user, 600);
    return user;
  } catch (_e) {
    return null;
  }
}

/**
 * Personel F (Yetki) sütunu:
 * - Doğrudan 1–5 → ekipman seviyesi (iletişim bayrakları fakülte/bölümden).
 * - super_admin | technician | iiw_instructor → rol getUserByEmail'de; seviye 5 (tam ekipman dilimi).
 * - SENIOR → seviye 5.
 * - instructor veya boş → aşağıdaki fakülte/bölüm taban seviyeleri.
 */
function resolveStaffLevel(staffStatus, fakulte, bolum, sheetYetki) {
  var raw = String(sheetYetki || '').trim();
  var yetkiUp = raw.toUpperCase();
  var st = String(staffStatus || '').toLowerCase();
  var fak = String(fakulte || '').toLowerCase();
  var bol = String(bolum || '').toUpperCase().trim();

  var isComm = fak.includes('iletişim') || fak.includes('iletisim') ||
               fak.includes('communication') || fak.includes('comm') ||
               fak.includes('İletişim');
  var isApplied = APPLIED_DEPTS.some(function(d) { return bol.includes(d); });

  if (/^[1-5]$/.test(raw)) {
    return { level: raw, isComm: isComm, isApplied: isApplied };
  }

  var yl = raw.toLowerCase();
  if (yl === 'super_admin' || yl === 'technician' || yl === 'iiw_instructor') {
    return { level: '5', isComm: isComm, isApplied: isApplied };
  }

  if (yetkiUp === 'SENIOR') {
    return { level: '5', isComm: isComm, isApplied: isApplied };
  }

  if (st === 'idari') {
    return { level: '1', isComm: isComm, isApplied: false };
  }

  if (!isComm) {
    return { level: '1', isComm: false, isApplied: false };
  }

  if (isApplied) {
    return { level: '3', isComm: true, isApplied: true };
  }

  return { level: '2', isComm: true, isApplied: false };
}

/**
 * Lightweight backend smoke tests (read-only).
 * Run manually before deploy to catch common regressions.
 */
function qaSmokeTestReport() {
  var out = {
    ok: true,
    ranAt: now(),
    checks: [],
    errors: []
  };
  function add(name, pass, detail) {
    out.checks.push({ name: name, pass: !!pass, detail: detail || '' });
    if (!pass) out.ok = false;
  }
  try {
    // 1) Reservation sheet column mapping sanity
    try {
      var resSh = getSheet(SHEETS.RESERVATIONS);
      var resVals = resSh.getDataRange().getValues();
      var c = _reservationSheetColIxs_(resVals);
      add(
        'reservation columns distinct',
        c.group !== c.eqId && c.group >= 0 && c.eqId >= 0,
        'group=' + c.group + ', eqId=' + c.eqId
      );
    } catch (e1) {
      add('reservation columns distinct', false, e1.message || String(e1));
    }

    // 2) Studio blocking statuses should include pending/approved/checked_out
    try {
      var bs = (studioStatusesBlockingKey_() || []).map(function(x) { return String(x || '').toLowerCase(); });
      var hasPending = bs.indexOf('pending') >= 0;
      var hasApproved = bs.indexOf('approved') >= 0;
      var hasCheckedOut = bs.indexOf(String(STUDIO_STATUS_CHECKED_OUT || '').toLowerCase()) >= 0 ||
        bs.indexOf(String(STATUS.KEY_OUT || '').toLowerCase()) >= 0;
      add('studio blocking statuses', hasPending && hasApproved && hasCheckedOut, bs.join(', '));
    } catch (e2) {
      add('studio blocking statuses', false, e2.message || String(e2));
    }

    // 3) Date parser should preserve provided time for Date inputs
    try {
      var dIso = studioCombineSheetDateTime_(new Date('2026-04-08T14:12:00Z'), '15:30');
      var dObj = new Date(dIso);
      var hhmm = isNaN(dObj.getTime()) ? 'invalid' : Utilities.formatDate(dObj, Session.getScriptTimeZone() || 'Europe/Istanbul', 'HH:mm');
      add('studio date-time combine preserves time', hhmm === '15:30', String(dIso || ''));
    } catch (e3) {
      add('studio date-time combine preserves time', false, e3.message || String(e3));
    }

    // 4) Pending date formatter should not collapse valid datetime to 00:00
    try {
      var fmt = fmtAdminPendingDt_('2026-04-08T15:30:00');
      add('admin pending datetime formatter', /15:30/.test(String(fmt || '')), String(fmt || ''));
    } catch (e4) {
      add('admin pending datetime formatter', false, e4.message || String(e4));
    }

    // 5) Studio canonical conversion should keep start/end when split date+time exists
    try {
      var can = canonicalFromStudioSheetRow_({
        'Seç': 'SRES_TEST',
        'Stüdyo Adı': 'GREEN STUDIO',
        'Kimlik/Sicil No': 'USR_TEST',
        'Ad Soyad': 'Test User',
        'Giriş Tarihi': '2026-04-08',
        'Giriş Saati': '13:30',
        'Çıkış Tarihi': '2026-04-08',
        'Çıkış Saati': '15:30',
        'Tekrar Durumu': '—',
        'Tekrar Bitiş Tarihi': '',
        'status': 'pending',
        'studio_id': 'GREEN'
      }) || {};
      var cs = new Date(can.start_dt || '');
      var ce = new Date(can.end_dt || '');
      var okCan = !isNaN(cs.getTime()) && !isNaN(ce.getTime()) && ce.getTime() > cs.getTime();
      add('studio canonical preserves start/end', okCan, 'start=' + String(can.start_dt || '') + ', end=' + String(can.end_dt || ''));
    } catch (e5) {
      add('studio canonical preserves start/end', false, e5.message || String(e5));
    }
  } catch (e) {
    out.ok = false;
    out.errors.push(e.message || String(e));
  }
  return out;
}

function qaSmokeTestLog() {
  var r = qaSmokeTestReport();
  Logger.log(JSON.stringify(r, null, 2));
  return r;
}

/**
 * Apps Script editor: run once to see why GCal import preview works but write fails.
 * Logs importError when importOk is false.
 */
function debugStudioImportPipeline() {
  var out = {};
  out.supabaseOnlyStudioReservations = _supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_();
  out.supabaseCredentialsOk = !!supabaseBaseAndKey_();

  var p = importGoogleCalendarStudioEventsOnce('', '', true);
  out.previewOk = !!(p && p.ok);
  out.previewCount = Number((p && p.count) || 0);

  var r = null;
  try {
    r = importGoogleCalendarStudioEventsOnce('', '', false);
  } catch (eImp) {
    out.importThrown = true;
    out.importError = eImp.message || String(eImp);
  }
  if (!out.importThrown) {
    out.importOk = !!(r && r.ok);
    out.imported = Number((r && r.imported) || 0);
    out.mode = (r && r.mode) || '';
    out.rowsBuilt = (r && r.rowsBuilt !== undefined) ? r.rowsBuilt : '';
    out.importError = (r && r.error) ? String(r.error) : '';
    out.importRaw = r ? JSON.stringify(r) : '';
  }

  var rows = toObjsStudioReservations_() || [];
  out.totalStudioRows = rows.length;
  out.greenRows = rows.filter(function(x) {
    return String(x.studio_id || '').toUpperCase() === 'GREEN';
  }).length;
  var block = (studioStatusesBlockingKey_() || []).map(function(s) { return String(s).toLowerCase(); });
  out.greenBlockingRows = rows.filter(function(x) {
    return String(x.studio_id || '').toUpperCase() === 'GREEN' &&
      block.indexOf(String(x.status || '').toLowerCase()) >= 0;
  }).length;

  Logger.log(JSON.stringify(out, null, 2));
  return out;
}

/**
 * Apps Script editor: tek satır upsert ile studio_reservations yazılabilir mi söyler.
 * Başarılıysa Supabase Table Editor'da id ile satırı görürsün; istersen sil.
 */
function debugSupabaseStudioWrite() {
  var out = {
    targetTable: 'studio_reservations',
    credentialsOk: !!supabaseBaseAndKey_(),
    supabaseOnlyStudioReservations: _supabaseOnlyStudioReservationsEnabled_()
  };
  if (!out.credentialsOk) {
    out.ok = false;
    out.error = 'Script Properties: SUPABASE_URL veya SUPABASE_SERVICE_ROLE_KEY / SUPABASE_ANON_KEY eksik.';
    Logger.log(JSON.stringify(out, null, 2));
    return out;
  }
  var cfg = supabaseBaseAndKey_();
  var k = String(cfg.key || '');
  out.keyHint = k.length > 120 ? 'service_role veya uzun JWT' : (k.length > 40 ? 'JWT (anon veya service)' : 'kısa key — kontrol et');

  var testId = 'BOOKDECK_DEBUG_STUDIO_WRITE_' + String(Date.now());
  var testRow = {
    id: testId,
    studio_id: 'GREEN',
    studio_name: 'Green Studio',
    user_id: 'DEBUG',
    user_name: 'Debug Write Test',
    start_dt: new Date().toISOString(),
    end_dt: new Date(Date.now() + 60 * 60 * 1000).toISOString(),
    purpose: 'DBG_WRITE',
    pdf_url: '',
    key_id: 'GKEY-01',
    key_pickup_dt: new Date().toISOString(),
    status: STATUS.APPROVED,
    approved_by: 'DEBUG',
    approved_at: now(),
    rejected_reason: '',
    is_weekend: false,
    notes: 'debug row — güvenle sil',
    created_at: now(),
    updated_at: now(),
    request_type: 'İdari Birim Talebi',
    studio_usage_form_url: '',
    studio_handover_note: '',
    return_handover_note: ''
  };
  try {
    var payload = supabaseMirrorStudioRowPayload_(testRow);
    _supaUpsertBatch_('studio_reservations', [payload], 'id');
    out.ok = true;
    out.insertedId = testId;
    out.hint = 'Supabase → Table Editor → studio_reservations → id = ' + testId + ' (istersen sil).';
  } catch (e) {
    out.ok = false;
    out.error = e.message || String(e);
    out.hint = 'Hata genelde: yanlış key, RLS (anon ile insert kapalı), tablo adı farklı, veya kolon uyuşmazlığı.';
  }
  Logger.log(JSON.stringify(out, null, 2));
  return out;
}
